Yet most of them do not understand.

How many communities have We destroyed that were ungrateful for their means of livelihood! Their homes are now deserted, except for a few, and We are their inheritors. Your Lord never destroys a population until He has sent a messenger to its center, reciting Our signs to them. We only destroy populations when their people are unjust.

The material things you are given are just conveniences of this life and its glitter, but what is with God is better and more enduring. Will you not then be wise? Is the one to whom We have promised a goodly promise, which he will find true, like the one whom We allow to enjoy the comforts of this life, but who will be among those brought up for punishment on the Day of Judgment?

On that day, God will call to them and say, 'Where are My partners whom you imagined?' Those against whom the charge will be proved will say, 'Our Lord! These are the ones we led astray. We led them astray as we were astray ourselves. We free ourselves from them in Your presence; it was not us they worshipped.'

It will be said to them, 'Call upon your partners for help.' They will call upon them, but they will not listen to them, and they will see the penalty before them. If only they had been open to guidance! On that day, God will call to them and say, 'What was the answer you gave to the messengers?' The whole story will seem obscure to them, and they will not be able to question each other.

But anyone who repents, believes, and works righteousness will have hopes to be among those who achieve salvation. Your Lord creates and chooses as He pleases; they have no choice in the matter. Glory to God, and far is He above the partners they ascribe to Him! Your Lord knows all that their hearts conceal and all that they reveal.

He is God; there is no god but Him. To Him be praise, at the first and at the last. His is the command, and to Him you will be brought back. Say, 'Have you thought, if God made night everlasting for you until the Day of Resurrection, who is a god besides God who could bring you light? Will you not then hear?' Say, 'Have you thought, if God made day everlasting for you until the Day of Resurrection, who is a god besides God who could bring you night wherein you rest? Will you not then see?'

Out of His mercy, He has made for you night and day so that you may rest and seek His grace, and so that you may be grateful. On the Day when He will call to them and say, 'Where are My partners whom you pretended?' We will draw forth from every nation a witness and say, 'Bring your proof.' Then they will know that the truth is God's, and all that they invented will have failed them.

Qarun was doubtless of the people of Moses, but he acted insolently towards them."Korah, who was from the people of Moses, oppressed them. We gave him so much treasure that even the keys to his wealth were a burden for strong men. His people advised him, "Don't be arrogant, for God does not love those who are boastful."

They continued, "Use the wealth God has given you to seek the Hereafter, but don't forget your share of this world. Do good to others as God has been good to you, and don't seek to cause corruption on the earth, for God does not love those who spread corruption."

Korah arrogantly replied, "I have been given this wealth because of my own knowledge." Did he not realize that God had destroyed many generations before him who were stronger and richer than he was? The guilty are not always immediately called to account for their sins.

Korah went out among his people in his splendor, and those who desired the life of this world said, "We wish we had what Korah has; he is truly fortunate." But those who had been given true knowledge said, "Woe to you! The reward of God is better for those who believe and do good deeds, but only those who are patient will attain it."

Then We caused the earth to swallow him and his house. He had no one to help him against God, nor could he defend himself. Those who had envied his position the day before began to say, "It is indeed God who enlarges or restricts provision for any of His servants as He pleases. If God had not been gracious to us, He could have caused the earth to swallow us too. The ungrateful never prosper."

The Home of the Hereafter is for those who do not seek to exalt themselves on earth or cause corruption. The best outcome is for the righteous. Whoever does good will receive a reward better than their deed, but those who do evil will only be punished to the extent of their deeds.

He who has given you the Qur'an will bring you back to the Place of Return. Say, "My Lord knows best who brings true guidance and who is in manifest error." You did not expect that the Book would be sent to you except as a mercy from your Lord. Therefore, do not support those who reject God's message.

Do not let anything keep you back from the signs of God after they have been revealed to you. Invite people to your Lord and do not be among those who join gods with God. Do not call upon any other god besides God. There is no god but Him. Everything will perish except His own Face. To Him belongs the command, and to Him you will be brought back.

Chapter 29: The Spider (Al-Ankaboot)
In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

A.L.M. Do people think they will be left alone just because they say, "We believe," and will not be tested? We tested those before them, and God will certainly know those who are true from those who are false. Do those who practice evil think they will escape Us? Evil is their judgment!

For those who hope to meet God, the appointed time is surely coming, and He hears and knows all things. If anyone strives, they do so for their own soul, for God is free of all needs from all creation."And whoever strives, does so for their own benefit, for God is self-sufficient and independent of His creatures. Those who believe and do good deeds, We will erase their bad deeds and reward them according to the best of their actions. We have commanded people to be kind to their parents, but if they pressure you to associate others with Me, do not obey them. You will all return to Me, and I will inform you of what you did. Those who believe and do good deeds will be admitted among the righteous.

Some people say, 'We believe in God,' but when they face hardship for God's sake, they treat it as if it were God's punishment. If help comes from your Lord, they claim, 'We were always with you!' Does God not know what is in the hearts of all creation? God certainly knows those who believe and those who are hypocrites. The disbelievers say to the believers, 'Follow our way, and we will bear your sins.' But they cannot bear any of their sins; they are liars. They will carry their own burdens and other burdens along with their own, and on the Day of Judgment, they will be questioned about their falsehoods.

We sent Noah to his people, and he stayed with them for 950 years. The flood overwhelmed them while they persisted in sin. We saved him and those with him in the Ark, making it a sign for all people. We also saved Abraham, who told his people, 'Serve God and fear Him; that is best for you if you understand. You worship idols besides God and invent falsehoods. Those you worship besides God cannot provide for you. Seek sustenance from God, serve Him, and be grateful to Him; to Him you will return.'

If you reject the message, previous generations also rejected it. The messenger's duty is only to convey the message clearly. Do they not see how God initiates creation and then repeats it? That is easy for God. Say, 'Travel through the earth and see how God originated creation; He will produce a later creation. God has power over all things.' He punishes whom He wills and grants mercy to whom He wills, and to Him you will be returned. You cannot escape Him on earth or in the sky, and besides God, you have no protector or helper.

Those who reject God's signs and the meeting with Him in the Hereafter will despair of His mercy and face a grievous penalty. The response of Abraham's people was to say, 'Kill him or burn him.' But God saved him from the fire. There are signs in this for people who believe. Abraham said, 'You have taken idols besides God out of mutual love in this life, but on the Day of Judgment, you will disown and curse each other, and your abode will be the Fire, with no helpers.' But Lot had faith."Lot believed in Abraham and said, "I am fleeing to my Lord. He is the Mighty, the Wise." We gave Abraham Isaac and Jacob and established prophethood and revelation among his descendants. We rewarded him in this life, and in the Hereafter, he will be among the righteous.

Remember Lot, who told his people, "You commit lewdness that no one before you has ever done. Do you approach men, cut off travelers, and practice wickedness in your councils?" His people responded, "Bring us God's punishment if you are truthful." Lot prayed, "O my Lord, help me against these mischievous people."

When Our messengers brought Abraham the good news, they said, "We are going to destroy the people of this town because they are wrongdoers." Abraham said, "But Lot is there." They replied, "We know who is there. We will save him and his followers, except his wife, who will stay behind."

When Our messengers came to Lot, he was distressed and felt powerless to protect them. They reassured him, "Do not fear or grieve. We will save you and your followers, except your wife, who will stay behind." They said, "We will bring down a punishment from heaven on the people of this town because they are wickedly rebellious." We left a clear sign of this for people who understand.

We sent Shu'aib to the people of Midian. He said, "O my people, serve God and fear the Last Day. Do not commit evil on the earth with the intent to do mischief." But they rejected him, and a mighty blast seized them, leaving them prostrate in their homes by morning.

Remember the 'Ad and Thamud people. Their fate is evident from their ruined dwellings. Satan made their deeds seem fair to them and kept them from the right path, though they were intelligent and skilled. Remember Qarun, Pharaoh, and Haman. Moses came to them with clear signs, but they were arrogant on the earth and could not escape Our punishment.

Each of them was seized for their crime. Some were caught by a violent storm, some by a mighty blast, some were swallowed by the earth, and some were drowned. It was not God who wronged them; they wronged themselves.

The parable of those who take protectors other than God is like a spider building a house. The flimsiest of houses is the spider's house if they but knew. God knows whatever they call upon besides Him. He is the Mighty, the Wise. These parables are set forth for mankind, but only those with knowledge understand them.

God created the heavens and the earth in true proportions. This is a sign for those who believe. Recite what has been revealed to you of the Book and establish regular prayer. Prayer restrains from shameful and unjust deeds, and the remembrance of God is the greatest thing in life. God knows the deeds you do."Remember God is the greatest, and He knows what you do. 

Do not argue with the People of the Book (Jews and Christians) except in a kind and respectful manner, unless they are unjust. Say, 'We believe in what was revealed to us and what was revealed to you. Our God and your God is one, and we submit to Him.'

We have sent down the Book to you, and the People of the Book believe in it, as do some of the pagan Arabs. Only the disbelievers reject our signs. You were not able to read or write before this Book came to you, so those who doubt would have had reason to question it. But these are clear signs in the hearts of those who have been given knowledge, and only the unjust reject them.

They ask, 'Why are no signs sent down to him from his Lord?' Say, 'The signs are with God, and I am just a clear warner.' Is it not enough for them that we have sent down the Book which is recited to them? It is a mercy and a reminder for those who believe.

Say, 'God is enough as a witness between me and you. He knows what is in the heavens and the earth. Those who believe in falsehood and reject God are the losers.' They ask you to hasten the punishment. If it were not for an appointed time, the punishment would have already come to them. It will come upon them suddenly when they least expect it.

They ask you to hasten the punishment, but Hell will surely encompass the disbelievers. On the Day when the punishment will cover them from above and below, it will be said, 'Taste what you used to do.'

O My servants who believe! My earth is spacious, so worship Me alone. Every soul will taste death, and then you will be returned to Us. Those who believe and do good deeds will be given a home in Heaven, with lofty mansions beneath which rivers flow, to dwell there forever. What an excellent reward for those who do good!

Those who persevere in patience and put their trust in their Lord. How many creatures do not carry their own sustenance? God provides for them and for you. He is the Hearer, the Knower.

If you ask them who created the heavens and the earth and subjected the sun and the moon, they will certainly reply, 'God.' How are they then deluded away from the truth? God enlarges the sustenance for whom He pleases and restricts it for whom He pleases. He has full knowledge of all things.

If you ask them who sends down rain from the sky and gives life to the earth after its death, they will certainly reply, 'God.' Say, 'Praise be to God!' But most of them do not understand.

The life of this world is just amusement and play, but the Home in the Hereafter is the true life, if they only knew. When they embark on a boat, they call on God, making their devotion sincerely to Him. But when He delivers them safely to land, they start associating others with Him."They are ungrateful for Our gifts and indulge in worldly pleasures, but soon they will realize the truth. Do they not see that We have made a secure sanctuary for them while people around them are being taken away by force? Yet, they believe in falsehood and reject God's grace. Who is more unjust than the one who invents lies about God or denies the truth when it comes to them? Surely, there is a home in Hell for those who reject faith.

Those who strive in Our cause, We will guide them to Our paths. God is with those who do good. 

Chapter 30: AL-ROOM (THE ROMANS, THE BYZANTINES)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. Alif. Lam. Mim.
2. The Roman Empire has been defeated
3. In a nearby land, but after their defeat, they will soon be victorious
4. Within a few years. With God is the decision, in the past and in the future. On that day, the believers will rejoice
5. With the help of God. He helps whom He wills, and He is Exalted in Might, Most Merciful.
6. This is the promise of God. God never fails in His promise, but most people do not understand.
7. They only know the outward aspects of the worldly life, but they are heedless of the Hereafter.
8. Do they not reflect within themselves? God did not create the heavens and the earth and everything between them except with truth and for an appointed term. Yet many people deny the meeting with their Lord.
9. Have they not traveled through the earth and seen the end of those before them? They were stronger and cultivated the earth more than these people. Messengers came to them with clear signs, but they wronged themselves by rejecting them.
10. In the end, those who did evil faced a terrible fate because they denied God's signs and mocked them.
11. God begins the process of creation, then repeats it, and then you will be returned to Him.
12. On the Day the Hour is established, the guilty will be struck with despair.
13. They will have no intercessors among their partners, and they will reject their partners.
14. On the Day the Hour is established, people will be sorted out.
15. Those who believed and did good deeds will be made happy in a garden of delight.
16. But those who disbelieved and denied Our signs and the meeting of the Hereafter will be brought to punishment.
17. So glorify God when you reach the evening and when you rise in the morning.
18. To Him belongs praise in the heavens and the earth, and in the late afternoon and when the day begins to decline.
19. He brings out the living from the dead and the dead from the living, and He gives life to the earth after its death. Similarly, you will be brought forth.
20. Among His signs is that He created you from dust, and now you are human beings scattered far and wide.
21. And among His signs is that He created for you mates from among yourselves so that you may find tranquility with them, and He has put love and mercy between your hearts. Indeed, in this are signs for those who reflect.Among His signs is the creation of the heavens and the earth, and the diversity of your languages and colors. These are signs for those who know. Another sign is your sleep by night and day, and your quest for His bounty. These are signs for those who listen. He shows you lightning, both as a fear and a hope, and sends down rain to revive the earth after its death. These are signs for those who understand. The heavens and the earth stand by His command, and when He calls you from the earth, you will emerge. Everything in the heavens and on earth belongs to Him, and all are obedient to Him. He begins creation and then repeats it, and it is easy for Him. He has the highest attributes in the heavens and the earth, and He is the Mighty, the Wise.

He gives you an example from your own experience: Do you have partners among those you possess who share equally in the wealth We have given you? Do you fear them as you fear each other? This is how We explain the signs to people who understand. But the wrongdoers follow their desires without knowledge. Who can guide those whom God has left astray? They have no helpers.

So, set your face towards the true faith, the natural way God has created mankind. There is no changing God's creation. This is the right religion, but most people do not know. Turn to Him in repentance, fear Him, establish regular prayers, and do not be among those who join partners with God. Those who divide their religion and become sects, each group rejoicing in what they have.

When trouble touches people, they cry to their Lord, turning to Him in repentance. But when He gives them a taste of His mercy, some of them associate others with their Lord. This is to show their ingratitude for the favors We have bestowed on them. Enjoy your brief time, but soon you will know your folly. Have We sent down authority to them, which points out to them the things they associate with Him?

When We give people a taste of mercy, they rejoice, but when evil befalls them because of their own deeds, they despair. Do they not see that God enlarges and restricts provision for whom He pleases? These are signs for those who believe. So, give what is due to kindred, the needy, and the wayfarer. This is best for those who seek God's pleasure, and they will prosper.

What you lay out for increase through the property of others will have no increase with God, but what you give in charity, seeking God's pleasure, will be multiplied. God created you, provided for you, will cause you to die, and will give you life again. Are there any of your false partners who can do any of these things? Glory to Him, and He is above the partners they attribute to Him!God is the one who created you, provided for you, causes you to die, and brings you back to life. Can any of your false gods do any of these things? Glory to Him, and He is above what they associate with Him!

Corruption has spread on land and sea because of what people have done. This is so they may taste some of their deeds and turn back from evil. Travel the earth and see the fate of those before you; most of them worshipped others besides God.

Set your face towards the true faith before the Day comes from God that cannot be averted. On that Day, people will be divided. Those who reject faith will suffer, while those who do good will prepare for their own benefit. God will reward those who believe and do good deeds out of His bounty. He does not love those who reject faith.

Among His signs is that He sends the winds as heralds of good news, giving you a taste of His mercy, so that ships may sail by His command and you may seek His bounty and be grateful. We sent messengers to their people with clear signs, and those who transgressed faced retribution. It is our duty to help the believers.

God sends the winds to raise clouds, spreads them in the sky, and breaks them into fragments, causing rain to fall where He wills. Before the rain, people were in despair, but when it falls, they rejoice. Look at the signs of God's mercy, how He revives the earth after its death. He will also raise the dead to life, for He has power over all things.

If We send a wind and they see their crops turn yellow, they will continue in disbelief. You cannot make the dead hear, nor can you make the deaf hear the call when they turn away. You can only make those hear who believe in Our signs and submit.

God created you in a state of weakness, then gave you strength, and then weakness and grey hair after strength. He creates as He wills, and He is the Knower, the Mighty. On the Day of Reckoning, the transgressors will swear they only tarried for an hour, but they were always deceived. Those with knowledge and faith will say that they tarried until the Day of Resurrection, but they were unaware.

On that Day, excuses will not benefit the unjust, nor will they be allowed to make amends. We have given every kind of example in this Quran, but if you bring them a sign, the unbelievers will say you are just tricksters. God seals the hearts of those who do not understand.

So be patient, for God's promise is true. Do not let those who lack certainty shake your firmness.In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

**Chapter 31: Luqman**

**Verses: 34**

**Revealed at: Mecca**

1. Alif. Lam. Mim.
2. These are the verses of the Wise Book,
3. A guide and a mercy for those who do good,
4. Who establish regular prayer, give regular charity, and have firm belief in the Hereafter.
5. They are on true guidance from their Lord, and they are the ones who will prosper.
6. But among people, there are those who buy idle tales without knowledge to mislead others from God's path and make a mockery of it. For them, there is a humiliating penalty.
7. When Our signs are recited to them, they turn away in arrogance as if they did not hear them, as if there is deafness in their ears. Announce to them a grievous penalty.
8. For those who believe and do righteous deeds, there will be Gardens of Bliss,
9. Where they will dwell forever. This is a true promise from God, and He is Exalted in Power, Wise.
10. He created the heavens without visible pillars, set firm mountains on the earth to prevent it from shaking with you, and spread all kinds of creatures across it. We send down rain from the sky and produce every kind of noble creature in pairs.
11. This is God's creation. Show Me what others besides Him have created. Indeed, the wrongdoers are in clear error.
12. We bestowed wisdom on Luqman, saying: "Be grateful to God." Whoever is grateful does so for their own benefit, and whoever is ungrateful, God is free of all wants, worthy of all praise.
13. Luqman said to his son while advising him: "O my son, do not associate anything with God. Indeed, associating others with Him is a great injustice."
14. We have enjoined upon man to be good to his parents. His mother bore him with hardship upon hardship, and his weaning takes two years. Be grateful to Me and to your parents; to Me is the final return.
15. But if they strive to make you associate with Me what you have no knowledge of, do not obey them. Yet, bear them company in this life with justice and consideration, and follow the way of those who turn to Me. In the end, the return of you all is to Me, and I will inform you of what you did.
16. "O my son," said Luqman, "if there is anything as small as a mustard seed, hidden in a rock, in the heavens, or on the earth, God will bring it forth. God understands the finest mysteries and is well-acquainted with them."
17. "O my son, establish regular prayer, enjoin what is just, and forbid what is wrong. Bear with patience whatever befalls you. Indeed, these acts require courage."
18. "Do not turn your cheek in scorn towards people, nor walk arrogantly on the earth. God does not love any arrogant boaster."
19. "Be moderate in your pace and lower your voice. Indeed, the harshest of sounds is the braying of a donkey."
20. Do you not see that God has subjected to your use all things in the heavens and on earth and has made His bounties flow to you in exceeding measure, both seen and unseen? Yet, among people, there are those who dispute about God without knowledge, guidance, or an enlightening book.
21. When they are told to follow what God has sent down, they say: "No, we will follow what we found our fathers following." Even if it is Satan beckoning them to the penalty of the blazing fire?When they are told to follow what God has revealed, they say, "No, we will follow what we found our fathers doing." Even if the devil is leading them to the punishment of the blazing fire?

Whoever submits themselves to God and does good has indeed grasped the most trustworthy handhold. With God rests the end and decision of all matters.

If anyone rejects faith, do not let their rejection grieve you. Their return is to Us, and We will inform them of what they did. God knows well what is in people's hearts.

We grant them enjoyment for a little while, but in the end, We will drive them to a severe punishment.

If you ask them who created the heavens and the earth, they will certainly say, "God." Say, "Praise be to God!" But most of them do not understand.

To God belong all things in the heavens and the earth. God is free of all wants, worthy of all praise.

If all the trees on earth were pens and the ocean were ink, with seven more oceans to add to it, the words of God would not be exhausted. God is Exalted in Power, full of Wisdom.

Your creation and resurrection are like that of a single soul. God is the One who hears and sees all things.

Do you not see that God merges night into day and day into night, and has subjected the sun and the moon to His law, each running its course for an appointed term? God is well-acquainted with all that you do.

This is because God is the only Reality, and whatever else they invoke besides Him is falsehood. God is the Most High, Most Great.

Do you not see that the ships sail through the ocean by the grace of God, so that He may show you His signs? Indeed, in this are signs for all who constantly persevere and give thanks.

When a wave covers them like a canopy, they call to God, offering Him sincere devotion. But when He delivers them safely to land, some of them waver. None reject Our signs except the ungrateful traitors.

O mankind, do your duty to your Lord and fear the coming of a Day when no father can help his son, nor a son help his father. The promise of God is true. Do not let this present life deceive you, nor let the chief deceiver deceive you about God.

Verily, the knowledge of the Hour is with God alone. He sends down the rain and knows what is in the wombs. No one knows what they will earn tomorrow, nor in what land they will die. God is all-knowing and aware.

**Chapter 32: As-Sajda (The Prostration, Worship, Adoration)**

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. Alif. Lam. Mim.
2. This is the revelation of the Book in which there is no doubt, from the Lord of the Worlds.
3. Or do they say, "He has forged it"? No, it is the truth from your Lord, so that you may warn a people to whom no warner has come before you, so that they may receive guidance.
4. God is the One who created the heavens and the earth and all that is between them in six days, and then established Himself on the Throne. You have no protector or intercessor besides Him. Will you not then take heed?
5. He directs all affairs from the heavens to the earth, and then they ascend to Him in a day, the measure of which is a thousand years of your reckoning.He manages everything from the heavens to the earth, and it all returns to Him in a day that is like a thousand years of your reckoning. He knows everything, both hidden and visible, and He is powerful and merciful. He created everything perfectly and began the creation of man from clay. Then He made man's descendants from a simple fluid. He shaped him and breathed into him His spirit, giving him hearing, sight, and hearts, yet little thanks do people give.

They ask, "When we are lost in the earth, will we be recreated?" They deny the meeting with their Lord. Say, "The Angel of Death, who is in charge of you, will take your souls, and then you will be returned to your Lord." If only you could see when the guilty ones will bow their heads before their Lord, saying, "Our Lord, we have seen and heard. Send us back, and we will do good deeds. We now believe."

If We had willed, We could have given every soul its guidance, but My word will come true: "I will fill Hell with jinn and humans together." So taste the punishment for forgetting this Day. We will forget you. Taste the eternal penalty for your deeds. Only those who believe in Our signs, when they are recited to them, fall down in prostration and praise their Lord without pride. They forsake their beds to call on their Lord in fear and hope and spend in charity from what We have given them. No one knows what delights are kept hidden for them as a reward for their good deeds.

Is the believer like the wicked? They are not equal. Those who believe and do good deeds will have gardens as their homes, a reward for their deeds. But the rebellious and wicked will have the Fire as their abode. Whenever they try to escape, they will be forced back and told, "Taste the penalty of the Fire you used to deny." We will make them taste the lesser punishment before the greater one so that they may return.

Who does more wrong than the one who turns away from the signs of his Lord? We will exact retribution from the transgressors. We gave the Book to Moses, so do not doubt its reaching you. We made it a guide for the Children of Israel. We appointed leaders from among them who guided by Our command when they were patient and believed firmly in Our signs. Your Lord will judge between them on the Day of Resurrection concerning their differences.

Does it not teach them a lesson how many generations We destroyed before them, whose dwellings they now walk through? There are signs in this. Do they not listen? Do they not see that We drive rain to parched soil and produce crops for their cattle and themselves? Have they no vision? They ask, "When will this decision be if you are telling the truth?"They ask, "When will this judgment happen if you are truthful?" Say, "On the Day of Decision, it will be too late for unbelievers to believe, and they will not be given any respite." So, turn away from them and wait, for they too are waiting.

Chapter 33: AL-AHZAB (THE CLANS, THE COALITION, THE COMBINED FORCES)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

O Prophet! Fear God and do not listen to the unbelievers and hypocrites. God is full of Knowledge and Wisdom. Follow what is revealed to you from your Lord, for God is aware of all that you do. Put your trust in God, for He is sufficient as a disposer of affairs.

God has not made for any man two hearts in his body, nor has He made your wives whom you divorce by Zihar your mothers, nor has He made your adopted sons your real sons. These are just words from your mouths. But God speaks the truth and shows the right way. Call them by their fathers' names; that is more just in the sight of God. If you do not know their fathers, then they are your brothers in faith and your friends. There is no blame on you if you make a mistake, but what counts is the intention of your hearts. God is Oft-Returning, Most Merciful.

The Prophet is closer to the believers than their own selves, and his wives are their mothers. Blood-relations have closer personal ties in the decree of God than the Brotherhood of Believers and Muhajirs. Nevertheless, do what is just to your closest friends; this is written in the decree of God.

Remember when We took a covenant from the prophets, including you, Noah, Abraham, Moses, and Jesus, son of Mary. We took from them a solemn covenant so that God may question the custodians of truth about their truthfulness. He has prepared a grievous penalty for the unbelievers.

O believers! Remember the grace of God when hosts came down upon you, and We sent against them a hurricane and forces you could not see. God sees all that you do. When they came upon you from above and below, your eyes dimmed, and your hearts reached your throats, and you imagined various thoughts about God. In that situation, the believers were tried and shaken with a tremendous shaking.

The hypocrites and those with a disease in their hearts said, "God and His Messenger promised us nothing but delusion!" A party among them said, "O people of Yathrib! You cannot stand the attack, so go back!" And a band of them asked for leave of the Prophet, saying, "Our houses are exposed," though they were not. They intended nothing but to run away.

If the enemy had entered from all sides and incited them to sedition, they would have committed it with little hesitation. They had already covenanted with God not to turn their backs, and a covenant with God must be answered for. Say, "Running away will not profit you if you flee from death or slaughter; even if you escape, you will only enjoy a brief respite." Say, "Who can protect you from God if He wishes to punish or show mercy to you?"Say: "Who can protect you from God if He intends harm or mercy for you?" They will find no protector or helper besides God.

God knows those among you who hold back and those who say to their brothers, "Come to us," but they hardly join the fight.

They are stingy towards you. When fear comes, you see them looking at you with eyes rolling like someone fainting from death. But when the fear is gone, they attack you with sharp tongues, greedy for wealth. They have no faith, so God nullifies their deeds, and that is easy for God.

They think the Confederates have not withdrawn. If the Confederates come again, they would wish to be in the desert with the Bedouins, asking for news about you. If they were among you, they would fight very little.

Indeed, in the Messenger of God, you have a good example for anyone who hopes in God and the Last Day and remembers God often.

When the believers saw the Confederate forces, they said, "This is what God and His Messenger promised us, and God and His Messenger told the truth." It only increased their faith and submission.

Among the believers are men who have been true to their covenant with God. Some have fulfilled their vow by death, and some are still waiting. They have not changed in the least.

God will reward the truthful for their truth and punish the hypocrites if He wills, or turn to them in mercy. God is Forgiving, Merciful.

God turned back the unbelievers in their rage; they gained no advantage. God sufficed the believers in battle. God is Strong, Mighty.

He brought down those of the People of the Book who supported them from their strongholds and cast terror into their hearts. Some you killed, and some you took as prisoners.

He made you heirs of their lands, houses, and goods, and of a land you had not frequented before. God has power over all things.

O Prophet! Say to your wives: "If you desire the life of this world and its glitter, come! I will provide for your enjoyment and set you free in a handsome manner."

But if you seek God and His Messenger and the Hereafter, God has prepared a great reward for the good among you.

O wives of the Prophet! If any of you commits evident unseemly conduct, her punishment will be doubled, and that is easy for God.

But any of you who is devout in the service of God and His Messenger and works righteousness, will receive her reward twice, and We have prepared for her a generous sustenance.

O wives of the Prophet! You are not like other women. If you fear God, do not be too soft in speech, lest one in whose heart is a disease should be moved with desire. Speak justly.

Stay quietly in your houses and do not make a dazzling display like that of the former Times of Ignorance. Establish regular prayer, give regular charity, and obey God and His Messenger. God only wishes to remove all abomination from you, O Members of the Family, and to make you pure and spotless."God only desires to keep you pure and free from any impurity, O people of the House! Remember and recite the signs of God and His wisdom that are shared in your homes. God understands the finest mysteries and is well-acquainted with them.

For Muslim men and women, for believing men and women, for devout men and women, for truthful men and women, for patient and constant men and women, for humble men and women, for those who give in charity, for those who fast, for those who guard their chastity, and for those who engage much in God's praise—God has prepared forgiveness and a great reward.

It is not fitting for a believing man or woman, when God and His Messenger have decided a matter, to have any option about their decision. Anyone who disobeys God and His Messenger is on a clearly wrong path.

You said to the one who had received God's grace and your favor, 'Keep your wife and fear God.' But you hid in your heart what God was about to make manifest; you feared the people, but it is more fitting that you should fear God. When Zaid had dissolved his marriage with her, We joined her in marriage to you so that there may be no difficulty for believers in marrying the wives of their adopted sons after they have dissolved their marriages. God's command must be fulfilled.

There is no difficulty for the Prophet in what God has indicated to him as a duty. This was the practice approved by God among those who have passed away. God's command is a decree determined.

Those who preach the messages of God and fear Him, and fear none but God, are sufficient to call men to account. Muhammad is not the father of any of your men, but he is the Messenger of God and the Seal of the Prophets. God has full knowledge of all things.

O believers! Remember God often and glorify Him morning and evening. He sends blessings on you, as do His angels, to bring you out from the depths of darkness into light. He is full of mercy to the believers. Their greeting on the Day they meet Him will be 'Peace!' and He has prepared for them a generous reward.

O Prophet! We have sent you as a witness, a bearer of glad tidings, and a warner, and as one who invites to God's grace by His leave, and as a lamp spreading light. Give the glad tidings to the believers that they shall have a great bounty from God.

Do not obey the unbelievers and the hypocrites, and disregard their annoyances. Put your trust in God, for He is sufficient as a Disposer of affairs.

O believers! When you marry believing women and then divorce them before you have touched them, there is no waiting period for them. Give them a present and set them free in a handsome manner.

O Prophet! We have made lawful to you your wives to whom you have paid their dowers, and those whom your right hand possesses out of the prisoners of war whom God has assigned to you, and the daughters of your paternal uncles and aunts, and the daughters of your maternal uncles and aunts who migrated with you, and any believing woman who dedicates her soul to the Prophet if he wishes to wed her. This is only for you and not for the believers at large. We know what We have ordained for them."O Prophet! We have made lawful for you your wives to whom you have given their dowries, and those whom your right hand possesses from the captives of war that God has given you, and the daughters of your paternal uncles and aunts, and the daughters of your maternal uncles and aunts who migrated with you. Also, any believing woman who offers herself to the Prophet, if the Prophet wishes to marry her—this is a privilege for you only, not for the rest of the believers. We know what We have ordained for them regarding their wives and those whom their right hands possess, so there should be no difficulty for you. God is Forgiving and Merciful.

You may defer the turn of any of them that you please, and you may receive any you please. There is no blame on you if you invite one whose turn you had set aside. This is better for their comfort, to prevent their grief, and to ensure their satisfaction with what you give them. God knows what is in your hearts, and God is All-Knowing, Most Forbearing.

It is not lawful for you to marry more women after this, nor to change them for other wives, even if their beauty attracts you, except those whom your right hand possesses. God is Watchful over all things.

O believers! Do not enter the Prophet's houses unless permission is given to you for a meal, and do not wait for its preparation. When you are invited, enter, and when you have taken your meal, disperse without lingering for conversation. Such behavior annoys the Prophet, but he is too shy to ask you to leave. God is not shy of the truth. When you ask his wives for anything, ask them from behind a screen. This is purer for your hearts and their hearts. It is not right for you to annoy God's Messenger or to marry his widows after him. Truly, this is a grave offense in God's sight.

Whether you reveal anything or conceal it, God has full knowledge of all things.

There is no blame on the Prophet's wives if they appear before their fathers, their sons, their brothers, their brothers' sons, their sisters' sons, their women, or their slaves. O women, fear God, for God is Witness to all things.

God and His angels send blessings on the Prophet. O believers, send blessings on him and salute him with all respect.

Those who annoy God and His Messenger are cursed by God in this world and the Hereafter, and a humiliating punishment is prepared for them.

Those who annoy believing men and women undeservedly bear the guilt of slander and manifest sin.

O Prophet! Tell your wives, daughters, and the believing women to cast their outer garments over themselves when they go out. This is more appropriate so that they may be recognized and not molested. God is Forgiving and Merciful.

If the hypocrites, those with a disease in their hearts, and those who stir up sedition in the city do not desist, We shall certainly stir you up against them. Then they will not be able to stay in it as your neighbors for any length of time. They shall be cursed, seized wherever found, and slain without mercy.This has always been God's way with those who came before, and you will not find any change in God's way.

People ask you about the Hour. Say, "Only God knows about it." How can you understand? The Hour might be near!

God has cursed the disbelievers and prepared a blazing fire for them, where they will stay forever without any protector or helper. On the Day their faces are turned upside down in the Fire, they will say, "Oh, we wish we had obeyed God and His Messenger!" They will also say, "Our Lord, we followed our leaders and they led us astray. Our Lord, give them double the punishment and curse them greatly."

Believers, do not be like those who insulted Moses. God cleared him of their false accusations, and he was honorable in God's sight. Believers, fear God and always speak the truth. He will make your conduct right and forgive your sins. Whoever obeys God and His Messenger has achieved the highest success.

We offered the Trust to the heavens, the earth, and the mountains, but they refused to bear it and were afraid. However, man undertook it, and he was indeed unjust and foolish. As a result, God will punish hypocritical men and women and disbelieving men and women, but He will turn in mercy to believing men and women. God is Forgiving and Merciful.

Chapter 34: SABA (SABA, SHEBA)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

Praise be to God, to whom belongs everything in the heavens and on earth. Praise Him in the Hereafter too. He is Wise and Aware. He knows everything that goes into the earth and comes out of it, everything that descends from the sky and ascends to it. He is the Most Merciful, the Oft-Forgiving.

The disbelievers say, "The Hour will never come to us." Say, "By my Lord, it will surely come to you. He knows the unseen, and not even an atom's weight escapes Him in the heavens or on earth. Everything is in a clear record." This is so He may reward those who believe and do good deeds. For them, there is forgiveness and a generous provision. But those who strive against Our signs to frustrate them will face a humiliating punishment.

Those who have been given knowledge see that what has been revealed to you from your Lord is the truth and guides to the path of the Mighty, the Praised. The disbelievers say mockingly, "Shall we show you a man who claims that when you are scattered into pieces, you will be raised in a new creation?" They say, "Has he invented a lie against God, or is he possessed?" No, it is those who do not believe in the Hereafter who are in torment and far error.

Do they not see what is before them and behind them in the sky and the earth? If We wished, We could cause the earth to swallow them or make a piece of the sky fall upon them. Surely, in this is a sign for every servant who turns to God in repentance."land or bring down a portion from the sky; surely there is a sign in this for every servant who turns to God."

We granted David a special favor from Us: "O mountains, echo God's praises with him, and you birds too!" We made iron soft for him, saying, "Make coats of mail, balancing the rings well, and do good deeds. I see everything you do."

To Solomon, We made the wind obedient: its morning journey was a month's travel, and its evening journey was a month's travel. We made a fountain of molten brass flow for him, and some jinn worked under his command by his Lord's permission. If any of them disobeyed, We made them taste the penalty of the blazing fire.

They made for him whatever he desired: arches, images, basins as large as reservoirs, and fixed cauldrons. "Work, O family of David, with gratitude!" But few of My servants are truly grateful.

When We decreed Solomon's death, nothing indicated his death to them except a little worm of the earth, which kept gnawing away at his staff. When he fell, the jinn realized that if they had known the unseen, they would not have remained in humiliating toil.

There was a sign for Sheba in their homeland: two gardens on the right and the left. "Eat from your Lord's provision and be grateful to Him: a good land and a forgiving Lord." But they turned away, so We sent against them the flood from the dams, and We converted their two gardens into gardens producing bitter fruit, tamarisks, and a few stunted lote-trees.

This was their recompense for their ingratitude. We do not punish anyone except the ungrateful. Between them and the cities We had blessed, We placed prominent cities and appointed stages of journey in due proportion: "Travel safely by night and day." But they said, "Our Lord, make the distances between our journey-stages longer," and they wronged themselves. So We made them as a tale and scattered them in fragments. Surely, in this are signs for every patient and grateful person.

Satan proved his idea true about them, and they followed him, except for a group of true believers. He had no authority over them, except that We might test who believes in the Hereafter from who is in doubt about it. Your Lord watches over all things.

Say, "Call upon those you claim besides God. They do not possess even an atom's weight in the heavens or on earth, nor do they have any share in either, nor is any of them a helper to God." No intercession will be of any use with Him except for those He permits. When fear is removed from their hearts, they will say, "What did your Lord say?" They will say, "The truth." He is the Most High, the Great.

Say, "Who provides for you from the heavens and the earth?" Say, "God. Surely, either we or you are on right guidance or in manifest error." Say, "You will not be questioned about our sins, nor will we be questioned about what you do." Say, "Our Lord will gather us together and will decide the matter between us in truth and justice.""He is the one to decide, the One Who knows all." 

Say: "Our Lord will bring us all together, then He will judge between us with truth. He is the All-knowing Judge."

Say: "Show me those whom you have joined with Him as partners. You cannot do it! He is God, the Mighty, the Wise."

We have sent you, Muhammad, as a universal Messenger to all people, bringing good news and warning them, but most people do not understand.

They ask, "When will this promise come to pass if you are telling the truth?"

Say: "The appointment is for a Day you cannot delay or advance by even an hour."

The disbelievers say, "We will not believe in this scripture or any that came before it." If only you could see when the wrongdoers are made to stand before their Lord, blaming each other! Those who were oppressed will say to the arrogant ones, "If it weren't for you, we would have been believers!"

The arrogant ones will respond, "Did we stop you from guidance after it reached you? No, you were the ones who transgressed."

The oppressed will say, "No, it was your scheming day and night, telling us to disbelieve in God and set up equals to Him." They will be filled with regret when they see the punishment, and We will put shackles on the necks of the disbelievers. They will only be repaid for what they did.

Whenever We sent a warner to a population, the wealthy ones among them said, "We do not believe in the message you have been sent with."

They said, "We have more wealth and children, and we will not be punished."

Say: "My Lord enlarges and restricts provision for whom He pleases, but most people do not understand."

It is not your wealth or your children that bring you closer to Us, but those who believe and do good deeds. They will have a multiplied reward and will reside securely in high places.

Those who strive against Our signs to frustrate them will be given over to punishment.

Say: "My Lord enlarges and restricts sustenance for whom He pleases. Whatever you spend in His cause, He replaces it. He is the Best of Providers."

One day, He will gather them all together and say to the angels, "Was it you that these people used to worship?"

They will say, "Glory to You! You are our Protector, not them. They worshipped the jinn; most of them believed in them."

On that day, they will have no power over each other for profit or harm. We will say to the wrongdoers, "Taste the penalty of the Fire, which you used to deny."

When Our clear signs are recited to them, they say, "This is just a man who wants to turn you away from what your fathers worshipped." They say, "This is a lie invented!" The disbelievers say of the truth when it comes to them, "This is nothing but evident magic!"

We did not give them any books to study, nor did We send messengers to them before you as warners.

Their predecessors also rejected the truth; these people have not received even a tenth of what We granted to those before them. Yet when they rejected My messengers, how terrible was My rejection of them!Those before them also rejected the truth, and these people haven't even received a tenth of what was given to their predecessors. Yet, they still denied My messengers. How severe was My disapproval of them!

Say: "I advise you on one thing: Stand up for God, whether in pairs or alone, and reflect. Your companion is not possessed; he is only a warner to you of a severe punishment."

Say: "I do not ask for any reward from you; my reward is only from God. He is a witness over all things."

Say: "My Lord reveals the truth. He knows everything hidden."

Say: "The truth has come, and falsehood neither creates anything new nor restores anything."

Say: "If I am wrong, I only harm myself. But if I am guided, it is because of what my Lord reveals to me. He hears all things and is always near."

If you could see when they are terrified with no escape and are seized from a close position, they will say, "We now believe in the truth." But how can they attain faith from such a distant place?

They disbelieved before and cast slanders on the unseen from afar. A barrier will be placed between them and their desires, just as it was done with their predecessors. They were indeed in suspicious doubt.

Chapter 35: FATIR (THE ANGELS, ORIGINATOR)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

Praise be to God, who created the heavens and the earth and made the angels messengers with wings—two, three, or four pairs. He adds to creation as He pleases, for God has power over all things.

Whatever mercy God bestows on mankind, no one can withhold it. And whatever He withholds, no one can grant it apart from Him. He is the Exalted in Power, full of Wisdom.

O people! Remember God's grace upon you. Is there any creator other than God who provides for you from the sky and the earth? There is no god but Him. How then are you deluded away from the truth?

If they reject you, messengers before you were also rejected. All affairs return to God for decision.

O people! The promise of God is true. Do not let this present life deceive you, nor let the Chief Deceiver deceive you about God.

Satan is an enemy to you, so treat him as an enemy. He only invites his followers to become companions of the Blazing Fire.

For those who reject God, there is a terrible penalty. But for those who believe and do righteous deeds, there is forgiveness and a magnificent reward.

Is the one whose evil deeds are made to seem attractive to him, so he considers them good, equal to one who is rightly guided? God leads astray whom He wills and guides whom He wills. Do not let your soul waste away in grief for them. God knows well all that they do.

It is God who sends forth the winds, raising the clouds. We drive them to a dead land and revive the earth after its death. This is how the Resurrection will be.

If anyone seeks glory and power, know that all glory and power belong to God. Pure words ascend to Him, and He exalts righteous deeds. Those who plot evil will face a terrible penalty, and their plotting will come to nothing.

God created you from dust, then from a sperm-drop, then He...God created you from dust, then from a tiny drop of fluid, and then made you into pairs (male and female). No woman becomes pregnant or gives birth without His knowledge. No one lives a long life or has their life shortened without it being recorded in a decree. This is easy for God.

The two bodies of water are not alike: one is fresh, sweet, and good to drink, while the other is salty and bitter. Yet, from both, you eat fresh meat and extract ornaments to wear. You see ships sailing through them so you may seek God's bounty and be grateful.

God merges night into day and day into night. He has subjected the sun and the moon, each running its course for an appointed term. This is God, your Lord; to Him belongs all dominion. Those you call upon besides Him have no power.

If you call upon them, they will not hear you, and even if they could hear, they cannot answer you. On the Day of Judgment, they will reject your partnership. None can inform you like the One who is aware of all things.

O people! You are in need of God, but God is free of all wants and worthy of all praise. If He wills, He can remove you and bring a new creation. This is not difficult for God.

No soul burdened with sin can bear the burden of another. If a heavily laden soul calls for help, none of its burden will be carried, even by a close relative. You can only warn those who fear their Lord in secret and establish regular prayer. Whoever purifies themselves does so for their own benefit. The final destination is to God.

The blind and the seeing are not alike, nor are darkness and light, nor are the cool shade and the scorching heat. The living and the dead are not alike. God makes whom He wills to hear, but you cannot make those in the graves hear.

You are only a warner. We have sent you with the truth, as a bearer of good news and a warner. There has never been a people without a warner among them. If they reject you, so did those before them. Their messengers came with clear signs, scriptures, and the enlightening book.

In the end, I punished those who rejected faith, and how terrible was My rejection of them!

Do you not see that God sends down rain from the sky, and with it, We bring forth produce of various colors? In the mountains, there are tracts of white, red, and intense black. Among people, animals, and cattle, there are also various colors. Only those who have knowledge truly fear God. God is mighty and forgiving.

Those who recite the Book of God, establish regular prayer, and spend in charity secretly and openly hope for a reward that will never fail. God will pay them their due and give them even more out of His bounty. He is forgiving and appreciative.

What We have revealed to you of the Book is the truth, confirming what was revealed before it. God is well-acquainted and fully observant of His servants.What we have revealed to you from the Book is the truth, confirming what was revealed before it. God is fully aware and observant of His servants.

We have given the Book as an inheritance to those of Our servants whom We have chosen. Among them, some wrong their own souls, some follow a middle course, and some, by God's permission, are foremost in good deeds. This is the highest grace.

They will enter Gardens of Eternity, adorned with bracelets of gold and pearls, and their garments will be of silk. They will say, "Praise be to God, who has removed all sorrow from us. Our Lord is indeed forgiving and appreciative."

God, out of His bounty, has settled us in a home that will last forever, where no toil or weariness will touch us.

But those who reject God will face the Fire of Hell. They will neither die nor will its penalty be lightened for them. This is how We reward the ungrateful.

In Hell, they will cry out, "Our Lord! Bring us out; we will do righteous deeds, different from what we used to do." But it will be said to them, "Did We not give you a long enough life for anyone who would reflect to do so? And a warner came to you. So taste the consequences of your deeds, for the wrongdoers have no helper."

God knows all the hidden things of the heavens and the earth. He is fully aware of what is in people's hearts.

He has made you inheritors on the earth. If anyone rejects God, their rejection works against themselves. Their disbelief only increases their loss and the odium in the sight of their Lord.

Say, "Have you seen these 'partners' you call upon besides God? Show me what they have created on the earth, or do they have a share in the heavens? Or have We given them a Book from which they derive clear evidence? No, the wrongdoers promise each other nothing but delusions."

God sustains the heavens and the earth, lest they cease to function. If they were to fail, no one could sustain them after Him. He is Most Forbearing, Oft-Forgiving.

They swore their strongest oaths by God that if a warner came to them, they would follow his guidance better than any other people. But when a warner came to them, it only increased their aversion.

This was due to their arrogance in the land and their plotting of evil. But the plotting of evil will only trap its authors. Are they waiting for anything except the way the ancients were dealt with? You will not find any change in God's way of dealing, nor will you find any turning off in God's way of dealing.

Have they not traveled through the earth and seen the end of those before them, who were superior in strength? God is not to be frustrated by anything in the heavens or on earth. He is All-Knowing, All-Powerful.

If God were to punish people according to what they deserve, He would not leave a single living creature on the earth. But He gives them respite for a stated term. When their term expires, God is fully aware of His servants.In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

Ya Seen. By the wise Qur'an, you are indeed one of the messengers, on a straight path. This is a revelation from the Mighty, the Merciful, so that you may warn a people whose ancestors were not warned, and thus they are heedless. The word has already proven true against most of them, for they do not believe. We have placed yokes around their necks up to their chins, so their heads are forced up. We have put a barrier in front of them and a barrier behind them, and covered them so they cannot see. It is the same whether you warn them or not; they will not believe.

You can only warn those who follow the message and fear the Most Gracious in secret. Give them good news of forgiveness and a generous reward. We will surely bring the dead to life and record what they have sent ahead and what they have left behind. Everything is recorded in a clear book.

Tell them the story of the people of the city when messengers came to them. We sent two messengers, but they rejected them. So, We reinforced them with a third, and they said, "We have been sent to you." The people replied, "You are just humans like us. The Most Gracious has not revealed anything; you are lying." The messengers said, "Our Lord knows that we have been sent to you, and our duty is only to deliver the clear message."

The people said, "We see an evil omen in you. If you do not stop, we will stone you, and a painful punishment will befall you." The messengers replied, "Your evil omen is with yourselves. Is it because you are reminded of the truth? No, you are a transgressing people."

Then a man came running from the farthest part of the city, saying, "O my people, follow the messengers. Follow those who do not ask for any reward and are rightly guided. Why should I not worship the One who created me and to whom you will be returned? Should I take other gods besides Him? If the Most Gracious intends harm for me, their intercession will not help me, nor can they save me. I would then be in clear error. I believe in your Lord, so listen to me."

It was said to him, "Enter Paradise." He said, "If only my people knew how my Lord has forgiven me and made me one of the honored ones." We did not send any hosts from heaven against his people after him, nor do We ever send such. It was just one mighty blast, and they were extinguished.

Alas for the servants! No messenger comes to them but they mock him. Do they not see how many generations We destroyed before them? They will not return to them, but all of them will be brought before Us.

A sign for them is the dead earth. We give it life and produce grain from it, which they eat. We have placed gardens of date-palms and vines, and caused springs to gush forth therein.We create gardens of date palms and grapevines and make springs of water flow within them. This is so people can enjoy the fruits, which they did not create with their own hands. Will they not then be grateful?

Glory to God, who created all things in pairs, including what the earth produces, their own kind, and things they do not know.

A sign for them is the night; We strip the day from it, and they are left in darkness. The sun runs its course for a determined period; this is the decree of the Mighty, the All-Knowing. The moon has phases until it returns like an old, withered date stalk. The sun cannot overtake the moon, nor can the night outstrip the day. Each floats in its own orbit.

A sign for them is that We carried their ancestors in the loaded Ark. We created similar vessels for them to ride. If We willed, We could drown them, and there would be no one to help or save them, except by Our mercy and for their temporary enjoyment.

When they are told, "Fear what is before you and what is behind you, so you may receive mercy," they turn away. No sign comes to them from their Lord, but they turn away from it. When they are told, "Spend from what God has provided you," the disbelievers say to the believers, "Shall we feed those whom God could have fed if He willed? You are in clear error."

They ask, "When will this promise come to pass if you are truthful?" They await but a single blast, which will seize them while they are disputing. They will not be able to make a will or return to their families.

The trumpet will be blown, and they will rush forth from their graves to their Lord. They will say, "Woe to us! Who has raised us from our resting place?" This is what the Most Gracious had promised, and the messengers spoke the truth. It will be but a single blast, and they will all be brought before Us.

On that day, no soul will be wronged, and you will only be repaid for what you used to do. The companions of the Garden will be joyfully occupied. They and their spouses will be in pleasant shade, reclining on thrones. They will have fruits and whatever they desire. "Peace!" - a word from a Merciful Lord.

But to the guilty, it will be said, "Get apart this day! Did I not enjoin on you, O children of Adam, that you should not worship Satan, for he is your open enemy, and that you should worship Me? This is the straight path. Yet he led astray a great multitude of you. Did you not understand? This is the Hell you were warned about. Enter it today because you disbelieved."

On that day, We will seal their mouths, and their hands will speak to Us, and their feet will bear witness to what they used to do. If We willed, We could have blotted out their eyes, and they would struggle to find the way. How could they see?If it had been Our will, We could have immobilized them in their places, making them unable to move forward or turn back. If We grant someone a long life, We reverse their development, making them weak after being strong. Do they not understand?

We did not teach the Prophet poetry, nor is it fitting for him. This is a clear message and a Qur'an to warn those who are alive and to confirm the truth against the disbelievers. Do they not see that We created cattle for them, which they own and use for riding and food? They also get other benefits and drinks from them. Will they not be grateful?

Yet, they worship other gods besides God, hoping for help. These gods cannot help them; instead, they will be brought before Us for judgment. Do not let their words grieve you, Muhammad. We know what they hide and what they reveal.

Doesn't man see that We created him from a drop of seed, yet he becomes an open adversary? He forgets his own creation and asks, "Who can give life to these decomposed bones?" Say, "He who created them the first time will give them life again. He is knowledgeable about every creation."

He who produces fire from green trees for you, is He not able to create the like of them? Yes, indeed! He is the Creator Supreme, with infinite skill and knowledge. When He intends a thing, He simply says, "Be," and it is.

So, glory to Him in whose hands is the dominion of all things, and to Him, you will all be brought back.

Chapter 37: AS-SAAFFAT (THOSE WHO SET THE RANKS, DRAWN UP IN RANKS)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

By those who range themselves in ranks, and those who drive away evil, and those who recite the message, your God is one. He is the Lord of the heavens and the earth and all that is between them, and the Lord of every point at the rising of the sun.

We have adorned the lowest heaven with stars for beauty and as a guard against rebellious evil spirits. They cannot listen to the exalted assembly and are pelted from every side, outcast, and under perpetual torment. Except for those who snatch something by stealth, they are pursued by a flaming fire.

Ask them, "Are they more difficult to create, or the other beings We have created?" We created them from sticky clay. You marvel while they ridicule, and when they are admonished, they pay no heed. When they see a sign, they mock and say, "This is nothing but evident sorcery!"

They ask, "What! When we die and become dust and bones, shall we be raised up again, along with our forefathers?" Say, "Yes, and you will be humiliated." It will be a single compelling cry, and they will begin to see. They will say, "Ah! Woe to us! This is the Day of Judgment!""This is the Day of Judgment, the day you denied!" A voice will declare, "This is the Day of Sorting Out, which you used to deny." It will be said, "Bring forth the wrongdoers and their spouses, and everything they worshipped besides God, and lead them to the path of Hell. But stop them, for they must be questioned: 'What is wrong with you that you do not help each other?'" On that day, they will submit to judgment and turn to one another, questioning each other. They will say, "You used to come to us with authority!" But the others will reply, "No, you were not believers. We had no power over you; you were a rebellious people. Now the word of our Lord has come true against us; we will taste the punishment. We led you astray because we were astray ourselves." On that day, they will all share in the penalty. This is how We deal with the guilty. When they were told, "There is no god but God," they were arrogant and said, "Should we abandon our gods for a mad poet?" But he brought the truth and confirmed the previous messengers. Now you will taste the painful punishment, a retribution for what you did. But the sincere servants of God will have a known provision: fruits and honor in the Gardens of Delight, facing each other on thrones. They will be served a cup from a clear-flowing fountain, crystal-white and delicious to drink, free from headiness and intoxication. With them will be chaste women with beautiful eyes, as if they were delicate eggs closely guarded. They will turn to one another and question each other. One will say, "I had a close companion who used to say, 'Do you really believe in the truth? When we die and become dust and bones, will we really be judged?'" He will look down and see his companion in the midst of the Fire and say, "By God, you almost ruined me! If it were not for the grace of my Lord, I would have been among those brought to doom." They will say, "Are we not to die except for our first death, and we will not be punished?" This is the supreme achievement. For this, let all strive who wish to strive. Is this better as an entertainment or the tree of Zaqqum? We have made it a trial for the wrongdoers. It is a tree that springs from the bottom of Hell, with fruit like the heads of devils. They will eat from it and fill their bellies, then drink boiling water. Their return will be to the Blazing Fire. They found their fathers on the wrong path, and they rushed to follow in their footsteps. Many of the ancients went astray before them.Most of the people from ancient times went astray before them. We sent messengers to warn them, but they didn't listen. Look at what happened to those who ignored the warnings. Only the sincere servants of God were saved. 

Noah called out to Us, and We heard his prayer. We saved him and his people from the great calamity and made his descendants the survivors. We left a blessing for him among future generations: "Peace be upon Noah among the nations!" This is how We reward those who do right, for he was one of Our believing servants. The rest were overwhelmed by the Flood.

Among those who followed Noah's way was Abraham. He approached his Lord with a pure heart and questioned his father and people about their worship of false gods. He challenged their beliefs and turned away from their idols. When they tried to harm him, We saved him and made them the ones humiliated. Abraham said, "I will go to my Lord; He will guide me." He prayed for a righteous son, and We gave him the good news of a patient and forbearing boy.

When the boy was old enough to work with him, Abraham told him about his vision to sacrifice him. The son agreed, showing patience and faith. As they submitted to God's will, We called out to Abraham, telling him he had fulfilled the vision. We ransomed the boy with a great sacrifice and left a blessing for Abraham among future generations: "Peace be upon Abraham!" This is how We reward those who do right, for he was one of Our believing servants.

We also gave Abraham the good news of Isaac, a prophet among the righteous. We blessed both Abraham and Isaac, and among their descendants, some do right while others wrong themselves.

We bestowed Our favor on Moses and Aaron, delivering them and their people from great distress. We helped them overcome their troubles and gave them the clear Scripture, guiding them to the right path. We left a blessing for them among future generations: "Peace be upon Moses and Aaron!" This is how We reward those who do right, for they were two of Our believing servants.Elias was also one of the messengers sent by Us. He asked his people, "Will you not fear God? Will you call upon Baal and forsake the Best of Creators, God, your Lord and the Lord of your forefathers?" But they rejected him, and they will certainly face punishment, except for the sincere servants of God. We left a blessing for him among future generations: "Peace be upon Elias!" This is how We reward those who do right, for he was one of Our believing servants.

Lot was also one of the messengers. We saved him and his followers, except for an old woman who lagged behind. Then We destroyed the rest. You pass by their ruins by day and by night; will you not understand?

Jonah was also one of the messengers. When he ran away to a fully laden ship, he drew lots and was thrown overboard. The big fish swallowed him, and he had done acts worthy of blame. Had he not repented and glorified God, he would have remained inside the fish until the Day of Resurrection. But We cast him forth on the shore while he was sick, and caused a gourd plant to grow over him. We sent him to a hundred thousand or more, and they believed, so We allowed them to enjoy their life for a while.

Ask them: Does your Lord have daughters while they have sons? Did We create the angels as females while they were witnesses? They lie when they say, "God has begotten children." They are liars! Did He choose daughters over sons? What is the matter with you? How do you judge? Will you not then receive admonition? Do you have clear authority? Then bring your book if you are truthful. They have invented a relationship between God and the jinn, but the jinn know they will be brought before Him. Glory to God! He is free from what they ascribe to Him. Not so the sincere servants of God.

Neither you nor those you worship can lead anyone into temptation concerning God, except those who are destined for the blazing Fire. Those ranged in ranks say, "Not one of us but has a place appointed; we are ranged in ranks for service, and we declare God's glory!"

They used to say, "If only we had a message from those of old, we would certainly have been sincere servants of God." But now that the Qur'an has come, they reject it. Soon they will know! Our word has already been passed to our servants sent by Us, that they would certainly be assisted and that Our forces must conquer. So turn away from them for a little while and watch them; they will soon see. Do they wish to hurry on our punishment? When it descends upon them, it will be a terrible morning for those who were warned but did not heed. So turn away from them for a little while."Turn away from them for a while and watch; they will soon see. Glory to your Lord, the Lord of Honor and Power! He is free from what they ascribe to Him. Peace be upon the messengers! Praise be to God, the Lord of the Worlds.

Chapter 38: Sad (The Letter Sad)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

Sad. By the Qur'an, full of admonition. But the unbelievers are steeped in self-glory and separatism. How many generations before them did We destroy? They cried for mercy when it was too late to be saved. They wonder that a warner has come to them from among themselves, and the unbelievers say, 'This is a sorcerer telling lies!' They say, 'Has he made the gods into one God? This is a strange thing!' The leaders among them go away impatiently, saying, 'Remain constant to your gods! This is a plot against you!' They say, 'We never heard of this in the former faith; this is nothing but a made-up tale!'

They question why the message was sent to him among all people. They doubt My message and have not yet tasted My punishment. Do they have the treasures of the mercy of your Lord, the Exalted in Power, the Grantor of Bounties without measure? Or do they have dominion over the heavens and the earth and all between? If so, let them ascend by ropes! But they will be put to flight, even a host of confederates.

Before them, many rejected messengers: the people of Noah, 'Ad, and Pharaoh, the Lord of Stakes, and Thamud, the people of Lot, and the Companions of the Wood. All of them denied the messengers, and My punishment was justified. They only wait for a single mighty blast, which will brook no delay. They say, 'Our Lord! Hasten to us our sentence before the Day of Account!'

Have patience with what they say, and remember Our servant David, the man of strength, who always turned to God. We made the hills declare Our praises with him at eventide and at break of day, and the birds gathered in assemblies, all turning to God. We strengthened his kingdom and gave him wisdom and sound judgment in speech and decision.

Has the story of the disputants reached you? They climbed over the wall of the private chamber. When they entered David's presence, he was terrified of them. They said, 'Fear not: we are two disputants, one of whom has wronged the other. Decide between us with truth and guide us to the even path.' One said, 'This man is my brother; he has ninety-nine ewes, and I have but one. Yet he says, "Commit her to my care," and is harsh to me in speech.' David said, 'He has undoubtedly wronged you in demanding your single ewe to be added to his flock. Many partners wrong each other, except those who believe and do good deeds, and they are few.' David realized that We had tested him, so he asked for forgiveness, fell down in prostration, and repented.

So We forgave him this lapse. He enjoyed a near approach to Us and a beautiful place of return. O David, We made you a vicegerent on earth.""O David, We have appointed you as a ruler on earth. Judge people fairly and do not follow your desires, as they will lead you away from God's path. Those who stray from God's path will face severe punishment because they forget the Day of Judgment.

We did not create the heavens, the earth, and everything in between without purpose. This is the belief of the disbelievers. Woe to those who disbelieve, for they will face the Fire of Hell.
