Should We treat those who believe and do good deeds the same as those who cause corruption on earth? Should We treat the righteous the same as the wicked? This is a blessed Book We have revealed to you so that people may reflect on its verses and those with understanding may take heed.

We gave David a son, Solomon, who was an excellent servant and always turned to Us. One evening, swift horses were brought before him, and he said, 'I love these good things for the glory of my Lord,' until they disappeared from sight. He then said, 'Bring them back to me,' and he began to stroke their legs and necks.

We tested Solomon by placing a lifeless body on his throne, and he repented. He prayed, 'My Lord, forgive me and grant me a kingdom that will not be inherited by anyone after me. You are the Bestower.' So, We made the wind subservient to him, flowing gently wherever he wished. We also subjected the evil ones, including every kind of builder and diver, and others bound together in chains.

We said, 'This is Our gift, so give freely or withhold without reckoning.' Solomon enjoyed a close relationship with Us and a beautiful place of return.

Remember Our servant Job, who cried to his Lord, 'The Evil One has afflicted me with distress and suffering!' We told him, 'Strike the ground with your foot; here is a cool bath and a refreshing drink.' We restored his family to him and doubled their number as a mercy from Us and a reminder for those with understanding.

We said to him, 'Take a handful of grass and strike with it, and do not break your oath.' We found him patient and steadfast, an excellent servant who always turned to Us.

Remember Our servants Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob, who possessed power and vision. We chose them for a special purpose: proclaiming the message of the Hereafter. They were truly among the elect and the good in Our sight.

Remember Ishmael, Elisha, and Zul-Kifl; they were all among the chosen. This is a message of admonition, and for the righteous, there is a beautiful place of return: Gardens of Eternity, whose doors will always be open to them. There, they will recline at ease, call for abundant fruit and delicious drink, and be accompanied by chaste women of equal age.

This is the promise made to you for the Day of Account. Truly, this is Our provision, which will never fail. But for the wrongdoers, there will be an evil place of return."Indeed, Hell is a terrible place for the arrogant. They will burn there, an awful bed to lie on. They will taste boiling and freezing fluids, and other similar punishments. When a group rushes in, those already there will say, "No welcome for them! They will burn in the Fire!" The newcomers will respond, "No welcome for you either! You brought this upon us. What a terrible place to stay!" They will ask God to double the punishment for those who led them astray.

They will wonder why they don't see the people they used to mock. They will question if they underestimated them or if their eyes missed them. This is the reality of the arguments among the people of the Fire.

Say, "I am only a warner. There is no god but God, the Supreme and Irresistible, the Lord of the heavens and the earth and everything in between, the Mighty and Forgiving." This is a significant message, yet you turn away from it. I had no knowledge of the highest chiefs when they disputed. It has only been revealed to me that I am to give a clear warning.

When your Lord said to the angels, "I am about to create a human from clay. When I have fashioned him and breathed into him of My spirit, fall down in prostration to him," all the angels prostrated except Iblis. He was arrogant and became a disbeliever. God asked, "What prevented you from prostrating to what I created with My hands? Are you too proud or one of the exalted?" Iblis replied, "I am better than him. You created me from fire and him from clay." God said, "Then get out from here, for you are rejected and cursed until the Day of Judgment."

Iblis asked for respite until the Day of Resurrection, and God granted it. Iblis vowed to mislead all except God's sincere servants. God declared, "The truth is, I will fill Hell with you and those who follow you."

Say, "I ask no reward for this message, nor am I a pretender. This is a reminder for all the worlds, and you will come to know its truth in time."

Chapter 39: AZ-ZUMAR (THE TROOPS, THRONGS)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

The revelation of this Book is from God, the Exalted in Power, full of Wisdom. We have revealed the Book to you in truth, so worship God with sincere devotion. Is it not to God that sincere devotion is due? But those who take protectors other than God say, "We only serve them to bring us closer to God." God will judge between them in their disputes. God does not guide those who are false and ungrateful.

If God had wished to take a son, He could have chosen anyone He pleased from His creation.If God had wanted to take a son, He could have chosen anyone from His creation. But He is above such things. He is God, the One, the Irresistible. He created the heavens and the earth with truth. He makes the night overlap the day and the day overlap the night. He has subjected the sun and the moon to His law, each running its course for an appointed time. Is He not the Exalted in Power, the One who forgives again and again?

He created you all from a single person, then created his mate of similar nature. He sent down for you eight types of cattle in pairs. He forms you in the wombs of your mothers, stage by stage, in three layers of darkness. This is God, your Lord and Cherisher. To Him belongs all dominion. There is no god but Him. How can you turn away from the truth?

If you reject God, He has no need of you, but He dislikes ingratitude from His servants. If you are grateful, He is pleased with you. No one can bear the burden of another. In the end, you will return to your Lord, and He will tell you the truth of all that you did. He knows well what is in the hearts of men.

When trouble touches a person, they cry out to their Lord, turning to Him in repentance. But when He bestows a favor upon them, they forget what they cried and prayed for before and set up rivals to God, misleading others from His path. Say, "Enjoy your blasphemy for a little while; you are one of the companions of the Fire!"

Is the one who worships devoutly during the night, prostrating and standing, who takes heed of the Hereafter and places his hope in the mercy of his Lord, equal to one who does not? Say, "Are those who know equal to those who do not know?" Only those with understanding will take heed.

Say, "O my servants who believe! Fear your Lord. Good is the reward for those who do good in this world. God's earth is spacious. Those who patiently persevere will receive a reward without measure."

Say, "I am commanded to serve God with sincere devotion and to be the first to bow to Him in Islam." Say, "If I disobey my Lord, I fear the penalty of a mighty day." Say, "It is God I serve with sincere and exclusive devotion."

Serve what you will besides Him. Say, "Those who lose their own souls and their people on the Day of Judgment are truly the losers. That is the evident loss!" They will have layers of fire above and below them. With this, God warns His servants: "O My servants, fear Me!"

Those who avoid evil and turn to God in repentance will have good news. So announce the good news to My servants who listen to the Word and follow the best meaning in it. These are the ones whom God has guided, and they are the ones endowed with understanding.

Is the one against whom the decree of punishment is justly due equal to one who avoids evil? Can you save someone who is in the Fire? But for those who fear their Lord, there are lofty mansions, one above another, with rivers flowing beneath them. This is the promise of God, and He never fails in His promise."Don't you see that God sends down rain from the sky, which then flows into the earth to form springs? With it, He produces crops of various colors. Then they wither, turn yellow, and eventually crumble away. This is a reminder for those who understand.

Is someone whose heart God has opened to Islam, receiving enlightenment from Him, the same as someone with a hardened heart? Woe to those whose hearts are hardened against remembering God; they are clearly in error.

God has revealed the most beautiful message in the form of a consistent Book, repeating its teachings in various ways. The skins of those who fear their Lord tremble at it, then their skins and hearts soften to God's praise. This is God's guidance, and He guides whom He wills. But those whom God leaves to stray, no one can guide.

Is someone who fears the punishment on the Day of Judgment, and faces it, the same as someone who is protected from it? It will be said to the wrongdoers, 'Taste what you earned!'

Those before them also rejected the revelation, and the punishment came to them from directions they did not perceive. God made them taste humiliation in this life, but the punishment of the Hereafter is even greater if they only knew.

We have presented every kind of parable in this Qur'an so that people may receive admonition. It is a Qur'an in Arabic, without any crookedness, so that they may guard against evil.

God gives an example: a man belonging to many partners who are at odds with each other, and a man belonging entirely to one master. Are the two equal? Praise be to God! But most people do not know.

You will die, and they will die. Then, on the Day of Resurrection, you will dispute before your Lord.

Who does more wrong than someone who lies about God and rejects the truth when it comes to him? Is there not a place in Hell for the blasphemers?

Those who bring the truth and those who accept it are the ones who do right. They will have all that they wish for in the presence of their Lord. This is the reward for those who do good. God will turn away the worst of their deeds and reward them according to the best of what they have done.

Is God not enough for His servant? Yet they try to frighten you with others besides Him. Whoever God leaves to stray, there is no guide for him. And whoever God guides, no one can lead astray. Is God not Mighty and capable of retribution?

If you ask them who created the heavens and the earth, they will surely say, 'God.' Say, 'Do you see then? Can those you invoke besides God remove His harm or withhold His mercy?' Say, 'God is sufficient for me. In Him, the trusting put their trust.'

Say, 'O my people! Do whatever you can; I will do my part. Soon you will know who will face a penalty of ignominy and who will be in the Fire.'""Who will face a disgraceful punishment and an everlasting doom?"

We have revealed the Book to you in truth for the guidance of humanity. Whoever follows the guidance benefits their own soul, and whoever strays harms only themselves. You are not responsible for their actions.

God takes the souls at the time of death and during sleep. He keeps those destined to die and sends the others back for a set term. These are signs for those who reflect.

Do they take intercessors besides God? Even if they have no power or understanding? Say, "To God belongs all intercession. He controls the heavens and the earth, and to Him, you will be returned."

When God alone is mentioned, those who do not believe in the Hereafter feel disgusted. But when others are mentioned, they rejoice.

Say, "O God, Creator of the heavens and the earth, Knower of the unseen and the seen, You will judge between Your servants in their disputes."

Even if the wrongdoers had all the wealth on earth and more, they would offer it as ransom from the punishment on the Day of Judgment. But they will face consequences they never expected.

The evils of their deeds will confront them, and they will be surrounded by what they used to mock.

When trouble touches a person, they cry to Us. But when We bestow a favor, they say, "I got this because of my knowledge." No, it is a test, but most do not understand.

Those before them said the same, but their deeds did not benefit them. The consequences of their actions overtook them, and the same will happen to the wrongdoers of this generation. They cannot escape.

Do they not know that God expands or restricts provision for whom He wills? These are signs for those who believe.

Say, "O my servants who have wronged themselves, do not despair of God's mercy. God forgives all sins. He is the Most Forgiving, Most Merciful."

Turn to your Lord in repentance and submit to Him before the punishment comes, and you cannot be helped.

Follow the best of what has been revealed to you from your Lord before the punishment comes suddenly, while you are unaware.

Lest a soul should say, "Woe to me for neglecting my duty to God and being among the mockers."

Or it should say, "If only God had guided me, I would have been among the righteous."

Or it should say when it sees the punishment, "If only I had another chance, I would be among the doers of good."

But the reply will be, "No, My signs came to you, but you rejected them, were arrogant, and disbelieved."

On the Day of Judgment, you will see those who lied against God with their faces turned black.Isn't Hell the home for the arrogant? On the Day of Resurrection, you will see those who lied about God with their faces darkened. Isn't Hell the place for the proud?

But God will save the righteous and bring them to a place of safety. No evil will touch them, and they will not grieve. God is the Creator and Guardian of all things.

To Him belong the keys of the heavens and the earth. Those who reject God's signs are the true losers. Say, "Do you order me to worship someone other than God, you ignorant ones?"

It has been revealed to you, as it was to those before you, that if you associate partners with God, your deeds will be in vain, and you will be among the losers. Worship God alone and be thankful.

They have not valued God as He deserves. On the Day of Judgment, the whole earth will be in His grasp, and the heavens will be rolled up in His right hand. Glory to Him, He is above what they associate with Him.

The Trumpet will be blown, and everyone in the heavens and on earth will fall unconscious, except those God wills. Then it will be blown again, and they will stand up, looking on.

The earth will shine with the light of its Lord, the Record of Deeds will be placed open, and the prophets and witnesses will be brought forward. A just decision will be pronounced, and no one will be wronged.

Every soul will be paid in full for what it has done, and God knows best what they do. The disbelievers will be led to Hell in crowds. When they arrive, its gates will be opened, and the keepers will ask, "Did messengers not come to you from among yourselves, reciting your Lord's signs and warning you of this Day?" They will say, "Yes, but the decree of punishment is justified against the disbelievers."

They will be told, "Enter the gates of Hell to dwell there. What an evil abode for the arrogant!"

But those who feared their Lord will be led to the Garden in crowds. When they arrive, its gates will be opened, and the keepers will say, "Peace be upon you! You have done well, so enter to dwell forever."

They will say, "Praise be to God, who has fulfilled His promise to us and given us this land to inherit. We can dwell in the Garden as we please. How excellent a reward for those who work righteousness!"

You will see the angels surrounding the Throne, singing Glory and Praise to their Lord. The judgment will be made in perfect justice, and the final cry will be, "Praise be to God, the Lord of the Worlds!"

Chapter 40: AL-GHAFIR (THE FORGIVER)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

Ha Mim. The revelation of this Book is from God, Exalted in Power, Full of Knowledge, who forgives sin, accepts repentance, is strict in punishment, and has a long reach in all things. There is no god but He; to Him is the final goal.

None can dispute God's signs except the unbelievers. Do not let their strutting about through the land deceive you. Before them, people denied the signs—like the people of Noah and the Confederates of Evil after them. Every people plotted against their messenger.The people of Noah and the groups after them denied their prophets. Each nation tried to capture their messenger and argued with falsehood to reject the truth. But I seized them, and how terrible was My punishment!

Thus, the decree of your Lord proved true against the unbelievers: they are indeed the companions of the Fire.

Those who carry the Throne and those around it sing praises to their Lord, believe in Him, and ask forgiveness for those who believe, saying, "Our Lord, Your mercy and knowledge encompass all things. Forgive those who repent and follow Your path, and protect them from the punishment of the Blazing Fire.

And grant, our Lord, that they enter the Gardens of Eternity, which You have promised them, along with the righteous among their ancestors, their spouses, and their descendants. You are the Exalted in Might, the Wise.

And protect them from all ills. Anyone You protect from ills on that Day will have received Your mercy, and that is the highest achievement."

The unbelievers will be addressed: "God's aversion to you is greater than your aversion to yourselves, for you were called to the faith, but you refused."

They will say, "Our Lord, You made us die twice and gave us life twice. Now we confess our sins. Is there any way out?"

The answer will be, "This is because when God alone was invoked, you disbelieved, but when partners were associated with Him, you believed. The command belongs to God, the Most High, the Most Great."

He is the One who shows you His signs and sends down sustenance for you from the sky. Only those who turn to God will take heed.

So call upon God with sincere devotion, even though the unbelievers may detest it.

He is exalted in ranks, the Lord of the Throne. By His command, He sends the Spirit to any of His servants He pleases, to warn them of the Day of Meeting.

On that Day, they will all come forth, and nothing about them will be hidden from God. Whose will be the dominion that Day? It will be God's, the One, the Irresistible.

On that Day, every soul will be recompensed for what it has earned, and no injustice will be done. God is swift in taking account.

Warn them of the Day that is drawing near, when hearts will come right up to the throats to choke them. The wrongdoers will have no friend or intercessor who will be listened to.

God knows the deceitful glances and what the hearts conceal.

God will judge with justice and truth, but those whom people invoke besides Him cannot judge at all. God alone hears and sees everything.

Do they not travel through the earth and see what was the end of those before them? They were superior in strength and left more traces in the land, but God called them to account for their sins, and they had no one to defend them against God.

That was because their messengers came to them with clear signs, but they rejected them. So God called them to account, for He is strong and severe in punishment.

We sent Moses with Our signs and an...Moses was sent with clear signs and authority to Pharaoh, Haman, and Qarun, but they dismissed him as a lying sorcerer. When Moses brought the truth from God, they plotted to kill the sons of those who believed in him and spared their women, but their plans were doomed to fail.

Pharaoh said, "Let me kill Moses and let him call upon his Lord. I fear he will change your religion or cause chaos in the land." Moses responded, "I seek refuge in my Lord and your Lord from every arrogant person who does not believe in the Day of Reckoning."

A believer from Pharaoh's people, who had kept his faith hidden, said, "Will you kill a man just because he says, 'My Lord is God,' and has brought clear signs from your Lord? If he is lying, his lie will be on him, but if he is truthful, you will face the consequences of what he warns you about. God does not guide those who are extravagant and liars."

He continued, "O my people! Today you have power in the land, but who will save us from God's punishment if it comes? Pharaoh said, 'I only show you what I see and guide you to the right path.'"

The believer warned, "O my people! I fear for you a fate like that of the previous nations, like the people of Noah, 'Ad, and Thamud, and those after them. God does not wish injustice for His servants. O my people! I fear for you a Day when there will be mutual calling and wailing, a Day when you will turn and flee with no protector from God. Whoever God leaves to stray, there is no guide for him."

He reminded them, "Joseph came to you before with clear signs, but you doubted his message. When he died, you said, 'God will not send another messenger after him.' Thus, God leaves to stray those who are extravagant and doubters, those who dispute God's signs without any authority. This is greatly hated by God and the believers. God seals the heart of every arrogant and obstinate transgressor."

Pharaoh said, "O Haman! Build me a lofty palace so I may reach the ways and means to the heavens and look upon the god of Moses, though I think he is a liar." Thus, Pharaoh's evil deeds were made appealing to him, and he was hindered from the right path. His plot ended in ruin.

The believer continued, "O my people! Follow me, and I will guide you to the right path. This worldly life is just temporary convenience; the Hereafter is the lasting home. Whoever does evil will be repaid with the like of it, but whoever does good, whether male or female, and is a believer, will enter the Garden of Bliss, where they will have abundance without measure."

He concluded, "O my people! How strange it is that I call you to salvation while you call me to the Fire. You call me to disbelieve in God and associate partners with Him, of whom I have no knowledge, while I call you to the Exalted in Power, who forgives again and again.""You call me to reject God and worship others without any knowledge, while I call you to the Mighty, the Most Forgiving. What you call me to has no basis in this world or the Hereafter, and our return will be to God. The transgressors will be companions of the Fire.

You will remember my words one day. I entrust my affairs to God, for He watches over His servants. God saved him from their evil plans, but the punishment surrounded Pharaoh's people.

They are exposed to the Fire morning and evening, and on the Day of Judgment, it will be said, 'Throw Pharaoh's people into the severest punishment.' In the Fire, they will argue, and the weak will say to the arrogant, 'We followed you; can you take some of the Fire from us?' The arrogant will reply, 'We are all in this together. God has judged between His servants.'

Those in the Fire will ask the keepers of Hell to pray to their Lord to lighten the punishment for a day. The keepers will ask, 'Did your messengers not come to you with clear signs?' They will say, 'Yes.' The keepers will reply, 'Then pray, but the prayer of disbelievers is in vain.'

We will help our messengers and those who believe in this life and on the Day when the witnesses stand forth. On that Day, excuses will not benefit the wrongdoers; they will have the curse and the home of misery.

We gave Moses the Book of Guidance, and it was inherited by the Children of Israel, a guide and a reminder for people of understanding. Be patient, for God's promise is true. Ask forgiveness for your faults and praise your Lord in the evening and morning.

Those who dispute God's signs without authority are filled with pride they will never attain. Seek refuge in God, for He hears and sees all things. The creation of the heavens and the earth is greater than the creation of mankind, but most people do not understand.

The blind and those who see are not equal, nor are those who believe and do good equal to those who do evil. The Hour is coming without doubt, yet most people do not believe. Your Lord says, 'Call on Me, and I will answer you. Those too arrogant to serve Me will enter Hell in humiliation.'

God made the night for rest and the day for seeing. He is full of grace and bounty, yet most people are ungrateful. God is your Creator; there is no god but Him. How are you turned away from the truth? Those who reject God's signs are deluded.

God made the earth a resting place and the sky a canopy. He shaped you beautifully and provided you with good things. Such is God, your Lord. Glory to God, the Lord of the Worlds!"He is the Living One. There is no god but Him. Call upon Him with sincere devotion. Praise be to God, the Lord of the Worlds!

Say: "I have been forbidden to worship those you call upon besides God, as clear signs have come to me from my Lord. I am commanded to submit to the Lord of the Worlds."

He created you from dust, then from a sperm-drop, then from a clot. He brings you forth as a child, lets you grow to full strength, and then become old, though some die before reaching this stage. This is so you may understand.

He gives life and death. When He decides upon an affair, He says to it, "Be," and it is.

Have you not seen those who dispute God's signs? How are they turned away from reality?

Those who reject the Book and the revelations sent with Our messengers will soon know the truth. When yokes are around their necks and chains drag them through boiling water and into the Fire, they will be asked, "Where are the deities you worshipped besides God?" They will say, "They have left us. We did not worship anything real." Thus, God leaves the disbelievers to stray.

This is because you exulted on earth without right and behaved insolently. Enter the gates of Hell to dwell therein. Evil is the abode of the arrogant.

So be patient, for God's promise is true. Whether We show you some part of what We promise them or take your soul before that, they will all return to Us.

We sent messengers before you. Some of their stories We have related to you, and some We have not. No messenger could bring a sign except by God's permission. When God's command comes, the matter is decided in truth and justice, and those who stood on falsehoods perish.

God made cattle for you to ride and eat. They provide other benefits, and you can fulfill your needs through them. You are carried on them and on ships.

He shows you His signs. Which of God's signs will you deny?

Do they not travel through the earth and see the end of those before them? They were more numerous and stronger, yet all they accomplished was of no profit to them.

When their messengers brought them clear signs, they exulted in their own knowledge. But the very wrath they mocked surrounded them.

When they saw Our punishment, they said, "We believe in God alone and reject what we used to associate with Him." But their faith did not benefit them when they saw Our punishment. This has always been God's way with His servants, and the disbelievers are ruined.This chapter, "Fussilat" (Explained in Detail), contains 54 verses and was revealed in Mecca. 

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. Ha Mim.
2. This is a revelation from God, the Most Gracious, the Most Merciful.
3. It is a Book with verses explained in detail, an Arabic Qur'an for people who understand.
4. It brings good news and a warning, but most people turn away and do not listen.
5. They say, "Our hearts are covered, our ears are deaf, and there is a barrier between us and you. Do what you will; we will do what we will."
6. Say, "I am just a human like you. It has been revealed to me that your God is one God. So, follow the straight path to Him and seek His forgiveness. Woe to those who associate others with God."
7. Those who do not give charity and deny the Hereafter.
8. For those who believe and do good deeds, there is an everlasting reward.
9. Say, "Do you deny the One who created the earth in two days? Do you set up equals with Him? He is the Lord of all the worlds."
10. He placed mountains on the earth, blessed it, and measured its sustenance in four days, equally for all who seek it.
11. Then He turned to the sky, which was smoke, and said to it and the earth, "Come willingly or unwillingly." They said, "We come willingly."
12. He completed them as seven heavens in two days and assigned each heaven its duty. He adorned the lowest heaven with lights and protection. This is the decree of the Mighty, the All-Knowing.
13. If they turn away, say, "I have warned you of a punishment like the one that struck 'Ad and Thamud."
14. When messengers came to them from all directions, saying, "Worship none but God," they said, "If our Lord had willed, He would have sent down angels. We disbelieve in what you have been sent with."
15. The 'Ad were arrogant and said, "Who is stronger than us?" Did they not see that God, who created them, was stronger? Yet they denied Our signs.
16. So, We sent a furious wind upon them for several days to make them taste the punishment of disgrace in this life. The punishment of the Hereafter will be even more humiliating, and they will have no help.
17. As for Thamud, We guided them, but they preferred blindness over guidance. So, the punishment of humiliation seized them for what they earned.
18. But We saved those who believed and practiced righteousness.
19. On the Day when the enemies of God are gathered to the Fire, they will be marched in ranks.
20. When they reach it, their hearing, sight, and skins will testify against them for what they used to do.
21. They will ask their skins, "Why do you testify against us?" The skins will reply, "God, who makes everything speak, has made us speak. He created you the first time, and to Him, you will return."
22. You did not hide yourselves so that your hearing, sight, and skins would not testify against you. You thought that God did not know much of what you did."You didn't hide yourselves thinking your ears, eyes, and skin wouldn't testify against you, but you assumed God didn't know much of what you did. This assumption about your Lord has led to your ruin, and now you are among the lost.

If they endure, the Fire will still be their home. If they ask for favor, they won't receive it. We assigned them companions who made their past and present seem appealing. The same fate that befell previous generations of jinn and humans now applies to them—they are utterly lost.

The disbelievers say, 'Don't listen to this Qur'an, talk over it so you might overpower it.' But We will make them taste a severe punishment and repay them for their worst deeds. This is the fate of God's enemies: the Fire, their eternal home, as a reward for rejecting Our signs.

The disbelievers will say, 'Our Lord! Show us those who misled us among jinn and humans so we can trample them underfoot and make them the lowest.' For those who say, 'Our Lord is God,' and remain steadfast, angels will descend upon them, saying, 'Don't fear or grieve, but receive the good news of the Paradise you were promised. We are your protectors in this life and the Hereafter. You will have everything your souls desire and ask for—a hospitable gift from the Forgiving, the Merciful.'

Who is better in speech than one who calls to God, does good deeds, and says, 'I am one of the Muslims'? Goodness and evil are not equal. Repel evil with what is better, and the one who was your enemy will become your close friend. But only those who are patient and fortunate will achieve this. If the devil incites you to discord, seek refuge in God. He hears and knows everything.

Among His signs are the night and day, the sun and moon. Don't prostrate to the sun or moon, but to God who created them. If they are arrogant, those with your Lord glorify Him night and day without tiring. Among His signs is the barren earth that comes to life with rain. He who gives life to the dead earth can surely give life to the dead. He has power over all things.

Those who distort Our signs are not hidden from Us. Is the one cast into the Fire better, or the one who comes safe on the Day of Judgment? Do what you will; He sees everything you do. Those who reject the Message when it comes to them are not hidden from Us. It is a powerful Book, free from falsehood, sent down by the Wise, the Praised One. Nothing is said to you that wasn't said to previous messengers."Your Lord has control over both forgiveness and severe punishment. Nothing is said to you, Muhammad, that wasn't said to the messengers before you. Your Lord is the master of forgiveness and also of dire punishment.

If We had sent this Qur'an in a language other than Arabic, they would have said, "Why aren't its verses explained in detail? A non-Arabic book and an Arab messenger?" Say, "It is a guide and a healing for those who believe. For those who don't believe, it is like deafness in their ears and blindness in their eyes. They are like people being called from a distant place."

We gave Moses the Book before, but people disputed about it. If it weren't for a decree from your Lord, their differences would have been settled. But they remain in doubt and suspicion about it.

Whoever does good, it benefits their own soul. Whoever does evil, it harms their own soul. Your Lord is never unjust to His servants.

Only God knows the Hour of Judgment. No fruit emerges from its sheath, and no female conceives or gives birth without His knowledge. On the Day He asks, "Where are My partners?" they will say, "We confess, none of us can bear witness to them."

The deities they used to invoke will abandon them, and they will realize they have no escape.

Humans never tire of asking for good things, but when evil touches them, they lose hope and despair.

When We give them a taste of mercy after adversity, they say, "This is due to my merit. I don't think the Hour will come, but if I am brought back to my Lord, I will have good things with Him." But We will show the disbelievers the truth of their deeds and make them taste severe punishment.

When We bestow favors on humans, they turn away and distance themselves. But when evil touches them, they are full of prolonged prayer.

Say, "Consider if this revelation is from God and you reject it. Who is more astray than one who is in open conflict with God?"

We will show them Our signs in the universe and within themselves until it becomes clear to them that this is the truth. Isn't it enough that your Lord is a witness over all things?

Are they still in doubt about meeting their Lord? Indeed, He encompasses all things.

Chapter 42: ASH-SHURA (COUNCIL, CONSULTATION)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

Ha-Mim. 'Ain. Sin. Qaf.

This is how God, the Mighty, the Wise, sends inspiration to you, Muhammad, as He did to those before you.

To Him belongs everything in the heavens and on earth. He is the Most High, the Most Great.

The heavens almost break apart from above them, and the angels praise their Lord and ask forgiveness for those on earth. Indeed, God is the Forgiving, the Merciful.

As for those who take protectors other than Him, God watches over them, and you are not responsible for their affairs.

We have sent you an Arabic Qur'an so you may warn the Mother of Cities and those around it, and warn them of the Day of Assembly, which is certain to come. Some will be in the Garden, and some in the Blazing Fire.If God had willed, He could have made everyone a single community, but He admits whom He wills into His mercy. Wrongdoers will have no protector or helper. 

Have they taken protectors besides Him? God alone is the Protector. He gives life to the dead and has power over all things.

Whatever you differ about, the decision rests with God. He is my Lord; in Him I trust and to Him I turn.

He is the Creator of the heavens and the earth. He made pairs from among yourselves and among cattle, multiplying you. There is nothing like Him; He hears and sees all things.

To Him belong the keys of the heavens and the earth. He enlarges and restricts sustenance to whom He wills. He knows all things.

He has established the same religion for you as He enjoined on Noah, and that which We revealed to you, and that which We enjoined on Abraham, Moses, and Jesus: to remain steadfast in religion and not to be divided. It is hard for those who worship other things than God to accept this. God chooses whom He wills and guides to Himself those who turn to Him.

They became divided only after knowledge reached them, through selfish envy. Had it not been for a decree from your Lord, the matter would have been settled between them. Those who inherited the Book after them are in doubt concerning it.

Call them to the faith and stand steadfast as you are commanded. Do not follow their vain desires. Say, "I believe in the Book God has sent down, and I am commanded to judge justly between you. God is our Lord and your Lord. We are responsible for our deeds, and you for yours. There is no contention between us and you. God will bring us together, and to Him is our final goal."

Those who dispute concerning God after He has been accepted have a futile dispute in the sight of their Lord. They will face a terrible penalty.

God has sent down the Book in truth and the Balance. Perhaps the Hour is close at hand.

Only those who do not believe in it wish to hasten it. Those who believe hold it in awe and know it is the truth. Those who dispute concerning the Hour are far astray.

God is gracious to His servants. He provides sustenance to whom He pleases. He is strong and mighty.

Whoever desires the rewards of the Hereafter, We will increase his rewards. Whoever desires the rewards of this world, We grant him some of it, but he has no share in the Hereafter.

Have they partners who have established some religion without God's permission? If it weren't for the decree of judgment, the matter would have been decided between them. Wrongdoers will have a grievous penalty.

You will see the wrongdoers in fear because of what they have earned, and the burden must fall on them. But those who believe and do righteous deeds will be in the luxuriant meadows of the Gardens. They will have all that they wish for before their Lord.You will see the wrongdoers fearful of what they have earned, and it will surely befall them, while those who believe and do good deeds will be in the lush meadows of the Gardens, having whatever they wish from their Lord. This is the great bounty from God.

This is the good news God gives to His servants who believe and do righteous deeds. Say, "I ask no reward from you except love for my close relatives." Whoever does good, We will increase their good. God is Forgiving and Appreciative.

Do they say, "He has fabricated a lie against God"? If God willed, He could seal your heart. God wipes out falsehood and confirms the truth by His words. He knows the secrets of all hearts.

He is the One who accepts repentance from His servants and forgives sins. He knows all that you do. He listens to those who believe and do righteous deeds and gives them more of His bounty. But for the disbelievers, there is a terrible penalty.

If God were to give abundant provision to His servants, they would transgress beyond bounds on the earth. But He sends it down in due measure as He pleases. He is well aware and watchful over His servants.

He is the One who sends down rain after people have lost hope and spreads His mercy. He is the Protector, Worthy of all Praise.

Among His signs is the creation of the heavens and the earth and the living creatures He has scattered through them. He has the power to gather them together whenever He wills.

Whatever misfortune happens to you is because of what your hands have done, but He forgives much. You cannot escape on earth, and besides God, you have no protector or helper.

Among His signs are the ships that sail smoothly through the ocean, tall as mountains. If He wills, He can still the wind, making them motionless on the ocean's surface. In this are signs for everyone who patiently perseveres and is grateful.

Or He can cause them to perish because of what people have earned, but He forgives much. Those who dispute about Our signs should know they have no escape.

Whatever you are given is just a convenience of this life, but what is with God is better and more lasting for those who believe and put their trust in their Lord. They avoid major sins and shameful deeds, and when they are angry, they forgive.

They respond to their Lord, establish regular prayer, conduct their affairs by mutual consultation, and spend out of what We have provided them. When an oppressive wrong is inflicted on them, they defend themselves.

The recompense for an injury is an injury equal to it, but if a person forgives and makes reconciliation, their reward is from God. God does not love wrongdoers.

There is no blame on those who defend themselves after being wronged. The blame is only on those who oppress people and transgress beyond bounds through the land, defying right and justice. For them, there will be a grievous penalty.

But if anyone shows patience and forgives, that is a sign of courageous will and resolution in the conduct of affairs.You will see the wrongdoers fearful of what they have earned, and it will surely befall them, while those who believe and do good deeds will be in the lush meadows of the Gardens, having whatever they wish from their Lord. This is the great bounty from God.

This is the good news God gives to His servants who believe and do righteous deeds. Say, "I ask no reward from you except love for my close relatives." Whoever does good, We will increase their good. God is Forgiving and Appreciative.

Do they say, "He has fabricated a lie against God"? If God willed, He could seal your heart. God wipes out falsehood and confirms the truth by His words. He knows the secrets of all hearts.

He is the One who accepts repentance from His servants and forgives sins. He knows all that you do. He listens to those who believe and do righteous deeds and gives them more of His bounty. But for the disbelievers, there is a terrible penalty.

If God were to give abundant provision to His servants, they would transgress beyond bounds on the earth. But He sends it down in due measure as He pleases. He is well aware and watchful over His servants.

He is the One who sends down rain after people have lost hope and spreads His mercy. He is the Protector, Worthy of all Praise.

Among His signs is the creation of the heavens and the earth and the living creatures He has scattered through them. He has the power to gather them together whenever He wills.

Whatever misfortune happens to you is because of what your hands have done, but He forgives much. You cannot escape on earth, and besides God, you have no protector or helper.

Among His signs are the ships that sail smoothly through the ocean, tall as mountains. If He wills, He can still the wind, making them motionless on the ocean's surface. In this are signs for everyone who patiently perseveres and is grateful.

Or He can cause them to perish because of what people have earned, but He forgives much. Those who dispute about Our signs should know they have no escape.

Whatever you are given is just a convenience of this life, but what is with God is better and more lasting for those who believe and put their trust in their Lord. They avoid major sins and shameful deeds, and when they are angry, they forgive.

They respond to their Lord, establish regular prayer, conduct their affairs by mutual consultation, and spend out of what We have provided them. When an oppressive wrong is inflicted on them, they defend themselves.

The recompense for an injury is an injury equal to it, but if a person forgives and makes reconciliation, their reward is from God. God does not love wrongdoers.

There is no blame on those who defend themselves after being wronged. The blame is only on those who oppress people and transgress beyond bounds through the land, defying right and justice. For them, there will be a grievous penalty.

But if anyone shows patience and forgives, that is a sign of courageous will and resolution in the conduct of affairs.

You will see the wrongdoers, when they face the penalty, say, "Is there any way to return?" Those whom God leads astray have no protector after Him. You will see the wrongdoers when they see the punishment, saying, "Is there any way to return?"

You will see them brought forward to the penalty, humbled by disgrace, looking with a stealthy glance. The believers will say, "Those are indeed in loss, who have given to perdition their own selves and those belonging to them on the Day of Judgment. Truly the wrongdoers are in a lasting penalty!"

They will have no protectors to help them other than God. Those whom God leaves to stray have no way to the goal.

Listen to your Lord before a Day comes from God which cannot be averted. On that Day, you will have no refuge nor any room for denial of your sins.

If they turn away, We have not sent you as a guard over them. Your duty is only to convey the message. When We give man a taste of mercy from Us, he exults in it, but when some ill happens to him because of what his hands have done, then man is ungrateful.

To God belongs the dominion of the heavens and the earth. He creates what He wills. He bestows children, male or female, according to His will.

Or He bestows both males and females, and He leaves barren whom He wills. He is full of Knowledge and Power.

It is not fitting for a man that God should speak to him except by inspiration, or from behind a veil, or by sending a messenger to reveal, with God's permission, what God wills. He is Most High, Most Wise.

And thus have We, by Our command, sent inspiration to you. You did not know what Revelation was, nor what Faith was, but We have made the Qur'an a light, guiding whom We will of Our servants. You indeed guide to the Straight Way.

The Way of God, to Whom belongs whatever is in the heavens and whatever is on earth. All affairs tend towards God."so that we can sit firmly on their backs and remember the favor of our Lord, saying: 'Glory be to Him who made this subservient to us, for we could not have done it on our own.' And surely, we must return to our Lord.

Yet, they attribute a share of His divinity to some of His servants! Truly, humans are ungrateful. Do they claim that He has taken daughters from what He creates and granted sons to you? When one of them hears news of what he likens to God, his face darkens with grief. Is one brought up among trinkets and unable to give a clear account in a dispute to be associated with God?

They make angels, who serve God, into females. Did they witness their creation? Their testimony will be recorded, and they will be questioned. They say, 'If it had been God's will, we would not have worshipped these deities.' They have no knowledge of this; they only lie.

Have We given them a book before this to which they are holding fast? No, they say, 'We found our fathers following a certain religion, and we guide ourselves by their footsteps.' Whenever We sent a warner to any people, the wealthy ones among them said, 'We found our fathers following a religion, and we will follow in their footsteps.' The warner said, 'Even if I bring you better guidance than what your fathers followed?' They replied, 'We deny that you are sent.'

So, We exacted retribution from them. See the end of those who rejected the truth! Abraham said to his father and his people, 'I disassociate myself from what you worship, except for Him who created me, for He will guide me.' He left this as a lasting word among his descendants so they might return to God.

I have given the good things of this life to these people and their fathers until the truth and a clear messenger came to them. But when the truth came, they said, 'This is sorcery, and we reject it.' They also said, 'Why wasn't this Qur'an sent down to some leading man in either of the two chief cities?' Is it they who distribute the mercy of your Lord? We distribute among them their livelihood in this world, raising some above others in rank so that some may command work from others. But the mercy of your Lord is better than the wealth they amass.

If it weren't for the risk of all people becoming one evil community, We would have provided for everyone who blasphemes against God silver roofs for their houses and silver stairways to ascend, silver doors, and silver couches to recline on, and gold adornments. But all this is just the convenience of this life; the Hereafter with your Lord is for the righteous.

If anyone turns away from the remembrance of God, We appoint a devil to be his companion. These devils hinder them from the path, but they think they are rightly guided. When such a person comes to Us, he will say to his evil companion, 'I wish there was a great distance between me and you!' What an evil companion indeed!"When the Day of Judgment comes, those who were friends will become enemies, except for the righteous. On that day, God will say to His devoted servants, "My worshippers, you have nothing to fear today, nor will you grieve. Enter Paradise, you and your spouses, rejoicing."

In Paradise, they will be served with golden dishes and cups, and there will be everything their hearts desire and their eyes delight in. They will be told, "This is the Paradise you have inherited because of your deeds."

But for the wrongdoers, it will be said, "Taste the punishment of eternity. Are you being repaid for anything except what you used to do?"

They will cry out, "Our Lord, remove us from this torment, and we will do righteous deeds, different from what we used to do." But they will be told, "Did We not give you lives long enough for anyone who would remember to remember? And the warner came to you. So taste the punishment, for the wrongdoers have no helper."

God is the Knower of the unseen of the heavens and the earth. He is the All-Knowing, the All-Wise.On the Day of Judgment, God will say to His devoted servants, "You have nothing to fear today, nor will you grieve. Enter Paradise, you and your spouses, rejoicing."

God is the Knower of the unseen of the heavens and the earth. He is the All-Knowing, the All-Wise.

On that Day, God will say to His servants, 'You have nothing to fear today, nor will you grieve. Enter Paradise, you and your spouses, rejoicing.'

In Paradise, they will be served with golden dishes and cups, and there will be everything their hearts desire and their eyes delight in. They will be told, 'This is the Paradise you have inherited because of your deeds.'

But for the wrongdoers, it will be said, 'Taste the punishment of eternity. Are you being repaid for anything except what you used to do?'

They will cry out, 'Our Lord, remove us from this torment, and we will do righteous deeds, different from what we used to do.' But they will be told, 'Did We not give you lives long enough for anyone who would remember to remember? And the warner came to you. So taste the punishment, for the wrongdoers have no helper.'

God is the Knower of the unseen of the heavens and the earth. He is the All-Knowing, the All-Wise.

On that Day, God will say to His servants, 'You have nothing to fear today, nor will you grieve. Enter Paradise, you and your spouses, rejoicing.'

In Paradise, they will be served with golden dishes and cups, and there will be everything their hearts desire and their eyes delight in. They will be told, 'This is the Paradise you have inherited because of your deeds.'

But for the wrongdoers, it will be said, 'Taste the punishment of eternity. Are you being repaid for anything except what you used to do?'

They will cry out, 'Our Lord, remove us from this torment, and we will do righteous deeds, different from what we used to do.' But they will be told, 'Did We not give you lives long enough for anyone who would remember to remember? And the warner came to you. So taste the punishment, for the wrongdoers have no helper.'

But they will be told, 'Did We not give you lives long enough for anyone who would remember to remember? And the warner came to you. So taste the punishment, for the wrongdoers have no helper.'

In Paradise, they will be served with golden dishes and cups, and there will be everything their hearts desire and their eyes delight in. They will be told, 'This is the Paradise you have inherited because of your deeds.'

But they will be told, 'Did We not give you lives long enough for anyone who would remember to remember? And the warner came to you. So taste the punishment, for the wrongdoers have no helper.'

On that Day, God will say to His servants, 'You have nothing to fear today, nor will you grieve. Enter Paradise, you and your spouses, rejoicing.'

In Paradise, they will be served with golden dishes and cups, and there will be everything their hearts desire and their eyes delight in. They will be told, 'This is the Paradise you have inherited because of your deeds.'

But for the wrongdoers, it will be said, 'Taste the punishment of eternity. Are you being repaid for anything except what you used to do?'

They will cry out, 'Our Lord, remove us from this torment, and we will do righteous deeds, different from what we used to do.' But they will be told, 'Did We not give you lives long enough for anyone who would remember to remember? And the warIn the heavens and the earth, there are signs for those who believe. In your own creation and the scattering of animals across the earth, there are signs for those with assured faith. The alternation of night and day, the sustenance God sends from the sky to revive the earth, and the changing winds are signs for those who understand.

These are the signs of God, recited to you in truth. What will they believe in if they reject God's signs? Woe to every sinful liar who hears God's revelations but remains arrogant, as if he didn't hear them. Announce to him a painful punishment. When he learns of Our signs, he mocks them. For such people, there is a humiliating penalty.

In front of them is Hell. Nothing they earned or any protectors they took besides God will benefit them. They will face a tremendous penalty. This is true guidance, and those who reject the signs of their Lord will face a grievous penalty.

God has subjected the sea to you so that ships may sail by His command, allowing you to seek His bounty and be grateful. He has made everything in the heavens and on earth subservient to you. These are signs for those who reflect.

Tell those who believe to forgive those who do not look forward to the Days of God. It is for Him to recompense each person according to what they have earned. Whoever does a righteous deed benefits his own soul, and whoever does evil, it works against his own soul. In the end, you will all be brought back to your Lord.

We granted the Children of Israel the Book, the Power of Command, and Prophethood. We gave them good and pure sustenance and favored them above the nations. We gave them clear signs in religious matters, but they fell into disputes out of envy after knowledge had been granted to them. Your Lord will judge between them on the Day of Judgment regarding their differences.

We have set you on a clear path of religion, so follow it and do not follow the desires of those who do not know. They will be of no use to you in the sight of God. Wrongdoers are protectors of each other, but God is the Protector of the righteous.

These are clear evidences and guidance for those with assured faith. Do those who seek evil ways think they will be treated the same as those who believe and do righteous deeds? Bad is their judgment! God created the heavens and the earth with truth so that every soul may be repaid for what it has earned, and none will be wronged.

Have you seen the one who takes his own vain desire as his god? God, knowing this, has left him astray, sealed his hearing and heart, and covered his sight. Who will guide him after God has withdrawn guidance? Will you not then receive admonition?

They say, "What is there but our life in this world?""They say, 'There is nothing but our life in this world; we live and die, and only time destroys us.' But they have no knowledge of this; they are merely guessing. When Our clear signs are recited to them, their only argument is, 'Bring back our forefathers if you are truthful!' Say, 'It is God who gives you life, then causes you to die, then gathers you on the Day of Judgment, about which there is no doubt.' But most people do not understand. To God belongs the dominion of the heavens and the earth, and on the Day the Hour is established, those who followed falsehood will perish. You will see every community kneeling, each community summoned to its record: 'Today you will be repaid for what you did.' This is Our record that speaks the truth about you; We were recording everything you did.

Those who believed and did righteous deeds will be admitted by their Lord into His mercy. That is the clear triumph. But to those who rejected God, it will be said, 'Were not Our signs recited to you? But you were arrogant and became sinful people.' And when it was said, 'God's promise is true, and there is no doubt about the Hour,' you said, 'We do not know what the Hour is; we think it is just a conjecture, and we are not convinced.' The evil consequences of what they did will become clear to them, and they will be surrounded by what they used to mock. It will be said, 'Today We will forget you as you forgot the meeting of this Day of yours; your abode is the Fire, and you have no helpers.' This is because you took God's signs in jest and were deceived by the life of this world. So today, they will not be brought out of it, nor will they be granted any favor.

Then praise be to God, Lord of the heavens and the earth, Lord of all the worlds. To Him belongs all glory in the heavens and the earth, and He is Exalted in Power, Full of Wisdom."They say, "This life is all there is; we live, we die, and time alone destroys us." But they have no real knowledge of this; they are just guessing. When Our clear signs are shown to them, they argue, "Bring back our ancestors if you are truthful!" Say, "It is God who gives you life, then causes you to die, and will gather you on the Day of Judgment, about which there is no doubt." But most people do not understand. God owns the heavens and the earth, and on the Day the Hour is established, those who followed falsehood will perish. You will see every community kneeling, each summoned to its record: "Today you will be repaid for what you did." This is Our record that speaks the truth about you; We were recording everything you did.

Those who believed and did good deeds will be admitted by their Lord into His mercy. That is the clear triumph. But to those who rejected God, it will be said, "Were not Our signs recited to you? But you were arrogant and sinful." And when it was said, "God's promise is true, and there is no doubt about the Hour," you said, "We do not know what the Hour is; we think it is just a guess, and we are not convinced." The evil consequences of what they did will become clear to them, and they will be surrounded by what they used to mock. It will be said, "Today We will forget you as you forgot the meeting of this Day of yours; your abode is the Fire, and you have no helpers." This is because you took God's signs in jest and were deceived by the life of this world. So today, they will not be brought out of it, nor will they be granted any favor.

Then praise be to God, Lord of the heavens and the earth, Lord of all the worlds. To Him belongs all glory in the heavens and the earth, and He is Exalted in Power, Full of Wisdom.

They say, "He has made it up." Say, "If I have made it up, you do not control anything for me from God; He knows best what you say about it; He is enough as a witness between me and you, and He is the Forgiving, the Merciful." Say, "I am not a new messenger, nor do I know what will happen to me or to you. I follow only what is revealed to me; I am just a clear warner." Say, "Have you considered if this teaching is from God and you reject it, and a witness from the Children of Israel testifies to its similarity with earlier scripture and believes, while you are arrogant? Truly, God does not guide unjust people." The disbelievers say of those who believe, "If this message were good, they would not have believed in it before us!" And since they do not guide themselves by it, they say, "This is an old lie." Before this, there was the Book of Moses as a guide and a mercy, and this Book confirms it in the Arabic tongue; to warn the unjust and give good news to those who do right.

Those who say, "Our Lord is God," and remain firm, will have no fear, nor will they grieve. They will be companions of the Gardens, dwelling there forever as a reward for their good deeds. We have enjoined on man kindness to his parents: his mother bore him with pain and gave birth to him with pain. The carrying and weaning of him is thirty months. When he reaches full strength and attains forty years, he says, "My Lord! Grant me that I may be grateful for Your favor which You have bestowed upon me and my parents, and that I may do righteous deeds that please You; and be gracious to me in my offspring. Truly, I have turned to You and truly do I bow to You in Islam." These are the ones from whom We accept the best of their deeds and overlook their ill deeds; they will be among the companions of the Garden, a promise of truth which they were given.

But there is one who says to his parents, "Fie on you! Do you hold out the promise to me that I shall be raised up, even though generations have passed before me without rising again?" And they seek God's aid, saying, "Woe to you! Believe! The promise of God is true." But he says, "This is nothing but tales of the ancients!" Such are they against whom the sentence among the previous generations of jinn and men has been proved; they will be utterly lost. And to all are assigned degrees according to their deeds, so that God may recompense their deeds, and no injustice will be done to them.

On the Day the disbelievers are placed before the Fire, it will be said to them, "You received your good things in the life of the world and took your pleasure from them; but today you will be recompensed with a penalty of humiliation because you were arrogant on earth without just cause and because you transgressed." Mention Hud, one of 'Ad's own brethren: he warned his people about the winding sand-tracts, but there have been warners before him and after him, saying, "Worship none other than God; truly, I fear for you the penalty of a mighty day." They said, "Have you come to turn us away from our gods? Then bring upon us the calamity you threaten us with if you are telling the truth." He said, "The knowledge of when it will come is only with God."He said, "Only God knows. I am just delivering the message I was sent with, but I see you are ignorant people." When they saw a cloud approaching their valleys, they thought it would bring rain. But it was the calamity they had asked for—a wind carrying a severe punishment. It destroyed everything by the command of its Lord, leaving only their ruins by morning. This is how We repay the sinful.

We had given them power and faculties of hearing, seeing, and intellect, which were of no use because they rejected God's signs. They were surrounded by what they used to mock. We destroyed the towns around you and showed them Our signs in various ways so they might turn to Us. But their false gods did not help them; they abandoned them. This was their lie and invention.

A group of jinn listened to the Qur'an and, when it was finished, they warned their people, saying, "We have heard a Book revealed after Moses, confirming what came before it. It guides to the truth and a straight path. Respond to God's caller and believe in Him. He will forgive your sins and protect you from a painful punishment. Those who do not respond cannot escape on earth and have no protectors besides God. They are in clear error."

Do they not see that God, who created the heavens and the earth and was not tired by their creation, can give life to the dead? He has power over all things. On the Day the disbelievers are placed before the Fire, they will be asked, "Is this not the truth?" They will say, "Yes, by our Lord!" Then they will be told, "Taste the punishment for your disbelief."

Be patient, as the messengers of firm resolve were patient. Do not hasten the punishment for them. On the Day they see what they are promised, it will seem as if they had only tarried for an hour of daylight. This is a clear message. Only the transgressing people will be destroyed.

Chapter 47: Muhammad

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

Those who reject God and hinder others from His path will have their deeds rendered useless. But those who believe, do good deeds, and believe in the revelation sent to Muhammad, which is the truth from their Lord, will have their sins removed and their condition improved. This is because those who reject God follow falsehood, while those who believe follow the truth from their Lord. God sets forth lessons for people through these examples.

When you meet the disbelievers in battle, strike at their necks. When you have subdued them, bind them firmly. Afterward, you can either show generosity or ransom them until the war ends. This is the command.If God had willed, He could have punished them directly, but He lets you fight to test you against each other. Those who die in God's cause will never have their deeds wasted. When you meet the disbelievers in battle, strike at their necks until you have subdued them, then bind them firmly. Afterward, you can either release them as a favor or ransom them until the war ends. This is the command. If God had willed, He could have punished them without you, but He tests you through each other. Those who are killed in God's cause will not have their actions go to waste.

Soon, He will guide them and improve their condition, and admit them to the Garden He has promised. Believers, if you support God's cause, He will support you and make your foothold firm. But those who reject God will face destruction, and their deeds will be in vain because they hate what God has revealed. Have they not traveled the earth and seen the fate of those before them who rejected God? God destroyed them, and similar fates await those who disbelieve. God is the protector of those who believe, but disbelievers have no protector.

God will admit those who believe and do good deeds to Gardens with rivers flowing beneath them. Those who reject God will enjoy this world and eat like cattle, but the Fire will be their abode. How many cities stronger than yours, which drove you out, have We destroyed? They had no helper. Is someone who follows clear guidance from their Lord like someone whose evil deeds seem pleasing to them and who follow their desires?

The Garden promised to the righteous has rivers of unpolluted water, milk with unchanging taste, delicious wine, and clear honey. They will have all kinds of fruits and grace from their Lord. Can this be compared to those who will dwell forever in the Fire and drink boiling water that tears their bowels apart?

Among them are those who listen to you, but when they leave, they ask others what you just said. These are people whose hearts God has sealed, and they follow their desires. But those who receive guidance, He increases their guidance and grants them piety. Are they waiting for the Hour to come upon them suddenly? Some signs have already come, but how will they benefit from the warning when it arrives?

Know that there is no god but God, and ask forgiveness for your sins and for the believing men and women. God knows your movements and your places of rest. Believers ask why a decisive chapter has not been revealed. But when a clear chapter is revealed and fighting is mentioned, you see those with disease in their hearts looking at you as if they are fainting from death. Obedience and a kind word would have been better for them. When the matter is resolved, if they are true to God, it will be better for them.Would you, if given authority, cause chaos in the land and break family ties? These are the people God has cursed, making them deaf and blind. Do they not reflect on the Quran, or are their hearts locked? Those who turn away after guidance has been shown to them are led astray by Satan, who fills them with false hopes. They say to those who hate what God has revealed, "We will obey you in some matters," but God knows their secrets. How will it be when the angels take their souls at death, striking their faces and backs? This is because they followed what angered God and hated what pleased Him, making their deeds worthless. Do those with disease in their hearts think God will not reveal their hatred? If God willed, He could show them to you, and you would recognize them by their speech. God knows your deeds. We will test you until we know who strives and is patient among you. Those who reject God and hinder others from His path, opposing the Messenger after guidance has been shown, will not harm God but will make their deeds fruitless. Believers, obey God and the Messenger, and do not let your deeds go to waste. Those who reject God and hinder others from His path, then die as disbelievers, will not be forgiven by God. Do not be weak and call for peace when you should be victorious. God is with you and will not let your good deeds go unrewarded. The life of this world is just play and amusement. If you believe and guard against evil, He will reward you and not ask for your possessions. If He did ask and pressed you, you would withhold, revealing your ill feelings. You are invited to spend in the way of God, but some of you are stingy. Whoever is stingy is stingy against their own soul. God is self-sufficient, and you are in need. If you turn away, He will replace you with others who will not be like you.

Chapter 48: AL-FATH (VICTORY, CONQUEST)
In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. We have granted you a clear victory,
2. So that God may forgive your past and future sins, complete His favor upon you, and guide you on the straight path,
3. And that God may help you with a powerful help.
4. It is He who sent down tranquility into the hearts of the believers to increase their faith. To God belong the forces of the heavens and the earth, and God is full of knowledge and wisdom.
5. He will admit the believing men and women to gardens beneath which rivers flow, to dwell therein forever, and remove their ills. This is the highest achievement in the sight of God.
6. He will punish the hypocrites and polytheists, men and women, who have evil thoughts about God. They will face a round of evil, the wrath of God, and His curse....prepared them for Hell, a terrible destination. God will punish the hypocritical men and women, and the idolatrous men and women, who harbor evil thoughts about Him. They will face misfortune, God's wrath, and His curse, and Hell is ready for them—a dreadful end.

To God belong the forces of the heavens and the earth, and He is all-powerful and wise. We have sent you, Muhammad, as a witness, a bringer of good news, and a warner, so that people may believe in God and His Messenger, honor Him, revere Him, and glorify Him morning and evening.

Those who pledge allegiance to you, Muhammad, are actually pledging allegiance to God. God's hand is over their hands. Whoever breaks this oath harms only themselves, but whoever keeps their covenant with God will receive a great reward.

The desert Arabs who stayed behind will say, "We were busy with our flocks and families, so ask forgiveness for us." They say with their tongues what is not in their hearts. Say, "Who can intervene on your behalf with God if He intends harm or benefit for you? God is fully aware of what you do."

You thought the Messenger and the believers would never return to their families, and this seemed pleasing to your hearts. You harbored evil thoughts and became a doomed people. If anyone does not believe in God and His Messenger, We have prepared a blazing fire for the disbelievers.

To God belongs the dominion of the heavens and the earth. He forgives whom He wills and punishes whom He wills. God is oft-forgiving, most merciful.

Those who lagged behind will say, when you march to take war booty, "Let us follow you." They wish to change God's decree. Say, "You shall not follow us; God has already declared this beforehand." They will say, "You are jealous of us." But they understand little.

Say to the desert Arabs who lagged behind, "You will be called to fight against a people of great might until they submit. If you obey, God will grant you a good reward, but if you turn back as you did before, He will punish you with a grievous penalty."

There is no blame on the blind, the lame, or the sick if they do not join the war. But whoever obeys God and His Messenger will be admitted to gardens beneath which rivers flow, and whoever turns back will be punished with a painful penalty.

God was pleased with the believers when they swore allegiance to you under the tree. He knew what was in their hearts, sent down tranquility upon them, and rewarded them with a near victory and many gains. God is mighty and wise.

God has promised you many gains that you will acquire. He has given you these beforehand and restrained the hands of men from you, so it may be a sign for the believers and guide you on the straight path. There are other gains you have not yet achieved, but God has encompassed them, and He has power over all things.If the disbelievers fight you, they will surely turn and flee, finding no protector or helper. This has always been God's way, and you will not find any change in His method. He is the one who restrained their hands from you and your hands from them in Mecca after giving you victory. God sees everything you do.

They are the ones who denied the revelation and prevented you from reaching the Sacred Mosque and the sacrificial animals from reaching their place of sacrifice. If it weren't for the believing men and women you might have harmed unknowingly, God would have allowed you to force your way. But He held back your hands to admit into His mercy whom He wills. If the believers and disbelievers had been clearly separated, We would have punished the disbelievers with a severe punishment.

When the disbelievers harbored zealotry in their hearts, God sent down His tranquility upon His Messenger and the believers, making them adhere to the command of self-restraint. They were entitled to it and worthy of it, and God knows all things.

God fulfilled the vision for His Messenger: you will enter the Sacred Mosque, if God wills, with minds secure, heads shaved, hair cut short, and without fear. He knew what you did not know and granted you a near victory.

He is the one who sent His Messenger with guidance and the true religion to make it prevail over all other religions. God is enough as a witness.

Muhammad is the Messenger of God, and those with him are strong against disbelievers but compassionate among themselves. You will see them bowing and prostrating in prayer, seeking grace from God and His pleasure. The marks of their prostration are on their faces. This is their description in the Torah and the Gospel: like a seed that sprouts, strengthens, and stands firm, delighting the sowers. This enrages the disbelievers. God has promised those who believe and do righteous deeds forgiveness and a great reward.

Chapter 49: AL-HUJRAAT (THE PRIVATE APARTMENTS, THE INNER APARTMENTS)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

O you who believe! Do not put yourselves forward before God and His Messenger, but fear God. God hears and knows all things.

O you who believe! Do not raise your voices above the voice of the Prophet, nor speak loudly to him as you do to one another, lest your deeds become void without you realizing it.

Those who lower their voices in the presence of God's Messenger are the ones whose hearts God has tested for piety. They will have forgiveness and a great reward.

Those who shout to you from outside the private apartments mostly lack understanding.

If they had patience until you came out to them, it would be better for them. God is Oft-Forgiving, Most Merciful.

O you who believe! If a wicked person comes to you with any news, verify it, lest you harm people unknowingly and later regret what you have done.Believers, if a wicked person brings you news, verify it to avoid harming others unknowingly and later regretting it. Know that God's Messenger is among you. If he followed your wishes in many matters, you would face trouble. But God has made faith dear to you and made disbelief, wickedness, and rebellion hateful to you. Such are the rightly guided, by God's grace and wisdom.

If two groups of believers fight, make peace between them. If one group wrongs the other, fight the wrongdoers until they return to God's command. Then, make peace justly, for God loves those who act fairly. Believers are brothers, so make peace between your brothers and fear God to receive His mercy.

Believers, do not mock or insult each other, as some may be better than others. Avoid suspicion, as some suspicion is sinful. Do not spy or backbite. Would you like to eat the flesh of your dead brother? No, you would hate it. Fear God, for He is Merciful.

O mankind, We created you from a male and a female and made you into nations and tribes to know one another. The most honored in God's sight is the most righteous. God knows everything.

The desert Arabs say, "We believe." Say, "You have not yet believed; say instead, 'We have submitted,' for faith has not entered your hearts. If you obey God and His Messenger, He will not diminish your deeds. God is Forgiving, Merciful."

True believers are those who believe in God and His Messenger without doubt and strive with their wealth and lives for God's cause. They are sincere. Say, "Do you teach God about your religion? God knows everything in the heavens and the earth."

They think they favor you by becoming Muslims. Say, "Do not consider your Islam a favor to me; rather, God has favored you by guiding you to faith if you are truthful." God knows the secrets of the heavens and the earth and sees all that you do.

Chapter 50: QAF (THE LETTER QAF)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

Qaf. By the Glorious Qur'an, they wonder that a warner has come from among them. The disbelievers say, "This is a strange thing! When we die and become dust, shall we live again? That is a far return!" We know how much the earth takes of them, and with Us is a record guarding it.We know what the earth takes from them, and with Us is a record that preserves everything. But they deny the truth when it comes to them, so they are in a state of confusion. Have they not looked at the sky above them, how We have made it and adorned it without any flaws? And the earth, We have spread it out, set firm mountains on it, and produced every kind of beautiful growth. This is a vision and a reminder for every servant who turns to God.

We send down blessed rain from the sky, producing gardens and grain for harvests, and tall palm trees with clustered fruit. This is sustenance for God's servants, and We give life to dead land.
