This is how the resurrection will be. Before them, the people of Noah, the companions of the Rass, and the Thamud denied the truth. So did the 'Ad, Pharaoh, and the brethren of Lot, as well as the companions of the Wood and the people of Tubba'. Each of them rejected the messengers, and My warning was fulfilled in them.

Were We tired from the first creation? Yet they doubt a new creation. We created man and know what his soul whispers to him; We are closer to him than his jugular vein. Two guardian angels record his deeds, one on the right and one on the left. Not a word does he utter without a sentinel ready to note it. The stupor of death will bring the truth before his eyes: "This is what you were trying to escape!"

The trumpet will be blown, marking the Day of Warning. Every soul will come forth with an angel to drive and an angel to bear witness. It will be said, "You were heedless of this; now We have removed your veil, and your sight is sharp today!" His companion will say, "Here is his record ready with me!" It will be commanded, "Throw into Hell every stubborn rejecter of God, who forbade good, transgressed all bounds, and cast doubts."

His companion will say, "Our Lord! I did not make him transgress, but he was far astray." God will say, "Do not dispute in My presence; I had already sent you warning. My word does not change, and I am not unjust to My servants." On that day, Hell will be asked, "Are you filled?" and it will say, "Are there any more?"

The Garden will be brought near to the righteous, no longer distant. It will be said, "This is what you were promised, for every penitent and heedful one who feared God unseen and brought a devoted heart. Enter in peace; this is the day of immortality." They will have all they desire, and more besides in Our presence.

How many generations before them did We destroy, who were stronger in power? They wandered through the land, but was there any place of escape? Indeed, in this is a message for anyone with a heart and understanding or who listens and witnesses the truth. We created the heavens and the earth and all between them in six days, and We were not tired.We created the heavens and the earth and everything in between in six days, without any fatigue. So, be patient with what they say and praise your Lord before sunrise and sunset. Also, praise Him during part of the night and after your prayers.

Listen for the Day when the Caller will call out from a nearby place. On that Day, they will hear a mighty blast, marking the Day of Resurrection. We are the ones who give life and death, and to Us is the final return. On that Day, the earth will split open, and people will rush out. This gathering is easy for Us.

We know best what they say, and you are not to force them. So, remind them with the Qur'an, those who fear My warning.

Chapter 51: ADH-DHARIYAT (THE WINNOWING WINDS)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

By the winds that scatter far and wide, and those that carry heavy loads, and those that flow with ease and gentleness, and those that distribute blessings by command. What you are promised is true, and judgment will indeed come to pass.

By the sky with its numerous paths, you are in a state of discord. Those who are averse are turned away from the truth. Woe to the liars who are heedless in confusion. They ask, "When is the Day of Judgment?" It is the day when they will be tormented by the Fire. They will be told, "Taste your torment; this is what you sought to hasten."

As for the righteous, they will be in gardens and springs, taking joy in what their Lord gives them because they lived a good life before. They used to sleep little at night and seek forgiveness at dawn. In their wealth, there was a portion for the needy and the deprived.

On the earth are signs for those with assured faith, and in yourselves. Will you not see? In the heaven is your sustenance and what you are promised. By the Lord of heaven and earth, it is the truth, just as you speak.

Has the story of Abraham's honored guests reached you? They entered his presence and said, "Peace!" He replied, "Peace!" and thought they were unusual people. He quickly went to his household and brought out a fatted calf, placing it before them. He said, "Will you not eat?" When they did not eat, he felt fear. They said, "Fear not," and gave him glad tidings of a son endowed with knowledge.

His wife came forward laughing aloud, smote her forehead, and said, "A barren old woman!" They said, "Even so has your Lord spoken; He is full of Wisdom and Knowledge." Abraham asked, "What is your errand, O Messengers?" They replied, "We have been sent to a sinful people, to bring upon them a shower of stones of clay, marked by your Lord for those who trespass beyond bounds."

Then We evacuated the believers who were there, but We found no just persons except...In one house, we found only one family that had submitted to God. We left a sign there for those who fear a severe punishment. 

In Moses, there was another sign: We sent him to Pharaoh with clear authority, but Pharaoh turned away with his chiefs, calling Moses a sorcerer or madman. So, We seized Pharaoh and his forces and threw them into the sea because they were blameworthy.

In the people of 'Ad, there was a sign when We sent a devastating wind against them. It left nothing it touched but reduced it to ruin. Similarly, in the people of Thamud, they were told to enjoy themselves for a while, but they defied their Lord's command, and a thunderbolt overtook them while they watched. They couldn't stand or help themselves.

The people of Noah before them also transgressed. We built the heavens with power and spread out the earth excellently. We created everything in pairs so that you might reflect. So, hasten to God; I am a clear warner to you from Him. Do not set up any other god with God; I am a clear warner to you from Him.

No messenger came to the people before them without being called a sorcerer or madman. They are a transgressing people. So, turn away from them; you are not to blame. But continue to remind them, for the reminder benefits the believers. 

I created jinn and humans only to worship Me. I do not require sustenance from them, nor do I need them to feed Me. God is the Provider, the Lord of Power. For the wrongdoers, their portion is like that of their predecessors. Woe to the disbelievers on the Day they are promised.

Chapter 52: AT-TUR (THE MOUNT)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

By the Mount, by a decree inscribed in a scroll unfolded, by the much-frequented House, by the elevated canopy, and by the ocean filled with swell, the doom of your Lord will indeed come to pass. No one can avert it. On the Day when the sky will be in dreadful commotion and the mountains will move, woe to those who deny the truth. They will be thrust into the Fire of Hell and told, "This is the Fire you used to deny. Is this magic, or do you not see? Enter it, whether you are patient or not; you are only being repaid for what you did."

As for the righteous, they will be in gardens and happiness, enjoying what their Lord has given them and saved from the penalty of the Fire. They will be told, "Eat and drink with profit and health because of your good deeds.""Eat and drink in good health as a reward for your deeds." They will recline on dignified thrones, and We will join them with companions with beautiful, big, and lustrous eyes. Those who believe and whose families follow them in faith will be reunited with their families, and none of their good deeds will be diminished. Each person is accountable for their actions.

We will provide them with fruits and meats of their choice. They will exchange cups of drink that are free from frivolity and sin. Young male servants, as beautiful as hidden pearls, will serve them. They will converse with each other, saying, "We used to be anxious for our families, but God has been gracious to us and saved us from the punishment of the scorching wind. We used to call upon Him before; truly, He is the Beneficent, the Merciful."

Therefore, proclaim the praises of your Lord. By the grace of your Lord, you are neither a soothsayer nor mad. Do they say, "He is a poet, and we await some calamity for him"? Say, "Wait, for I too am waiting with you." Do their minds command them to do this, or are they a transgressing people? Do they say, "He fabricated the message"? No, they do not believe. Let them produce a message like it if they are truthful.

Were they created from nothing, or are they their own creators? Did they create the heavens and the earth? No, they have no firm belief. Do they possess the treasures of your Lord, or are they in charge? Do they have a ladder to heaven to listen to its secrets? Let their listener produce clear proof. Does God have daughters while they have sons? Do you ask them for a reward, burdening them with debt? Do they possess the unseen so they can write it down? Do they plot against you? Those who defy God are themselves involved in a plot.

Do they have a god other than God? Exalted is God above what they associate with Him. If they saw a piece of the sky falling, they would say, "Clouds gathered in heaps." Leave them until they encounter their Day, wherein they will swoon with terror. On that Day, their plotting will avail them nothing, and they will receive no help. For those who do wrong, there is another punishment besides this, but most of them do not understand.

Wait patiently for your Lord's command, for you are under Our watchful eye. Celebrate the praises of your Lord while you stand, and at night, and at the retreat of the stars.

Chapter 53: AN-NAJM (THE STAR)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

By the star when it goes down, your companion is neither astray nor misled. He does not speak from his own desire. It is an inspiration sent down to him, taught by one mighty in power, endowed with wisdom. He appeared in stately form while he was in the highest part of the horizon. Then he approached and came closer.He bowed and was at a distance of two bow-lengths or even closer. God conveyed the inspiration to His servant, revealing what He intended. The Prophet's heart did not deny what he saw. Will you then argue with him about what he saw? Indeed, he saw him again at another descent, near the Lote-tree beyond which none may pass. Near it is the Garden of Abode. The Lote-tree was shrouded in mystery. His sight did not swerve nor go wrong. Truly, he saw one of the greatest signs of his Lord.

Have you considered the deities Lat, Uzza, and the third, Manat? Do you think you get the male offspring and God gets the female? This is an unfair division. These are just names you and your ancestors have invented, for which God has sent no authority. They follow nothing but conjecture and their own desires, even though guidance has come to them from their Lord. Can man have whatever he desires? No, to God belongs the beginning and the end of all things.

How many angels are in the heavens whose intercession is of no use except after God permits it for whom He wills and is pleased with? Those who do not believe in the Hereafter name the angels with female names. They have no knowledge of this; they follow only conjecture, and conjecture is no substitute for the truth. So, avoid those who turn away from Our message and desire only the life of this world. That is the extent of their knowledge. Your Lord knows best who strays from His path and who is rightly guided.

To God belongs everything in the heavens and on earth, so He may reward those who do evil according to their deeds and those who do good with what is best. Those who avoid major sins and shameful deeds, only falling into small faults, will find their Lord ample in forgiveness. He knows you well when He brings you out of the earth and when you are hidden in your mothers' wombs. Do not justify yourselves; He knows best who guards against evil.

Have you seen the one who turns back, gives a little, and then withholds? Does he have knowledge of the unseen so he can see? Has he not been informed of what is in the scriptures of Moses and Abraham, who fulfilled his engagements? That no bearer of burdens can bear the burden of another, and that man can have nothing but what he strives for. The fruit of his striving will soon be in sight, and he will be rewarded with a complete reward. To your Lord is the final goal.

It is He who grants laughter and tears, death and life, and creates in pairs, male and female, from a seed when lodged in its place. He has promised a second creation (raising of the dead). It is He who gives wealth and satisfaction and is the Lord of Sirius (the mighty star). He destroyed the powerful ancient 'Ad people and the Thamud, giving them no lease of perpetual life.The Thamud people were not spared either. Before them, the people of Noah were also unjust and rebellious. They denied our servant, calling him mad, and he was driven away. When he called upon his Lord for help, we opened the gates of heaven with pouring water and caused the earth to gush forth with springs. The waters met for a predestined purpose, and we carried Noah on an ark made of planks and nails, which sailed under our watchful eyes as a reward for him who was rejected. We left this as a sign, but is there anyone who will take heed?

How terrible was My punishment and My warning! We have indeed made the Qur'an easy to understand and remember, but is there anyone who will receive admonition? The 'Ad people also rejected the truth, and we sent a furious wind on a day of violent disaster, plucking out men as if they were roots of palm trees torn up. How terrible was My punishment and My warning!

The Thamud people also rejected their warners, saying, "What! A man, a solitary one from among ourselves! Shall we follow such a one? Truly, we would be straying in mind and mad!" They claimed the message was sent to him alone among them, calling him a liar and insolent. They will know on the morrow who is the liar and insolent one.

We sent the she-camel as a trial for them, instructing Salih to watch them and be patient. The water was to be divided between them, each one's right to drink being brought forward by suitable turns. But they called their companion, who took a sword and hamstrung her. How terrible was My punishment and My warning! We sent a single mighty blast against them, and they became like dry stubble used by one who pens cattle.The people of Lot also ignored the warnings. We sent a violent storm with showers of stones against them, sparing only Lot's household, whom we saved at dawn. This was a favor from us, as we reward those who are grateful. Lot had warned them of our punishment, but they doubted him. They even tried to harm his guests, so we blinded their eyes and said, "Taste my wrath and warning." The punishment struck them early in the morning, and they were told, "Taste my wrath and warning."

We have indeed made the Qur'an easy to understand and remember, but is there anyone who will take heed? The people of Pharaoh also received warnings, but they rejected all our signs. So, we seized them with a mighty punishment. Are your disbelievers better than those, or do you have some immunity in the scriptures? Do they think they can defend themselves? Soon their multitude will be put to flight, and they will turn and flee. The Hour of Judgment is their appointed time, and it will be most grievous and bitter. The guilty are in error and madness. On the day they are dragged into the fire on their faces, they will be told, "Taste the touch of hell."

We have created everything in proportion and measure. Our command is but a single act, like the twinkling of an eye. We have destroyed many like you before; is there anyone who will take heed? Everything they did is recorded in the scriptures. Every small and great thing is written down. The righteous will dwell among gardens and rivers, in an assembly of truth, in the presence of a Sovereign Omnipotent.

Chapter 55: AR-RAHMAN (THE BENEFICENT, THE MERCY GIVING)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

God, the Most Gracious, has taught the Qur'an. He created man and taught him speech and intelligence. The sun and the moon follow courses exactly computed. The stars and the trees prostrate in adoration. He raised the firmament high and set up the balance of justice so that you may not transgress it. Establish weight with justice and do not fall short in the balance. He spread out the earth for His creatures, with fruits, date-palms, corn, and sweet-smelling plants. Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny?

He created man from sounding clay like pottery and jinns from smokeless fire. Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? He is the Lord of the two Easts and the two Wests. He has let free the two bodies of flowing water, meeting together, with a barrier between them that they do not transgress. Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? Out of them come pearls and coral. Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? His are the ships sailing smoothly through the seas, lofty as mountains.In the sea, like banners. And His are the ships raised high in the sea like mountains. 

Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? 

Everything on earth will perish, but the face of your Lord, full of Majesty, Bounty, and Honor, will remain forever. 

Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? 

Every creature in the heavens and on earth seeks Him; every day He is in a new state of glory. 

Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? 

Soon, We will settle your affairs, O both worlds (man and jinn). 

Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? 

O assembly of jinn and men! If you can pass beyond the zones of the heavens and the earth, then pass! But you will not pass except with authority. 

Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? 

On you will be sent a flame of fire and smoke, and you will have no defense. 

Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? 

When the sky is rent asunder and becomes red like ointment. 

Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? 

On that day, neither man nor jinn will be questioned about his sin. 

Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? 

The guilty will be known by their marks and will be seized by their forelocks and their feet. 

Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? 

This is the Hell which the sinners deny. 

Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? 

In its midst and in the midst of boiling hot water, they will wander around. 

Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? 

But for those who fear the time when they will stand before their Lord, there will be two Gardens. 

Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? 

Containing all kinds of trees and delights. 

Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? 

In them will be two springs flowing freely. 

Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? 

In them will be fruits of every kind, in pairs. 

Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? 

They will recline on carpets, whose inner linings will be of rich brocade; the fruit of the gardens will be near and easy to reach. 

Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? 

In them will be maidens, chaste, restraining their glances, whom no man or jinn before them has touched. 

Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? 

Like rubies and coral. 

Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? 

Is there any reward for good other than good? 

Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? 

And besides these two, there are two other Gardens. 

Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? 

Dark-green in color from plentiful watering. 

Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? 

In them will be two springs pouring forth water in continuous abundance. 

Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? 

In them will be fruits, dates, and pomegranates. 

Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? 

In them will be fair companions, good and beautiful. 

Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? 

Companions restrained as to their glances, in goodly pavilions. 

Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny? 

Whom no man or jinn before them has touched.Neither man nor jinn has touched them before. 

Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny?

They will recline on green cushions and beautiful carpets. 

Which of the favors of your Lord will you deny?

Blessed be the name of your Lord, full of Majesty, Bounty, and Honor.

Chapter 56: AL-WAQIA (THE INEVITABLE)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

When the inevitable event happens, no one will deny its occurrence. It will bring some low and raise others high. When the earth is shaken to its core and the mountains crumble to dust, you will be divided into three groups: the companions of the right hand, the companions of the left hand, and those foremost in faith.

The companions of the right hand—how blessed they are! They will be among thornless lote-trees, clustered plantains, extended shade, flowing water, and abundant fruit. They will sit on raised thrones, created anew as pure and loving companions, equal in age.

A large number from the past and a good number from later times will be among them.

The companions of the left hand—how miserable they are! They will be in scorching wind, boiling water, and the shade of black smoke, neither cool nor refreshing. They indulged in luxury and persisted in great sin, denying resurrection after death.

They will be gathered for a well-known day. Then, you who go astray and deny the truth will eat from the tree of Zaqqum, filling your bellies and drinking boiling water like thirsty camels. This will be their entertainment on the Day of Requital.

We created you; why do you not believe? Have you considered the seed you emit? Do you create it, or are We the Creator?Is it you who create it, or are We the creators? We have decreed death as your common fate, and We cannot be thwarted. We determine death among you, and We cannot be outrun. We can change your forms and create you again in ways you do not know. You already know the first creation, so why do you not reflect and celebrate His praises?

Have you considered the seed you sow in the ground? Is it you who make it grow, or are We the cause? If We willed, We could turn it into dry powder, and you would be left in wonderment, saying, "We are indeed left with debts for nothing," or "We are deprived."

Have you considered the water you drink? Is it you who bring it down from the clouds, or do We? If We willed, We could make it salty; why then do you not give thanks?

Have you considered the fire you kindle? Is it you who grow the tree that feeds the fire, or do We? We have made it a reminder and a comfort for the dwellers in the wilderness. So, praise the name of your Lord, the Supreme.

I call to witness the setting of the stars, and that is indeed a mighty oath if you but knew. This is indeed a noble Qur'an, in a well-guarded Book, which none shall touch but those who are clean. It is a revelation from the Lord of the Worlds. Is this a message you would hold in light esteem and declare false?

Why do you not intervene when the soul of the dying man reaches the throat, while you sit looking on? We are nearer to him than you, but you do not see. If you are exempt from future account, call back the soul if you are true in your claim of independence.

If he is one of those nearest to God, there is for him rest and satisfaction, and a Garden of Delights. If he is one of the companions of the right hand, he will be greeted with "Peace be unto thee" from the companions of the right hand. But if he is one of those who treat the truth as falsehood and go wrong, his entertainment will be boiling water and burning in Hell-Fire. This is the certain truth. So, praise the name of your Lord, the Supreme.

Chapter 57: AL-HADID (THE IRON)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

Whatever is in the heavens and on earth declares the praises and glory of God, for He is the Exalted in Might, the Wise. To Him belongs the dominion of the heavens and the earth. He gives life and death, and He has power over all things. He is the First and the Last, the Evident and the Immanent, and He has full knowledge of all things.

He created the heavens and the earth in six days and is firmly established on the Throne of Authority. He knows what enters the earth and what comes forth from it, what comes down from heaven and what ascends to it. He is with you wherever you are, and God sees well all that you do.

To Him belongs the dominion of the heavens and the earth, and all affairs are referred back to God. He merges night into day and day into night, and He has full knowledge of the secrets of all hearts.

Believe in God and His messenger, and spend in charity out of what He has made you heirs. For those who believe and spend in charity, there is a great reward.Why don't you believe in God when the Messenger invites you to believe in your Lord? He has already made a covenant with you if you are true believers. God sends clear signs to His servant to lead you from darkness into light. He is kind and merciful to you.

Why don't you spend in the cause of God? Everything in the heavens and the earth belongs to Him. Those who spent and fought before the victory are higher in rank than those who did so later, but God has promised good to all. He knows everything you do.

Who will lend to God a good loan? He will multiply it for you and give you a generous reward. On the Day of Judgment, you will see believing men and women with their light shining before them. They will be told, "Good news for you today! Gardens beneath which rivers flow, where you will live forever. This is the highest achievement."

On that day, hypocrites will ask believers to share their light, but they will be told to go back and seek their own light. A wall with a gate will separate them, with mercy inside and punishment outside. The hypocrites will call out, "Weren't we with you?" The believers will reply, "Yes, but you led yourselves into temptation, doubted, and were deceived by false desires until God's command came."

No ransom will be accepted from you or those who rejected God. Your home is the Fire, and it is an evil refuge. Isn't it time for believers to humble their hearts in remembrance of God and the truth revealed to them? Don't be like those who received the scripture before but let their hearts harden over time.

Know that God gives life to the earth after its death. We have made the signs clear to you so you may understand. Those who give in charity and lend to God a good loan will have it doubled and receive a noble reward. Believers in God and His messengers are the truthful and faithful ones. They will have their reward and light, while those who disbelieve will be in Hell.

Understand that the life of this world is just play, amusement, and rivalry in wealth and children. It's like rain that makes vegetation grow, which then withers and turns yellow. In the Hereafter, there is severe punishment for wrongdoers and forgiveness and pleasure from God for the righteous. The life of this world is just an illusion.Rain makes plants grow, which pleases farmers, but then the plants wither, turn yellow, and dry up. In the Hereafter, there is severe punishment and also forgiveness and pleasure from God. This world's life is just a deception.

Strive for forgiveness from your Lord and a Garden as vast as the heavens and the earth, prepared for those who believe in God and His messengers. This is God's grace, which He gives to whom He pleases. God is the Lord of abundant grace.

No misfortune happens on earth or in yourselves without it being recorded in a decree before We bring it into existence. This is easy for God. This is so you don't despair over what you miss or boast about what you receive. God does not love the arrogant and boastful.

Those who are stingy and encourage others to be stingy should know that God is free of all needs and worthy of all praise. We sent our messengers with clear signs and sent down the Book and the Balance so that people may act justly. We also sent down iron, which has great power and benefits for humanity, so that God may test who will help Him and His messengers, even though unseen. God is Strong and Mighty.

We sent Noah and Abraham and established prophethood and revelation in their lineage. Some of them were rightly guided, but many were rebellious. After them, We sent other messengers, including Jesus, son of Mary, and gave him the Gospel. We placed compassion and mercy in the hearts of those who followed him. However, monasticism was their own invention; We did not prescribe it for them. They sought God's pleasure but did not observe it properly. We gave those who believed their reward, but many were rebellious.

Believers, fear God and believe in His Messenger. He will give you a double portion of His mercy, provide you with a light to walk by, and forgive you. God is Forgiving and Merciful. This is so that the People of the Book may know they have no control over God's grace, which is entirely in His hand to bestow on whom He wills. God is the Lord of abundant grace.

Chapter 58: AL-MUJADILA (THE PLEADING WOMAN)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

God has heard the statement of the woman who pleads with you about her husband and complains to God. God hears your arguments. God is Hearing and Seeing.

If any men among you divorce their wives by calling them mothers, they are not their mothers. Their mothers are only those who gave them birth. They utter an iniquitous and false word. But God is one who blots out sins and forgives repeatedly.

Those who divorce their wives by calling them mothers and then wish to go back on their words must free a slave before they touch each other. This is what you are admonished to do. God is well aware of what you do.

If they cannot afford it, they should fast for two consecutive months before they touch each other. If they are unable to do so, they should feed sixty needy people. This is to show your faith in God and His Messenger. These are the limits set by God. For those who reject Him, there is a grievous penalty.If someone can't afford to free a slave, they should fast for two consecutive months before they can be intimate again. If they can't do that either, they should feed sixty needy people. This is to show your faith in God and His Messenger. These are God's rules, and those who reject them will face severe punishment.

Those who oppose God and His Messenger will be humbled, just like those before them. We have sent clear signs, and disbelievers will face a humiliating penalty.

On the Day of Judgment, God will raise everyone and show them the truth of their actions. God has kept a record, even if they have forgotten. God is a witness to everything.

Don't you see that God knows everything in the heavens and on earth? There is no secret conversation among three people without God being the fourth, nor among five without Him being the sixth. He is with them wherever they are, and on the Day of Resurrection, He will inform them of what they did. God knows all things.

Have you noticed those who were forbidden secret meetings but still return to them, conspiring for sin and disobedience to the Messenger? When they come to you, they greet you in a way God does not approve of and say to themselves, "Why doesn't God punish us for what we say?" Hell is enough for them; they will burn in it, and it's a terrible destination.

Believers, when you hold secret meetings, don't do it for sin and hostility and disobedience to the Prophet. Instead, do it for righteousness and self-restraint, and fear God, to whom you will be brought back.

Secret meetings are only inspired by the devil to cause grief to the believers, but he can't harm them without God's permission. Believers should put their trust in God.

Believers, when you are told to make room in assemblies, make room; God will make room for you. When you are told to rise, rise; God will raise those who believe and have knowledge to high ranks. God is aware of what you do.

Believers, when you consult the Messenger in private, spend something in charity before your consultation. This is better and purer for you. But if you can't afford it, God is Forgiving and Merciful.

Are you afraid of spending in charity before your private consultation? If you don't do it and God forgives you, then at least establish regular prayer, practice regular charity, and obey God and His Messenger. God is aware of what you do.

Have you seen those who befriend people with whom God is angry? They are neither of you nor of them, and they swear falsely while knowing it.

God has prepared a severe punishment for them. Their deeds are evil.

They use their oaths as a cover for their misdeeds and obstruct people from the path of God. They will face a humiliating penalty.

Their wealth and children will not benefit them against God. They are the companions of the Fire, where they will dwell forever.

One day, God will raise them all for judgment. They will swear to Him as they swear to you, thinking they have something to stand on. No, indeed!On the Day of Judgment, God will gather everyone, and they will swear to Him just as they swear to you now, thinking they have some standing. But they are indeed the liars. The devil has taken control of them, making them forget to remember God. They are part of the devil's group, and it is the devil's group that will lose.

Those who oppose God and His Messenger will be among the most humiliated. God has decreed that He and His messengers will prevail, for God is strong and mighty. You will not find people who believe in God and the Last Day befriending those who oppose God and His Messenger, even if they are their fathers, sons, brothers, or relatives. God has written faith in their hearts and strengthened them with a spirit from Himself. He will admit them to gardens beneath which rivers flow, where they will live forever. God is pleased with them, and they are pleased with Him. They are the party of God, and it is the party of God that will succeed.

Chapter 59: AL-HASHR (EXILE, BANISHMENT)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

Whatever is in the heavens and on earth declares the praises and glory of God, for He is the Exalted in Might, the Wise. It is He who expelled the disbelievers among the People of the Book from their homes at the first gathering. You did not think they would leave, and they thought their fortresses would protect them from God. But God's wrath came upon them from where they did not expect, and He cast terror into their hearts, so they destroyed their homes with their own hands and the hands of the believers. Take warning, O you who have eyes to see!

If God had not decreed their exile, He would have punished them in this world, and in the Hereafter, they will have the punishment of the Fire. This is because they opposed God and His Messenger, and whoever opposes God will face severe punishment. Whether you cut down the tender palm trees or leave them standing, it was by God's permission, so that He might disgrace the rebellious transgressors.

What God has bestowed on His Messenger from them, you did not press forward against it with any horse or riding camel, but God gives authority to His messengers over whom He pleases. God has power over all things. What God has given to His Messenger from the people of the towns belongs to God, His Messenger, and to kindred, orphans, the needy, and the wayfarer, so that it does not circulate only among the wealthy. So take what the Messenger assigns to you and abstain from what he forbids you. Fear God, for God is strict in punishment.

Some part is due to the indigent Muhajirs, those who were expelled from their homes and their property while seeking grace from God and His good pleasure, and aiding God and His Messenger. They are indeed the sincere ones. Those who had homes in Medina and had adopted the faith before them show their affection to those who came to them for refuge. They entertain no desire in their hearts for things given to the latter but give them preference over themselves, even though they are in poverty. Those who are saved from the covetousness of their own souls are the ones who achieve prosperity.Those who came into the faith later say, "Our Lord, forgive us and our brothers who preceded us in faith. Do not let any resentment remain in our hearts towards those who believe. Our Lord, You are indeed Kind and Merciful."

Have you not seen the hypocrites say to their disbelieving brethren among the People of the Book, "If you are expelled, we will go out with you and never listen to anyone against you. If you are attacked, we will help you." But God bears witness that they are liars. If they are expelled, they will not go out with them, and if they are attacked, they will not help them. Even if they did help, they would turn and flee, receiving no help.

You are more feared in their hearts than God because they are people who do not understand. They will not fight you together except in fortified towns or from behind walls. Their internal fighting is severe; you may think they are united, but their hearts are divided because they lack wisdom.

They are like those who recently tasted the evil consequences of their actions and will face a painful punishment in the Hereafter. Their allies deceived them, like the devil who says to man, "Deny God." But when man denies, the devil says, "I am free of you; I fear God, the Lord of the Worlds." The end for both will be the Fire, where they will dwell forever. Such is the reward for wrongdoers.

O believers, fear God and let every soul consider what it has prepared for tomorrow. Fear God, for He is well-acquainted with all that you do. Do not be like those who forgot God, causing them to forget their own souls. They are the rebellious transgressors. The companions of the Fire and the companions of the Garden are not equal. The companions of the Garden are the successful ones.

If We had sent down this Qur'an on a mountain, you would have seen it humble itself and split asunder for fear of God. These are the parables We set forth for people so they may reflect. God is He, besides whom there is no other god. He knows all things, both secret and open. He is the Most Gracious, Most Merciful. He is God, the Sovereign, the Holy One, the Source of Peace, the Guardian of Faith, the Preserver of Safety, the Exalted in Might, the Irresistible, the Supreme. Glory to God, above the partners they attribute to Him.

He is God, the Creator, the Evolver, the Bestower of Forms. To Him belong the most beautiful names. Whatever is in the heavens and on earth declares His praises and glory. He is the Exalted in Might, the Wise.

Chapter 60: AL-MUMTAHINA (SHE THAT IS TO BE EXAMINED)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

O believers, do not take My enemies and yours as friends, offering them love even though they have rejected the truth that has come to you and have driven out the Prophet and yourselves from your homes simply because you believe in God, your Lord. If you have come out to strive in My way and seek My good pleasure, do not take them as friends, holding secret conversations of love with them. I know all that you conceal and reveal. Any of you who does this has strayed from the Straight Path.O believers, do not take My enemies and yours as friends, offering them love even though they have rejected the truth that has come to you and have driven out the Prophet and yourselves from your homes simply because you believe in God, your Lord. If you have come out to strive in My way and seek My good pleasure, do not take them as friends, holding secret conversations of love with them. I know all that you conceal and reveal. Any of you who does this has strayed from the Straight Path.

If they gain the upper hand over you, they will act as enemies and harm you with their hands and tongues, wishing you to disbelieve. Your relatives and children will not benefit you on the Day of Judgment. God will judge between you, and He sees everything you do.

You have a good example in Abraham and those with him when they said to their people, "We are clear of you and what you worship besides God. We reject you, and enmity and hatred have arisen between us and you forever until you believe in God alone." But Abraham said to his father, "I will pray for your forgiveness, though I have no power to get anything on your behalf from God." They prayed, "Our Lord, in You we trust, and to You we turn in repentance. To You is our final goal."

Our Lord, do not make us a trial for the disbelievers, and forgive us. You are the Mighty, the Wise. There is a good example for you in them for those who hope in God and the Last Day. But if anyone turns away, God is Free of all needs, Worthy of all praise.

It may be that God will create love between you and those you now hold as enemies. God is Powerful, and He is Forgiving, Merciful. God does not forbid you from being kind and just to those who do not fight you for your faith or drive you out of your homes. God loves those who are just.

God only forbids you from making friends with those who fight you for your faith, drive you out of your homes, and support others in driving you out. Whoever makes friends with them is a wrongdoer.

O believers, when believing women come to you as refugees, test them. God knows best their faith. If you find them to be believers, do not send them back to the disbelievers. They are not lawful for the disbelievers, nor are the disbelievers lawful for them. Give the disbelievers what they have spent on them. There is no blame on you if you marry them after giving them their dowries. Do not hold on to the guardianship of disbelieving women. Ask for what you have spent, and let the disbelievers ask for what they have spent. This is God's judgment. He judges between you, and God is Knowing, Wise.

If any of your wives desert you to the disbelievers, and you gain something in return, then pay those whose wives have deserted the equivalent of what they had spent. Fear God, in whom you believe.

O Prophet, when believing women come to you to take the oath of allegiance, that they will not associate anything with God, that they will not steal, commit adultery, kill their children, utter slander, or disobey you in any just matter, then accept their allegiance and pray to God for their forgiveness. God is Forgiving, Merciful."O believers, when women who believe come to you seeking refuge, test their faith. God knows best their belief. If you find them to be true believers, do not send them back to the disbelievers. They are not lawful for the disbelievers, nor are the disbelievers lawful for them. Return to the disbelievers what they have spent on them. There is no blame on you if you marry them after giving them their dowries. Do not hold onto the guardianship of disbelieving women. Ask for what you have spent, and let the disbelievers ask for what they have spent. This is God's judgment. He judges between you, and God is Knowing, Wise.

If any of your wives desert you to the disbelievers, and you gain something in return, then pay those whose wives have deserted the equivalent of what they had spent. Fear God, in whom you believe.

O Prophet, when believing women come to you to take the oath of allegiance, that they will not associate anything with God, that they will not steal, commit adultery, kill their children, utter slander, or disobey you in any just matter, then accept their allegiance and pray to God for their forgiveness. God is Forgiving, Merciful.

O believers, do not befriend people with whom God is angry. They have despaired of the Hereafter just as the disbelievers have despaired of those buried in graves.

Chapter 61: AS-SAFF (THE RANKS, BATTLE ARRAY)
In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

Whatever is in the heavens and on earth declares the glory of God. He is the Mighty, the Wise.

O believers, why do you say what you do not do? It is most hateful in the sight of God that you say what you do not do. Truly, God loves those who fight in His cause in ranks, as if they were a solid structure.

Remember when Moses said to his people, "O my people! Why do you vex and insult me, though you know that I am the messenger of God sent to you?" When they went wrong, God let their hearts go wrong. God does not guide those who are rebellious transgressors.

And remember, Jesus, the son of Mary, said, "O Children of Israel! I am the messenger of God sent to you, confirming the Law which came before me, and giving glad tidings of a Messenger to come after me, whose name shall be Ahmad." But when he came to them with clear signs, they said, "This is evident sorcery!"

Who does greater wrong than one who invents falsehood against God, even as he is being invited to Islam? God does not guide those who do wrong.

Their intention is to extinguish God's Light with their mouths, but God will complete His Light, even though the disbelievers may detest it. He is the One who has sent His Messenger with guidance and the religion of truth, to proclaim it over all religion, even though the pagans may detest it.

O believers, shall I lead you to a bargain that will save you from a grievous penalty? Believe in God and His Messenger, and strive in the cause of God with your property and your persons. That will be best for you if you but knew! He will forgive your sins and admit you to gardens beneath which rivers flow, and to beautiful mansions in gardens of eternity. That is indeed the supreme achievement. And another favor which you love: help from God and a speedy victory. So give the glad tidings to the believers.

O believers, be helpers of God, as Jesus the son of Mary said to the disciples, "Who will be my helpers in the cause of God?" The disciples said, "We are God's helpers!" Then a portion of the Children of Israel believed, and a portion disbelieved. But We gave power to those who believed against their enemies, and they became the ones who prevailed.

Chapter 62: AL-JUMUA (THE CONGREGATION, FRIDAY)
In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

Whatever is in the heavens and on earth declares the glory of God, the Sovereign, the Holy One, the Exalted in Might, the Wise. He is the One who has sent among the unlettered a messenger from among themselves, to recite to them His signs, to sanctify them, and to instruct them in Scripture and Wisdom, although they had been, before, in manifest error. Along with others of them who have not yet joined them. He is the Mighty, the Wise."He is the Mighty, the Wise. This is the bounty of God, which He bestows on whom He wills. God is the Lord of infinite bounty.

The example of those who were given the Mosaic Law but failed to uphold it is like a donkey carrying books—it doesn't understand their value. Evil is the example of people who deny God's signs, and God does not guide wrongdoers.

Say, "O Jews, if you claim to be God's chosen people to the exclusion of others, then wish for death if you are truthful." But they will never wish for it because of what their hands have done. God knows well those who do wrong.

Say, "The death you flee from will surely overtake you. Then you will be returned to the Knower of the unseen and the seen, and He will inform you of what you used to do."

O believers, when the call to prayer is made on Friday, hasten to the remembrance of God and leave off business. That is better for you if you only knew. When the prayer is finished, disperse in the land and seek God's bounty, and remember God often so that you may prosper.

But when they see some bargain or amusement, they rush to it and leave you standing. Say, "What is with God is better than amusement and merchandise, and God is the best provider."

Chapter 63: The Hypocrites

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

When the hypocrites come to you, they say, "We bear witness that you are indeed the Messenger of God." God knows that you are His Messenger, and God bears witness that the hypocrites are liars.

They use their oaths as a cover and turn people away from the path of God. Truly evil are their deeds. This is because they believed and then disbelieved, so their hearts were sealed, and they do not understand.

When you see them, their appearance pleases you, and when they speak, you listen to their words. They are like hollow pieces of timber propped up. They think every shout is against them. They are the enemy, so beware of them. May God curse them! How are they deluded away from the truth!

When it is said to them, "Come, the Messenger of God will pray for your forgiveness," they turn their heads aside, and you see them turning away in arrogance. It is the same whether you ask forgiveness for them or not; God will not forgive them. God does not guide rebellious transgressors.

They are the ones who say, "Do not spend on those who are with God's Messenger until they disperse." But to God belong the treasures of the heavens and the earth, yet the hypocrites do not understand. They say, "If we return to Medina, the more honorable will expel the meaner." But honor belongs to God, His Messenger, and the believers, though the hypocrites do not know.

O believers, do not let your wealth or your children distract you from the remembrance of God. Those who do so are the losers. Spend in charity from what We have provided you before death comes to any of you, and he says, "My Lord, why did You not give me respite for a little while? I would have given in charity and been among the righteous.""Spend from what We have provided you before death comes to one of you, and he says, 'My Lord, if only You would delay me for a little while, I would give in charity and be among the righteous.' But God will not delay a soul when its time has come, and God is fully aware of what you do.

Chapter 64: Mutual Disillusion (At-Taghabun)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

Everything in the heavens and on earth glorifies God. To Him belongs all dominion and praise, and He has power over all things. He created you, and among you are those who believe and those who do not. God sees everything you do. He created the heavens and the earth with truth and shaped you beautifully. To Him is your final return. He knows what is in the heavens and on earth, and He knows what you conceal and what you reveal. God knows the secrets of all hearts.

Have you not heard the story of those who rejected faith before? They tasted the consequences of their actions and faced a grievous penalty. This happened because messengers came to them with clear signs, but they said, 'Shall mere humans guide us?' So they disbelieved and turned away. God is independent of them and worthy of all praise.

Those who disbelieve think they will not be raised up for judgment. Say, 'Yes, by my Lord, you will surely be raised up and informed of what you did. That is easy for God.' So believe in God and His Messenger and the light We have revealed. God is fully aware of what you do.

On the Day He gathers you for the Day of Assembly, it will be a day of mutual loss and gain. Those who believe in God and do righteous deeds will have their sins removed and will be admitted to gardens beneath which rivers flow, to dwell there forever. That is the supreme achievement. But those who reject faith and deny Our signs will be companions of the Fire, to dwell there forever. What an evil destination!

No calamity occurs except by God's permission. Whoever believes in God, He guides their heart. God knows all things. So obey God and His Messenger. If you turn away, the duty of Our Messenger is only to convey the message clearly. God, there is no god but He. Let the believers put their trust in God.

O believers, among your spouses and children are enemies to you, so beware of them. But if you forgive, overlook, and pardon, then God is Forgiving, Merciful. Your wealth and children are only a test, but with God is a great reward. So be mindful of God as much as you can, listen, obey, and spend in charity. Whoever is saved from their own greed will be successful. If you lend to God a goodly loan, He will double it for you and forgive you. God is most appreciative and forbearing, knowing the unseen and the seen, the Mighty, the Wise.

Chapter 65: Divorce (At-Talaq)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

O Prophet, when you divorce women, divorce them at the appropriate time..."When you divorce women, do so at the appropriate time and accurately count their waiting period. Fear God, your Lord, and do not force them out of their homes, nor should they leave unless they commit clear immorality. These are the limits set by God, and whoever transgresses them wrongs their own soul. You do not know if God might bring about a new situation afterward.

When they have fulfilled their waiting period, either take them back on fair terms or part with them on fair terms. Call two just witnesses from among you and establish the testimony before God. This is the advice for those who believe in God and the Last Day. Whoever fears God, He will make a way out for them and provide for them from sources they could never imagine. Whoever trusts in God, He is sufficient for them. God will accomplish His purpose, for He has set a measure for all things.

For women who have passed the age of menstruation, their waiting period is three months if you have any doubts. The same applies to those who have not menstruated. For pregnant women, their waiting period is until they deliver their burden. Whoever fears God, He will make their path easy.

This is the command of God, which He has sent down to you. Whoever fears God, He will remove their ills and enlarge their reward. Let the women live in the same style as you live, according to your means. Do not annoy them to restrict them. If they are pregnant, spend on them until they deliver. If they suckle your child, give them their due payment and consult together in kindness. If you face difficulties, let another woman suckle the child.

Let the man of means spend according to his means, and the one with limited resources spend according to what God has given him. God does not burden any soul beyond what He has given it. After difficulty, God will soon grant relief.

Many communities that opposed the command of their Lord and His messengers were called to account and faced severe punishment. They tasted the evil result of their conduct, and their end was perdition. God has prepared a severe punishment for them. Therefore, fear God, O people of understanding who believe! God has indeed sent down a reminder to you.

A Messenger recites to you the clear signs of God to lead those who believe and do righteous deeds from darkness into light. Those who believe in God and do good deeds will be admitted to gardens beneath which rivers flow, to dwell there forever. God has indeed granted them excellent provision.

God is the One who created seven heavens and a similar number of earths. His command descends among them so that you may know that God has power over all things and that He comprehends all things in His knowledge."O Prophet! Why do you forbid yourself from what God has made lawful for you, seeking to please your wives? God is Forgiving and Merciful. God has already allowed you to dissolve certain oaths. He is your Protector, full of Knowledge and Wisdom.

When the Prophet confided a matter to one of his wives, and she disclosed it, God informed him. He confirmed part of it and ignored part. When he told her about it, she asked, 'Who told you this?' He replied, 'The Knower, the Aware informed me.'

If you two turn in repentance to God, your hearts are inclined to it. But if you support each other against him, then God is his Protector, and so are Gabriel, the righteous believers, and the angels.

If he divorces you, God may give him better wives who are submissive, believing, devout, penitent, worshipful, fasting, previously married, or virgins.

Believers, protect yourselves and your families from a Fire fueled by people and stones, overseen by stern and severe angels who do not disobey God's commands.

On that Day, it will be said to the disbelievers, 'Make no excuses today; you are being repaid for what you did.'

Believers, turn to God with sincere repentance. Your Lord may remove your ills and admit you to Gardens with rivers flowing beneath. On that Day, God will not disgrace the Prophet and those who believe with him. Their light will shine before them, and they will say, 'Our Lord, perfect our light for us and forgive us. You have power over all things.'

O Prophet, strive hard against the disbelievers and hypocrites and be firm with them. Their abode is Hell, a terrible destination.

God gives the example of the wives of Noah and Lot. They were under two righteous servants but betrayed them, and it was said to them, 'Enter the Fire with those who enter.'

God also gives the example of Pharaoh's wife, who prayed, 'My Lord, build for me a home with You in the Garden and save me from Pharaoh and his deeds and from the wrongdoers.'

And Mary, the daughter of 'Imran, who guarded her chastity, and We breathed into her of Our spirit. She believed in the words of her Lord and His Revelations and was one of the devout.

Blessed is He in Whose hands is Dominion, and He has power over all things. He created death and life to test which of you is best in deed. He is the Exalted in Might, the Forgiving.

He created the seven heavens in harmony. You will see no flaw in the creation of the Most Gracious. Look again, do you see any rifts? Look again and again; your vision will return to you dull and exhausted."Look again and again; your vision will return to you confused and fatigued. 

We have adorned the lowest heaven with lamps and made them missiles to drive away the evil ones, preparing for them the penalty of the blazing fire. For those who reject their Lord, the penalty of Hell awaits, a terrible destination. When they are cast into it, they will hear its terrible roaring as it blazes forth, almost bursting with fury. Every time a group is cast in, its keepers will ask, "Did no warner come to you?" They will say, "Yes, a warner did come to us, but we rejected him and said, 'God never sent down any message; you are in great error.'"

They will further say, "Had we but listened or used our intelligence, we would not be among the companions of the blazing fire!" They will then confess their sins, but forgiveness will be far from them. As for those who fear their Lord unseen, for them is forgiveness and a great reward. Whether you hide your word or publish it, He certainly knows the secrets of all hearts. Should He not know what He created? He understands the finest mysteries and is well-acquainted with them.

It is He who made the earth manageable for you, so traverse its paths and enjoy the sustenance He provides. But to Him is the resurrection. Do you feel secure that He who is in heaven will not cause the earth to swallow you when it shakes? Or do you feel secure that He will not send a violent tornado against you? Indeed, men before them rejected My warning, and how terrible was My rejection of them!

Do they not observe the birds above them, spreading and folding their wings? None can uphold them except God, Most Gracious. Truly, He watches over all things. Who can help you besides God, Most Merciful? The unbelievers are in nothing but delusion. Who can provide you with sustenance if He withholds His provision? Yet they persist in insolent impiety and flight from the truth.

Is one who walks headlong, with his face groveling, better guided, or one who walks evenly on a straight path? Say, "It is He who created you and made for you the faculties of hearing, seeing, feeling, and understanding. Little thanks you give." Say, "It is He who multiplied you through the earth, and to Him you shall be gathered together." They ask, "When will this promise be fulfilled if you are telling the truth?" Say, "The knowledge of the time is with God alone; I am only a plain warner."

When they see it close at hand, the faces of the unbelievers will be grieved, and it will be said to them, "This is the promise you were calling for!" Say, "See if God were to destroy me and those with me, or if He bestows His mercy on us, who can deliver the unbelievers from a grievous penalty?" Say, "He is God, Most Gracious. We have believed in Him, and on Him, we have put our trust. Soon you will know who is in manifest error." Say, "See if your stream is lost in the underground earth, who then can supply you with clear-flowing water?""If your water were to disappear, who could bring you fresh, flowing water?" - Chapter 68: AL-QALAM (THE PEN) Total Verses: 52 Revealed At: MAKKA

1. Nun. By the Pen and what they write,
2. You are not, by the grace of your Lord, mad or possessed.
3. Indeed, you will have an unfailing reward.
4. And you are of great moral character.
5. Soon you will see, and they will see,
6. Which of you is afflicted with madness.
7. Your Lord knows best who has strayed from His path and who is rightly guided.
8. So do not listen to those who deny the truth.
9. They wish you would compromise so they would compromise.
10. Do not obey any despicable person, ready with oaths,
11. A slanderer, spreading calumnies,
12. Habitually hindering good, transgressing beyond bounds, deep in sin,
13. Violent and cruel, with all that, base-born,
14. Because he possesses wealth and numerous sons.
15. When Our signs are recited to him, he says, "Tales of the ancients!"
16. Soon We will brand him on the snout!
17. We have tested them as We tested the People of the Garden, when they resolved to gather the fruits in the morning,
18. But made no reservation, "If it be God's Will."
19. Then a visitation from your Lord came upon it while they slept,
20. And by morning it was like a dark and desolate spot.
21. As the morning broke, they called out to one another,
22. "Go to your tilth in the morning if you would gather the fruits."
23. So they departed, conversing in secret low tones,
24. "Let not a single indigent person break in upon you into the garden this day."
25. And they went early, strong in an unjust resolve.
26. But when they saw the garden, they said, "We have surely lost our way."
27. "Indeed, we are shut out of the fruits of our labor!"
28. One of them, more just than the rest, said, "Did I not say to you, 'Why not glorify God?'"
29. They said, "Glory to our Lord! Verily, we have been doing wrong!"
30. Then they turned, one against another, in reproach.
31. They said, "Alas for us! We have indeed transgressed!"
32. "It may be that our Lord will give us in exchange a better garden than this, for we do turn to Him in repentance!"
33. Such is the punishment in this life, but greater is the punishment in the Hereafter, if only they knew!
34. For the righteous, there are Gardens of Delight in the presence of their Lord.
35. Shall We then treat the people of faith like the people of sin?
36. What is the matter with you? How do you judge?
37. Or do you have a book through which you learn,
38. That you shall have whatever you choose?
39. Or do you have covenants with Us, reaching to the Day of Judgment, that you shall have whatever you demand?
40. Ask them which of them will stand surety for that!
41. Or do they have partners in Godhead? Let them produce their partners if they are truthful!
42. The Day the shin shall be laid bare, and they shall be summoned to bow in adoration, but they shall not be able,
43. Their eyes will be cast down, ignominy will cover them; they had been summoned aforetime to bow in adoration while they were whole, but they refused.

Or is it that you ask them for a reward, so that they are burdened with a load of debt? Or do you ask a fee from them so that they are heavily taxed? Or do they have the knowledge of the unseen, so that they can write it down? So wait with patience for the Command of your Lord, and do not be like the Companion of the Fish, when he cried out in agony. But wait for your Lord's decree, and do not be like him of the fish, who cried out in despair. Had it not been for the favor from his Lord, he would have been cast off on the naked shore, in disgrace. But his Lord chose him and placed him among the righteous. And the Unbelievers would almost trip you up with their eyes when they hear the Message; and they say: "Surely he is possessed!" But it is nothing less than a Message to all the worlds.

Chapter 69: AL-HAAQQA (THE REALITY) Total Verses: 52 Revealed At: MAKKA

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. The Sure Reality!
2. What is the Sure Reality?
3. And what will make you realize what the Sure Reality is?
4. The Thamud and the 'Ad People branded as false the Stunning Calamity!
5. But the Thamud were destroyed by a terrible storm of thunder and lightning!
6. And the 'Ad were destroyed by a furious wind, exceedingly violent;
7. He made it rage against them seven nights and eight days in succession: so that you could see the people lying prostrate in its path, as if they were hollow palm-trees tumbled down!
8. Do you see any of them left surviving?
9. And Pharaoh, and those before him, and the Cities Overthrown, committed habitual sin.
10. And disobeyed each the messenger of their Lord; so He punished them with an abundant penalty.
11. We, when the water of Noah's Flood overflowed beyond its limits, carried you in the floating Ark,
12. That We might make it a Message unto you, and that ears that should hear the tale and retain its memory should bear its lessons in remembrance.
13. Then, when one blast is sounded on the Trumpet,
14. And the earth is moved, and its mountains, and they are crushed to powder at one stroke,
15. On that Day shall the Great Event come to pass.
16. And the sky will be rent asunder, for it will that Day be flimsy,
17. And the angels will be on its sides, and eight will, that Day, bear the Throne of your Lord above them.
18. That Day you will be brought to Judgment: not an act of yours that you hide will be hidden.
19. Then he that will be given his Record in his right hand will say: "Ah here! Read my Record!"
20. "I did really understand that my Account would one day reach me!"
21. And he will be in a life of Bliss,
22. In a Garden on high,
23. The fruits of which will hang in bunches low and near.
24. "Eat and drink with full satisfaction; because of the good that you sent before you, in the days that are gone!"
25. And he that will be given his Record in his left hand will say: "Ah! Would that my Record had not been given to me!"
26. "And that I had never realized how my account stood!"
27. "Ah! Would that death had made an end of me!"
28. "Of no profit to me has been my wealth!"
29. "My power has perished from me!"
30. (The stern command will say): "Seize him, and bind him,"
31. "And burn him in the Blazing Fire."
32. "Further, make him march in a chain, whereof the length is seventy cubits!"
33. "This was he that would not believe in God Most High."
34. "And would not encourage the feeding of the indigent!"
35. "So no friend has he here this Day."
36. "Nor has he any food except the corruption from the washing of wounds,"
37. "Which none do eat but those in sin."
38. So I do call to witness what you see,
39. And what you see not."This is not the word of a poet, as you believe so little. Nor is it the word of a soothsayer, as you remember so little. This is a message sent down from the Lord of the Worlds. If the messenger had fabricated any sayings in Our name, We would have seized him by his right hand and cut off his life-artery. None of you could have withheld Us from him. But this is a message for those who are mindful of God. We know that some of you will reject it, and it will be a cause of sorrow for the disbelievers. But it is the absolute truth. So glorify the name of your Lord, the Most High.

Chapter 70: AL-MAARIJ (THE ASCENDING STAIRWAYS)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. A questioner asked about a penalty that will befall the disbelievers, which none can repel,
2. From God, Lord of the Ascending Stairways.
3. The angels and the spirit ascend to Him in a day that measures fifty thousand years.
4. So be patient with a beautiful patience.
5. They see the Day as far off, but We see it as near.
6. The Day when the sky will be like molten brass,
7. And the mountains will be like wool,
8. And no friend will ask about a friend,
9. Though they will be put in sight of each other. The sinner will wish to ransom himself from the penalty of that Day by sacrificing his children,
10. His wife and his brother,
11. His kindred who sheltered him,
12. And all that is on earth, so it could deliver him.
13. But no! It will be the Fire of Hell,
14. Plucking out his being right to the skull,
15. Inviting all who turn their backs and turn away their faces from the Right,
16. And collect wealth and hide it from use.
17. Truly, man was created very impatient,
18. Fretful when evil touches him,
19. And niggardly when good reaches him,
20. Except those devoted to prayer,
21. Those who remain steadfast in their prayer,
22. And those in whose wealth is a recognized right,
23. For the needy who ask and those who are prevented from asking,
24. And those who hold to the truth of the Day of Judgment,
25. And those who fear the displeasure of their Lord,
26. For their Lord's displeasure is the opposite of peace and tranquility,
27. And those who guard their chastity,
28. Except with their wives and those whom their right hands possess, for then they are not to be blamed,
29. But those who trespass beyond this are transgressors,
30. And those who respect their trusts and covenants,
31. And those who stand firm in their testimonies,
32. And those who guard the sacredness of their worship,
33. Such will be the honored ones in the Gardens of Bliss.

34. Now, what is the matter with the disbelievers that they rush madly before you,
35. From the right and from the left, in crowds?
36. Does every man of them long to enter the Garden of Bliss?
37. By no means! For We have created them out of the base matter they know.
38. Now I call to witness the Lord of all points in the East and the West that We can certainly
39. Substitute for them better men than they, and We are not to be defeated in Our plan.""So let them continue with their idle talk and distractions until they face the Day they have been promised. On that Day, they will emerge from their graves in a rush, as if racing towards a goal. Their eyes will be downcast, and disgrace will cover them. This is the Day they were warned about.

Chapter 71: NOAH

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. We sent Noah to his people, saying, 'Warn your people before a painful punishment comes to them.'
2. Noah said, 'O my people, I am a clear and open warner to you.
3. Worship God, fear Him, and obey me.
4. He will forgive your sins and give you respite for a fixed term. When God's term comes, it cannot be delayed, if you only knew.'
5. Noah said, 'My Lord, I have called my people night and day,
6. But my call only increases their flight from the truth.
7. Every time I call them to seek Your forgiveness, they thrust their fingers in their ears, cover themselves with their garments, persist in their refusal, and grow more arrogant.
8. So I called to them aloud,
9. And I spoke to them in public and in private,
10. Saying, 'Ask forgiveness from your Lord; He is truly Most Forgiving.
11. He will send rain to you in abundance,
12. Increase your wealth and children, and provide you with gardens and rivers.
13. What is the matter with you that you do not hope for God's kindness and patience,
14. When He created you in stages?
15. Do you not see how God created the seven heavens one above another,
16. And made the moon a light in their midst, and the sun a radiant lamp?
17. God has caused you to grow from the earth,
18. And He will return you to it and bring you forth again.
19. God has made the earth a wide expanse for you,
20. So you may travel its spacious paths.'

Noah said, 'O my Lord, they have disobeyed me and followed those whose wealth and children only increase their loss.
22. They have devised a tremendous plot,
23. And said to each other, 'Do not abandon your gods. Do not abandon Wadd, Suwa', Yaguth, Ya'uq, or Nasr.'
24. They have already misled many, and You only increase the wrongdoers in straying from the right path.'
25. Because of their sins, they were drowned and made to enter the Fire. They found no helpers besides God.
26. Noah said, 'O my Lord, do not leave a single disbeliever on earth.
27. If You leave them, they will mislead Your servants and will only breed wicked and ungrateful offspring.
28. O my Lord, forgive me, my parents, all who enter my house in faith, and all believing men and women. Do not increase the wrongdoers in anything but destruction.'

Chapter 72: THE JINN

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. Say, 'It has been revealed to me that a group of jinn listened to the Qur'an. They said, 'We have heard a wonderful Recital!
2. It guides to the right path, and we have believed in it. We will not associate anyone with our Lord.
3. Exalted is the Majesty of our Lord. He has taken neither a wife nor a son.'"In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. Say, "It has been revealed to me that a group of jinn listened to the Qur'an. They said, 'We have heard a wonderful Recital!
2. It guides to the right path, and we have believed in it. We will not associate anyone with our Lord.
3. Exalted is the Majesty of our Lord. He has taken neither a wife nor a son.
4. There were some foolish ones among us who used to utter extravagant lies against God.
5. But we now realize that no human or jinn should say anything untrue about God.
6. True, there were people among mankind who sought protection from the jinn, but this only increased their folly.
7. They thought, as you did, that God would not raise anyone from the dead.
8. We tried to reach the secrets of heaven but found it filled with stern guards and flaming fires.
9. We used to sit in hidden places to eavesdrop, but now anyone who tries will find a flaming fire waiting for them.
10. We do not know whether harm is intended for those on earth or if their Lord intends to guide them.
11. Among us, some are righteous, and some are not. We follow different paths.
12. We know that we cannot escape from God on earth, nor can we escape by flight.
13. Since we have listened to the Guidance, we have accepted it. Anyone who believes in their Lord has no fear of loss or injustice.
14. Among us, some submit to God, and some deviate from justice. Those who submit have sought the right path.
15. But those who deviate are fuel for Hellfire.
16. If the pagans had remained on the right path, We would have given them abundant water to drink.
17. This is to test them. But if anyone turns away from the remembrance of their Lord, He will cause them to undergo severe punishment.
18. The places of worship are for God alone, so do not invoke anyone along with God.
19. When the Devotee of God stands to invoke Him, they crowd around him.
20. Say, "I only invoke my Lord and do not associate anyone with Him."
21. Say, "I do not have the power to cause you harm or to bring you to the right conduct."
22. Say, "No one can protect me from God, nor can I find refuge except in Him."
23. My duty is only to convey what I receive from God and His messages. For those who disobey God and His Messenger, there is Hell, where they will dwell forever.
24. When they see what they are promised, they will know who is weaker in helpers and fewer in number.
25. Say, "I do not know whether the punishment you are promised is near or if my Lord will appoint a distant term for it."
26. He alone knows the Unseen and does not reveal His secrets to anyone,
27. Except to a messenger whom He has chosen. He makes a band of watchers march before and behind him,
28. So that He may know that they have truly delivered the messages of their Lord. He surrounds all their doings and keeps count of all things.

Chapter 73: AL-MUZZAMMIL (THE ENSHROUDED ONE, BUNDLED UP)

1. O you who are wrapped up in garments!
2. Stand to pray by night, but not all night,
3. Half of it, or a little less,
4. Or a little more; and recite the Qur'an in slow, measured rhythmic tones.
5. Soon We shall send down to you a weighty Message.In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

2. It guides to the right path, and we have believed in it. We will not associate anyone with our Lord.
3. Exalted is the Majesty of our Lord. He has taken neither a wife nor a son.
4. There were some foolish ones among us who used to utter extravagant lies against God.
5. But we now realize that no human or jinn should say anything untrue about God.
6. True, there were people among mankind who sought protection from the jinn, but this only increased their folly.
7. They thought, as you did, that God would not raise anyone from the dead.
8. We tried to reach the secrets of heaven but found it filled with stern guards and flaming fires.
9. We used to sit in hidden places to eavesdrop, but now anyone who tries will find a flaming fire waiting for them.

11. Among us, some are righteous, and some are not. We follow different paths.
12. We know that we cannot escape from God on earth, nor can we escape by flight.
13. Since we have listened to the Guidance, we have accepted it. Anyone who believes in their Lord has no fear of loss or injustice.
14. Among us, some submit to God, and some deviate from justice. Those who submit have sought the right path.
15. But those who deviate are fuel for Hellfire.
16. If the pagans had remained on the right path, We would have given them abundant water to drink.
17. This is to test them. But if anyone turns away from the remembrance of their Lord, He will cause them to undergo severe punishment.
18. The places of worship are for God alone, so do not invoke anyone along with God.
19. When the Devotee of God stands to invoke Him, they crowd around him.
20. Say, "I only invoke my Lord and do not associate anyone with Him."
21. Say, "I do not have the power to cause you harm or to bring you to the right conduct."
22. Say, "No one can protect me from God, nor can I find refuge except in Him."
23. My duty is only to convey what I receive from God and His messages. For those who disobey God and His Messenger, there is Hell, where they will dwell forever.
24. When they see what they are promised, they will know who is weaker in helpers and fewer in number.
