Chapter 73: AL-MUZZAMMIL (THE ENSHROUDED ONE, BUNDLED UP)

1. O you who are wrapped up in garments!
2. Stand to pray by night, but not all night,
3. Half of it, or a little less,
4. Or a little more; and recite the Qur'an in slow, measured rhythmic tones.
5. Soon We shall send down to you a weighty Message.

Truly, the rising by night is most potent for governing the soul and most suitable for framing the Word of Prayer and Praise. The vigil of the night is a time when impression is more keen and speech more certain. Surely, the rising by night is the firmest way to tread and the best corrective of speech.

True, there is for you by day prolonged occupation with ordinary duties. You have in the daytime a long occupation. But keep in remembrance the name of your Lord and devote yourself to Him wholeheartedly. Remember the name of your Lord and devote yourself with complete devotion. The Lord of the East and the West: there is no god but He: take Him therefore for your Disposer of Affairs. The Lord of the East and the West; there is no God save Him; so choose Him alone for your defender. The Lord of the East and the West, there is no god but He, therefore take Him for a protector.

And have patience with what they say, and leave them with noble dignity. Bear with patience what they utter, and part from them with a fair leave-taking. Bear patiently what they say and avoid them with a becoming avoidance. Leave Me alone to deal with those in possession of the good things of life, who yet deny the Truth; and bear with them for a little while. Leave Me to deal with the deniers, lords of ease and comfort in this life; and do you respite them awhile. Leave Me and the rejecters, the possessors of ease and plenty, and respite them a little.

With Us are Fetters to bind them, and a Fire to burn them. With Us are heavy fetters and a raging fire. Surely with Us are heavy fetters and a flaming fire. And a Food that chokes, and a Penalty Grievous. And food which chokes the partaker, and a painful doom. And food that chokes and a painful punishment. One Day the earth and the mountains will be in violent commotion. And the mountains will be as a heap of sand poured out and flowing down. On the day when the earth and the hills rock, and the hills become a heap of running sand. On the day when the earth and the mountains shall quake and the mountains shall become as heaps of sand let loose.

We have sent to you, O men, a messenger, to be a witness concerning you, even as We sent a messenger to Pharaoh. We have sent unto you a messenger as witness against you, even as We sent unto Pharaoh a messenger. Surely We have sent to you a Messenger, a witness against you, as We sent a messenger to Pharaoh. But Pharaoh disobeyed the messenger; so We seized him with a heavy Punishment. But Pharaoh rebelled against the messenger, whereupon We seized him with no gentle grip. But Pharaoh disobeyed the messenger, so We laid on him a violent hold.

Then how shall you, if you deny God, guard yourselves against a Day that will make children hoary-headed? Then how, if you disbelieve, will you protect yourselves upon the day which will turn children grey? How, then, will you guard yourselves, if you disbelieve, on the day which shall make children grey-headed? Whereon the sky will be cleft asunder? His Promise needs must be accomplished. The very heaven being then rent asunder. His promise is to be fulfilled. The heaven shall rend asunder thereby; His promise is ever brought to fulfillment.

Verily this is an Admonition: therefore, whoso will, let him take a straight path to his Lord! This is a Reminder. Let him who will, then, choose a way unto his Lord. Surely this is a reminder, then let him, who will take the way to his Lord.

Your Lord knows that you stand to pray nearly two-thirds of the night, or half the night, or a third of the night, and so do a party of those with you. But God appoints night and day in due measure. He knows that you are unable to keep count thereof. So He has turned to you in mercy: read, therefore, of the Qur'an as much as may be easy for you. He knows that there may be some among you in ill-health; others traveling through the land, seeking God's bounty; yet others fighting in God's Cause. Read, therefore, as much of the Qur'an as may be easy for you; and establish regular Prayer and give regular Charity; and loan to God a Beautiful Loan. Whatever good you send forth for your souls, you shall find it in God's Presence, better and greater in reward. Seek the Grace of God: for God is Oft-Forgiving, Most Merciful.

Chapter 74: AL-MUDDATHTHIR (THE CLOAKED ONE, THE MAN WEARING A CLOAK)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. O you wrapped up in the mantle!
2. Arise and deliver your warning!
3. Magnify your Lord!
4. Keep your garments free from stain!
5. Shun all abomination!
6. Do not expect any increase for yourself in giving!
7. Be patient and constant for your Lord's Cause!
8. When the Trumpet is sounded,
9. That will be a Day of Distress,
10. Far from easy for those without Faith.
11. Leave Me alone to deal with the creature whom I created bare and alone!
12. To whom I granted resources in abundance,
13. And sons to be by his side!
14. To whom I made life smooth and comfortable!
15. Yet he is greedy, wanting more.
16. By no means! For he has been refractory to Our Signs.
17. Soon I will visit him with a mount of calamities!
18. For he thought and plotted;
19. And woe to him! How he plotted!
20. Yes, woe to him; how he plotted!
21. Then he looked around;
22. Then he frowned and scowled;
23. Then he turned back and was haughty;
24. Then he said, "This is nothing but magic, derived from of old;"
25. "This is nothing but the word of a mortal!"
26. Soon I will cast him into Hell-Fire!Chapter 74: AL-MUDDATHTHIR (THE CLOAKED ONE, THE MAN WEARING A CLOAK)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. O you wrapped in a cloak!
2. Get up and warn others!
3. Glorify your Lord!
4. Keep your clothes clean!
5. Avoid all evil!
6. Do not expect anything in return for your good deeds!
7. Be patient and steadfast for your Lord's cause!
8. When the Trumpet is blown,
9. It will be a day of distress,
10. Especially hard for those without faith.
11. Leave Me to deal with the one I created alone,
12. To whom I gave abundant resources,
13. And sons by his side,
14. To whom I made life easy and comfortable,
15. Yet he desires more.
16. No! For he has been stubborn against Our signs.
17. Soon I will overwhelm him with calamities!
18. For he thought and planned;
19. And woe to him! How he planned!
20. Yes, woe to him; how he planned!
21. Then he looked around;
22. Then he frowned and scowled;
23. Then he turned back and was arrogant;
24. Then he said, "This is nothing but magic from the past;"
25. "This is nothing but the word of a human!"
26. Soon I will throw him into Hell-Fire!

27. And what will explain to you what Hell-Fire is?
28. It leaves nothing and spares nothing.
29. It scorches the skin.
30. Over it are nineteen angels.
31. We have appointed only angels as guardians of the Fire, and their number is a trial for the disbelievers, so that the People of the Book may be certain, and the believers may increase in faith, and no doubts may be left for the People of the Book and the believers. Those with a disease in their hearts and the disbelievers will say, "What does God mean by this parable?" Thus God leads astray whom He wills and guides whom He wills. None knows the forces of your Lord except Him. This is nothing but a reminder to humanity.

32. No! By the Moon,
33. And the night as it retreats,
34. And the dawn as it shines forth,
35. This is one of the greatest signs,
36. A warning to humanity,
37. To anyone who chooses to move forward or lag behind.
38. Every soul is held accountable for its deeds,
39. Except the companions of the right hand.
40. They will be in gardens, asking each other
41. About the sinners:
42. "What led you into Hell-Fire?"
43. They will say, "We were not among those who prayed;
44. Nor did we feed the poor;
45. We indulged in vain talk with those who engaged in it;
46. And we denied the Day of Judgment,
47. Until the inevitable came to us."
48. Then no intercession of any intercessors will benefit them.
49. Why do they turn away from the reminder,
50. As if they were frightened donkeys
51. Fleeing from a lion?
52. Each one of them wants to be given open pages from God.
53. No! But they do not fear the Hereafter.
54. No! This is surely a reminder.
55. So whoever wills may remember it.
56. But they will not remember unless God wills. He is the source of righteousness and the source of forgiveness.

Chapter 75: AL-QIYAMA (THE RISING OF THE DEAD, RESURRECTION)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. I swear by the Day of Resurrection;
2. And I swear by the self-reproaching soul.
3. Does man think that We cannot assemble his bones?
4. Yes, We are able to restore even his fingertips.
5. But man wishes to deny what is ahead of him.
6. He asks, "When is the Day of Resurrection?"
7. But when the sight is dazed,
8. And the moon is eclipsed,
9. And the sun and moon are joined together,
10. On that day man will say, "Where is the refuge?"
11. No! There is no refuge!
12. To your Lord alone will be the place of rest that day.
13. On that day man will be informed of what he sent ahead and what he left behind.
14. No! Man will be a witness against himself,
15. Even if he presents his excuses.
16. Do not move your tongue with it to hasten it.
17. It is for Us to collect it and recite it.
18. So when We recite it, follow its recitation.
19. Then it is for Us to explain it.
20. No! But you love the fleeting life,
21. And neglect the Hereafter.
22. Some faces that day will be radiant,
23. Looking at their Lord;
24. And some faces that day will be gloomy,
25. Expecting some great calamity to befall them.Chapter 75: AL-QIYAMA (THE RISING OF THE DEAD, RESURRECTION)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. I swear by the Day of Resurrection;
2. And I swear by the self-reproaching soul.
3. Does man think that We cannot reassemble his bones?
4. Yes, We are able to restore even his fingertips.
5. But man wishes to deny what is ahead of him.
6. He asks, "When is the Day of Resurrection?"
7. But when the sight is dazed,
8. And the moon is eclipsed,
9. And the sun and moon are joined together,
10. On that day man will say, "Where is the refuge?"
11. No! There is no refuge!
12. To your Lord alone will be the place of rest that day.
13. On that day man will be informed of what he sent ahead and what he left behind.
14. No! Man will be a witness against himself,
15. Even if he presents his excuses.
16. Do not move your tongue with it to hasten it.
17. It is for Us to collect it and recite it.
18. So when We recite it, follow its recitation.
19. Then it is for Us to explain it.
20. No! But you love the fleeting life,
21. And neglect the Hereafter.
22. Some faces that day will be radiant,
23. Looking at their Lord;
24. And some faces that day will be gloomy,
25. Expecting some great calamity to befall them.

26. Yes, when the soul reaches the collarbone (in its exit),
27. And there will be a cry, "Who can restore him?"
28. And he will conclude that it is the time of parting;
29. And one leg will be joined with another:
30. That Day the drive will be to your Lord!
31. So he gave nothing in charity, nor did he pray!
32. But on the contrary, he rejected the truth and turned away!
33. Then he walked to his family in full conceit!
34. Woe to you, yes, woe!
35. Again, woe to you, yes, woe!
36. Does man think that he will be left uncontrolled, without purpose?
37. Was he not a drop of sperm emitted?
38. Then he became a clot; then God shaped and fashioned him.
39. And of him, He made two sexes, male and female.
40. Is not He able to give life to the dead?

Chapter 76: AL-INSAN (MAN)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. Has there not been over Man a long period of time when he was nothing, not even mentioned?
2. Verily We created Man from a drop of mingled sperm, in order to try him: So We gave him the gifts of hearing and sight.
3. We showed him the Way: whether he be grateful or ungrateful rests on his will.
4. For the Rejecters, We have prepared chains, yokes, and a blazing Fire.
5. As for the Righteous, they shall drink from a cup mixed with Kafur,
6. A fountain where the Devotees of God drink, making it flow in abundance.
7. They perform their vows and fear a Day whose evil spreads far and wide.
8. And they feed, for the love of God, the indigent, the orphan, and the captive,
9. Saying, "We feed you for the sake of God alone: no reward do we desire from you, nor thanks."
10. "We only fear a Day of distressful Wrath from our Lord."
11. But God will deliver them from the evil of that Day and will shed over them a Light of Beauty and Joy.
12. And because they were patient and constant, He will reward them with a Garden and garments of silk.
13. Reclining in the Garden on raised thrones, they will see neither the sun's excessive heat nor the moon's excessive cold.
14. And the shades of the Garden will come low over them, and the bunches of fruit will hang low in humility.
15. And amongst them will be passed round vessels of silver and goblets of crystal,
16. Crystal-clear, made of silver: they will determine the measure thereof according to their wishes.
17. And they will be given to drink from a cup mixed with Zanjabil,
18. A fountain there called Salsabil.
19. And around them will serve youths of perpetual freshness: if you see them, you would think them scattered pearls.
20. And when you look, you will see Bliss and a Magnificent Realm.
21. Upon them will be green garments of fine silk and heavy brocade, and they will be adorned with bracelets of silver; and their Lord will give them a pure and holy drink.
22. "Verily this is a reward for you, and your endeavor is accepted and recognized."
23. It is We Who have sent down the Qur'an to you in stages.
24. Therefore be patient with constancy to the Command of your Lord, and do not obey the sinner or the ungrateful among them.
25. And celebrate the name of your Lord morning and evening.Chapter 76: AL-INSAN (MAN)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. Was there not a time when man was nothing worth mentioning?
2. We created man from a drop of mixed fluid to test him, and We gave him hearing and sight.
3. We showed him the way, whether he chooses to be grateful or ungrateful.
4. For the disbelievers, We have prepared chains, yokes, and a blazing fire.
5. The righteous will drink from a cup mixed with Kafur,
6. A spring from which the devoted servants of God will drink, making it flow abundantly.
7. They fulfill their vows and fear a day whose evil will spread far and wide.
8. They give food, out of love for Him, to the poor, the orphan, and the captive,
9. Saying, "We feed you for the sake of God alone; we seek neither reward nor thanks from you."
10. "We fear a distressful day from our Lord."
11. So God will protect them from the evil of that day and give them radiance and joy.
12. Because they were patient, He will reward them with a garden and garments of silk.
13. Reclining in the garden on raised thrones, they will see neither the sun's excessive heat nor the moon's excessive cold.
14. The garden's shade will be close over them, and the clusters of fruit will hang low.
15. They will be served with silver vessels and crystal-clear goblets,
16. Crystal-clear, made of silver, perfectly measured.
17. They will drink from a cup mixed with ginger,
18. From a spring called Salsabil.
19. Youths of perpetual freshness will serve them; if you saw them, you would think they were scattered pearls.
20. When you look, you will see bliss and a magnificent realm.
21. They will wear green garments of fine silk and heavy brocade, adorned with silver bracelets, and their Lord will give them a pure drink.
22. "This is a reward for you, and your effort is appreciated."

23. We have sent down the Qur'an to you in stages.
24. So be patient with your Lord's command and do not obey the sinner or the ungrateful among them.
25. Celebrate your Lord's name morning and evening.

26. And during part of the night, prostrate yourself to Him and glorify Him for a long part of the night.
27. These people love the fleeting life and neglect a hard day ahead.
28. We created them and strengthened their frame, and when We will, We can replace them with others like them.
29. This is a reminder; whoever wills, let him take a straight path to his Lord.
30. But you will not, unless God wills; for God is full of knowledge and wisdom.
31. He admits to His mercy whom He wills, but for the wrongdoers, He has prepared a painful punishment.

Chapter 77: AL-MURSALAT (THE EMISSARIES, WINDS SENT FORTH)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. By the winds sent forth one after another,
2. Which then blow violently in tempestuous gusts,
3. And scatter things far and wide,
4. Then separate them one from another,
5. Then spread abroad a message,
6. Whether of justification or of warning;
7. Surely what you are promised must come to pass.
8. When the stars become dim,
9. When the sky is cleft asunder,
10. When the mountains are scattered as dust,
11. And when the messengers are appointed a time to collect;
12. For what day are these portents deferred?
13. For the Day of Sorting out.
14. And what will explain to you what the Day of Sorting out is?
15. Woe that day to the rejecters of truth!
16. Did We not destroy the men of old for their evil?
17. So shall We make later generations follow them.
18. Thus do We deal with men of sin.
19. Woe that day to the rejecters of truth!
20. Did We not create you from a despicable fluid?
21. Which We placed in a secure resting place,
22. For a period determined according to need?
23. We determine things; We are the best at determining.
24. Woe that day to the rejecters of truth!
25. Have We not made the earth a place to draw together,
26. Both for the living and the dead,
27. And made therein mountains standing firm, and provided you with sweet water?
28. Woe that day to the rejecters of truth!
29. "Depart to that which you used to reject as false!"
30. "Depart to a shadow of smoke ascending in three columns,"
31. "Which yields no shade of coolness and is of no use against the fierce blaze."
32. "Indeed, it throws about sparks as huge as forts,"
33. "As if they were yellow camels."
34. Woe that day to the rejecters of truth!
35. That will be a day when they shall not be able to speak,
36. Nor will it be open to them to put forth pleas.
37. Woe that day to the rejecters of truth!
38. That will be a day of sorting out! We shall gather you and those before you!
39. Now, if you have a trick or plot, use it against Me!
40. Woe that day to the rejecters of truth!
41. As for the righteous, they shall be amidst cool shades and springs of water,
42. And they shall have fruits, all they desire.
43. "Eat and drink to your heart's content for what you worked in righteousness."
44. Thus do We reward the doers of good.
45. Woe that day to the rejecters of truth!
46. "Eat and enjoy yourselves a little while, for you are sinners."
47. Woe that day to the rejecters of truth!
48. When it is said to them, "Prostrate yourselves!" they do not do so.
49. Woe that day to the rejecters of truth!
50. Then what message, after this, will they believe in?Chapter 78: AN-NABA (THE TIDINGS, THE ANNOUNCEMENT)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. What are they disputing about?
2. About the Great News,
3. Which they are in disagreement about.
4. Indeed, they will soon know!
5. Again, they will soon know!
6. Have We not made the earth a wide expanse,
7. And the mountains as pegs?
8. And created you in pairs,
9. And made your sleep for rest,
10. And made the night as a covering,
11. And made the day for livelihood?
12. And built above you seven strong heavens,
13. And placed a shining lamp (the sun)?
14. And sent down abundant water from the clouds,
15. To produce grain and plants,
16. And gardens of lush growth?
17. Indeed, the Day of Decision is appointed,
18. The Day when the Trumpet will be blown, and you will come forth in crowds,
19. And the heavens will be opened as if there were doors,
20. And the mountains will vanish like a mirage.
21. Truly, Hell is lying in wait,
22. A home for the rebellious.
23. They will dwell therein for ages.
24. They will taste neither coolness nor drink,
25. Except boiling water and a dark, murky fluid,
26. A fitting recompense for them.
27. For they did not fear any reckoning,
28. And they denied Our signs with strong denial.
29. And We have recorded everything in a Book.
30. So taste (the fruits of your deeds); for We will not increase you except in punishment.

31. Indeed, for the righteous, there will be a fulfillment of their desires;
32. Gardens enclosed and vineyards,
33. And companions of equal age,
34. And a cup full to the brim.
35. They will hear no vain talk or lying therein,
36. A reward from your Lord, a gift amply sufficient,
37. From the Lord of the heavens and the earth and all between, the Most Gracious: None shall have power to argue with Him.
38. The Day when the Spirit and the angels will stand forth in ranks, none shall speak except those permitted by the Most Gracious, and they will say what is right.
39. That Day will be the sure Reality: So whoever wills, let him take a straight path to his Lord!
40. Indeed, We have warned you of a near punishment, the Day when man will see what his hands have sent forth, and the disbeliever will say, "Woe unto me! Would that I were dust!"

Chapter 79: AN-NAZIAT (THOSE WHO DRAG FORTH, SOUL-SNATCHERS)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. By those (angels) who violently pull out the souls of the wicked,
2. And by those who gently draw out the souls of the blessed,
3. And by those who glide along (on errands of mercy),
4. Then press forward as in a race,
5. Then arrange to do the commands of their Lord,
6. One Day everything that can be in commotion will be in violent commotion,
7. Followed by oft-repeated commotions:
8. Hearts that Day will be in agitation;
9. Cast down will be their owners' eyes.
10. They say now: "What! Shall we indeed be returned to our former state?"
11. "What! When we shall have become rotten bones?"
12. They say: "It would, in that case, be a return with loss!"
13. But indeed, it will be but a single compelling cry,
14. When, behold, they will be in the full awakening to Judgment.
15. Has the story of Moses reached you?
16. How his Lord called him in the sacred valley of Tuwa:
17. "Go to Pharaoh, for he has indeed transgressed all bounds:
18. And say to him, 'Would you like to purify yourself?'"Chapter 80: ABASA (HE FROWNED)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. The Prophet frowned and turned away
2. Because a blind man came to him.
3. But how do you know? Maybe he wanted to grow in spiritual understanding,
4. Or receive guidance that might benefit him.
5. As for the one who thinks he is self-sufficient,
6. You pay attention to him,
7. Even though it’s not your concern if he doesn’t grow spiritually.
8. But the one who comes to you with earnest effort,
9. And has fear in his heart,
10. You are distracted from him.
11. No! This is indeed a message of instruction:
12. So let whoever wills, keep it in remembrance.
13. It is in books held in high honor,
14. Exalted and kept pure,
15. Written by the hands of noble and righteous scribes.
16. Woe to man! What has made him reject God?
17. From what substance did He create him?
18. From a sperm-drop: He created him and then shaped him in due proportions;
19. Then He made his path smooth for him;
20. Then He causes him to die and puts him in his grave;
21. Then, when He wills, He will raise him up again.
22. But man has not fulfilled what God commanded him.
23. Let man look at his food,
24. How We pour water in abundance,
25. And split the earth in fragments,
26. And produce therein grain,
27. And grapes and nutritious plants,
28. And olives and dates,
29. And enclosed gardens, dense with lofty trees,
30. And fruits and fodder,
31. For use and convenience to you and your cattle.
32. But when the Deafening Noise comes,
33. That Day a man will flee from his own brother,
34. And from his mother and his father,
35. And from his wife and his children.
36. Every man, that Day, will have enough to make him careless of others.
37. Some faces that Day will be bright,
38. Laughing, rejoicing at good news.
39. And other faces that Day will be dust-stained,
40. Covered with darkness.
41. Those are the disbelievers, the wicked ones.Chapter 81: AT-TAKWIR (THE OVERTHROWING)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. When the sun is folded up,
2. When the stars lose their light,
3. When the mountains vanish like a mirage,
4. When the pregnant camels are left untended,
5. When the wild beasts are gathered together,
6. When the oceans boil over,
7. When the souls are sorted out,
8. When the female infant buried alive is questioned
9. For what crime she was killed,
10. When the scrolls are laid open,
11. When the sky is unveiled,
12. When the Blazing Fire is kindled fiercely,
13. And when the Garden is brought near,
14. Then every soul will know what it has put forward.

15. I call to witness the planets that recede,
16. That go straight or hide,
17. And the Night as it dissipates,
18. And the Dawn as it breathes away the darkness,
19. This is the word of a most honorable Messenger,
20. Endowed with power, with rank before the Lord of the Throne,
21. With authority there, and faithful to his trust.
22. Your companion is not possessed;
23. He saw him in the clear horizon.
24. He does not withhold knowledge of the Unseen.
25. Nor is it the word of an evil spirit accursed.
26. So where are you going?
27. This is a message to all the worlds,
28. For whoever among you wills to go straight.
29. But you will not will except as God wills, the Cherisher of the Worlds.

Chapter 82: AL-INFITAR (THE CLEAVING, BURSTING APART)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. When the sky is cleft asunder,
2. When the stars are scattered,
3. When the oceans burst forth,
4. When the graves are turned upside down,
5. Then every soul will know what it has sent forward and what it has kept back.

6. O man! What has seduced you from your Lord Most Beneficent,
7. Who created you, fashioned you in due proportion, and gave you a just bias?
8. In whatever form He wills, He puts you together.
9. But you reject the Right and Judgment!
10. Over you are appointed angels to protect you,
11. Kind and honorable, writing down your deeds.
12. They know all that you do.

13. The Righteous will be in bliss,
14. And the Wicked will be in the Fire,
15. Which they will enter on the Day of Judgment,
16. And they will not be able to keep away from it.

17. What will explain to you what the Day of Judgment is?
18. Again, what will explain to you what the Day of Judgment is?
19. It is the Day when no soul shall have power to do anything for another; the command that Day will be entirely with God.

Chapter 83: AL-MUTAFFIFIN (DEFRAUDING, THE CHEATS, CHEATING)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. Woe to those who deal in fraud,
2. Those who, when they receive by measure from men, exact full measure,
3. But when they give by measure or weight to men, give less than due.
4. Do they not think that they will be called to account,
5. On a Mighty Day,
6. A Day when all...Chapter 84: AL-INSHIQAQ (THE SUNDERING, SPLITTING OPEN)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. When the sky is split apart,
2. When the stars are scattered,
3. When the earth is flattened out,
4. And it throws out everything inside it and becomes empty,
5. And listens to its Lord and obeys—it must do so.

6. O human! You are striving towards your Lord, and you will meet Him.
7. Whoever receives their record in their right hand,
8. Will have an easy reckoning,
9. And will return to their people, rejoicing.
10. But whoever receives their record behind their back,
11. Will cry for destruction,
12. And will enter a blazing fire.
13. They used to be happy among their people,
14. And thought they would never return to Us.
15. But their Lord was always watching them.

16. I swear by the afterglow of sunset,
17. And by the night and what it envelops,
18. And by the full moon,
19. You will surely move from stage to stage.

20. So what is the matter with them that they do not believe?
21. And when the Qur'an is recited to them, they do not prostrate?
22. Instead, the disbelievers deny it.
23. But God knows best what they hide in their hearts.
24. So give them the news of a painful punishment,
25. Except for those who believe and do good deeds; for them is a reward that will never end.

Chapter 85: AL-BUROOJ (THE MANSIONS OF THE STARS, CONSTELLATIONS)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.Chapter 85: AL-BUROOJ (THE MANSIONS OF THE STARS, CONSTELLATIONS)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. By the sky with its constellations,
2. And by the promised Day of Judgment,
3. And by the witness and the witnessed,
4. Cursed were the makers of the pit,
5. The fire supplied with fuel,
6. When they sat by it,
7. And witnessed what they did to the believers.
8. They persecuted them only because they believed in God, the Mighty, the Praiseworthy,
9. To whom belongs the dominion of the heavens and the earth. And God is Witness over all things.
10. Those who persecute the believing men and women and do not repent will have the punishment of Hell and the burning fire.
11. But those who believe and do righteous deeds will have gardens beneath which rivers flow. That is the great success.
12. Truly, the grip of your Lord is strong.
13. It is He who creates from the beginning and can restore life.
14. And He is the Oft-Forgiving, Full of Loving-Kindness,
15. Lord of the Throne of Glory,
16. Doer of what He intends.
17. Has the story reached you of the forces,
18. Of Pharaoh and Thamud?
19. Yet the disbelievers persist in denying the truth.
20. But God encompasses them from behind.
21. Nay, this is a Glorious Qur'an,
22. Inscribed in a Preserved Tablet.

Chapter 86: AT-TARIQ (THE MORNING STAR, THE NIGHTCOMER)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. By the sky and the night-visitant,
2. And what will explain to you what the night-visitant is?
3. It is the star of piercing brightness.
4. There is no soul but has a protector over it.
5. Let man consider from what he is created.
6. He is created from a gushing fluid,
7. That issues from between the loins and ribs.
8. Surely, God is able to bring him back to life.
9. On the day when hidden thoughts will be examined,
10. Then he will have no power nor any helper.
11. By the sky which returns rain,
12. And by the earth which splits with growth,
13. This is a decisive word,
14. It is not a thing for amusement.
15. They are plotting a scheme,
16. And I am planning a scheme.
17. So give respite to the disbelievers, deal gently with them for a while.

Chapter 87: AL-ALA (THE MOST HIGH, GLORY TO YOUR LORD IN THE HIGHEST)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. Glorify the name of your Lord, the Most High,
2. Who created and perfected,
3. Who determined and guided,
4. Who brings out the green pasture,
5. And then makes it dry stubble.
6. We will make you recite, so you will not forget,
7. Except what God wills. He knows what is manifest and what is hidden.
8. And We will make your way smooth.
9. So remind, if the reminder benefits.
10. The reminder will be received by those who fear God,
11. But the most unfortunate will avoid it,
12. Who will enter the great fire,
13. Where they will neither die nor live.
14. But those who purify themselves will prosper,
15. And remember the name of their Lord and pray.
16. But you prefer the life of this world,
17. While the Hereafter is better and more enduring.
18. This is in the former scriptures,
19. The scriptures of Abraham and Moses.Chapter 88: AL-GHASHIYA (THE OVERWHELMING EVENT)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. Have you heard about the overwhelming event?
2. On that day, some faces will be humbled,
3. Exhausted and weary,
4. Entering a blazing fire,
5. Drinking from a boiling spring,
6. With no food except bitter thorns,
7. Which neither nourish nor satisfy hunger.
8. Other faces that day will be joyful,
9. Pleased with their efforts,
10. In a high garden,
11. Where they will hear no idle talk,
12. With a bubbling spring,
13. Raised thrones,
14. Goblets ready,
15. Cushions set in rows,
16. And rich carpets spread out.
17. Do they not look at the camels, how they are created?
18. And at the sky, how it is raised high?
19. And at the mountains, how they are fixed firm?
20. And at the earth, how it is spread out?
21. So remind them, for you are only a reminder.
22. You are not a manager over them.
23. But if anyone turns away and rejects God,
24. God will punish them with a mighty punishment.
25. To Us is their return,
26. And then it is for Us to call them to account.

Chapter 89: AL-FAJR (THE DAWN)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. By the break of day,
2. And by the ten nights,
3. By the even and the odd,
4. And by the night when it passes away,
5. Is there not in these an oath for those who understand?
6. Have you not seen how your Lord dealt with the 'Ad people,
7. Of the city of Iram with lofty pillars,
8. The like of which was not created in the land?
9. And with the Thamud people, who carved out rocks in the valley,
10. And with Pharaoh, lord of stakes?
11. They all transgressed beyond bounds in the lands,
12. And heaped therein mischief.
13. So your Lord poured on them a scourge of diverse punishments.
14. For your Lord is ever watchful.
15. As for man, when his Lord tests him by giving him honor and gifts, he says, "My Lord has honored me."
16. But when He tests him by restricting his subsistence, he says, "My Lord has humiliated me."
17. No! But you do not honor the orphan,
18. Nor do you encourage one another to feed the poor,
19. And you devour inheritance with greed,
20. And you love wealth with inordinate love.
21. No! When the earth is pounded to powder,
22. And your Lord comes with angels, rank upon rank,
23. And Hell is brought near that day, on that day man will remember, but how will that remembrance benefit him?
24. He will say, "Oh, I wish I had sent forth good deeds for my life!"
25. For that day, His punishment will be such as none else can inflict,
26. And His bonds will be such as none other can bind.
27. (To the righteous soul will be said:) "O soul, in complete rest and satisfaction,
28. Come back to your Lord, well pleased and well-pleasing,
29. Enter among My devotees,
30. Yes, enter My Heaven."

Chapter 90: AL-BALAD (THE CITY)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. I swear by this city,

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. By the Glorious Morning Light,
2. And by the Night when it is still,
3. Your Guardian-Lord has not forsaken you, nor is He displeased.
4. Indeed, the Hereafter will be better for you than the present.
5. And soon your Guardian-Lord will give you so much that you will be pleased.
6. Did He not find you an orphan and give you shelter?
7. And He found you lost and guided you,
8. And He found you in need and made you self-sufficient.
9. Therefore, do not oppress the orphan,
10. Nor repulse the one who asks for help,

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. By the Glorious Morning Light,
2. And by the Night when it is still,
3. Your Guardian-Lord has not forsaken you, nor is He displeased.
4. Indeed, the Hereafter will be better for you than the present.

9. Therefore, do not oppress the orphan,

Chapter 94: AL-INSHIRAH (SOLACE, CONSOLATION, RELIEF)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. Have We not expanded your chest?
2. And removed from you your burden,
3. Which weighed down your back?
4. And raised high your esteem?
5. So, verily, with every difficulty, there is relief:
6. Indeed, with every difficulty, there is relief.
7. Therefore, when you are free from your immediate task, still labor hard,
8. And turn all your attention to your Lord.

Chapter 95: AT-TIN (THE FIG, THE FIGTREE)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. By the Fig and the Olive,
2. And the Mount of Sinai,
3. And this City of security,
4. We have indeed created man in the best of molds,
5. Then We reduce him to the lowest of the low,
6. Except those who believe and do righteous deeds: For they shall have a reward unfailing.
7. Then what can contradict you, as to the judgment to come?
8. Is not God the wisest of judges?

Chapter 96: AL-ALAQ (THE CLOT, READ)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. Read in the name of your Lord who created,
2. Created man from a clot.
3. Read, and your Lord is Most Bountiful,
4. Who taught by the pen,
5. Taught man what he knew not.
6. But man transgresses all bounds,
7. Because he sees himself as self-sufficient.
8. Surely, to your Lord is the return.
9. Have you seen the one who forbids
10. A servant when he prays?
11. Have you considered if he is on the right path,
12. Or enjoins righteousness?
13. Have you considered if he denies the truth and turns away?
14. Does he not know that God sees?
15. Let him beware! If he does not desist, We will drag him by the forelock,
16. A lying, sinful forelock!
17. Then let him call his council of comrades:
18. We will call on the angels of punishment to deal with him!
19. No, do not obey him. But bow down in adoration, and draw closer to God.

Chapter 97: AL-QADR (POWER, FATE)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. We have indeed revealed this message in the Night of Power:
2. And what will explain to you what the Night of Power is?
3. The Night of Power is better than a thousand months.
4. The angels and the Spirit descend therein, by the permission of their Lord, with all decrees.
5. Peace! It is until the rise of dawn.

Chapter 98: AL-BAYYINA (THE CLEAR PROOF, EVIDENCE)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. Those who reject the truth, among the People of the Book and among the Polytheists, were not going to depart from their ways until there came to them clear evidence,
2. A messenger from God, reciting pure scriptures,
3. Containing correct decrees.
4. Nor did the People of the Book make schisms until after there came to them clear evidence.
5. And they have been commanded no more than this: To worship God, offering Him sincere devotion, being true in faith; to establish regular prayer; and to practice regular charity; and that is the right religion.
6. Those who reject the truth, among the People of the Book and among the Polytheists, will be in Hell-Fire, to dwell therein forever. They are the worst of creatures.

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. Those who reject the truth, among the People of the Book and the Polytheists, were not going to change their ways until clear evidence came to them,
2. A messenger from God, reciting pure scriptures,
3. Containing correct decrees.
4. The People of the Book did not become divided until after clear evidence came to them.
5. They were only commanded to worship God, being sincere in their faith, to establish regular prayer, and to practice regular charity. This is the right religion.
6. Those who reject the truth, among the People of the Book and the Polytheists, will be in Hell-Fire, to dwell there forever. They are the worst of creatures.
7. Those who have faith and do righteous deeds are the best of creatures.
8. Their reward is with God: Gardens of Eternity, beneath which rivers flow; they will dwell there forever. God is well pleased with them, and they with Him. This is for those who fear their Lord.

Chapter 99: AL-ZALZALA (THE EARTHQUAKE)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. When the earth is shaken with its final earthquake,
2. And the earth throws up its burdens,
3. And man cries out, 'What is happening to her?'
4. On that Day, she will declare her news,
5. Because your Lord will have inspired her.
6. On that Day, people will come forward in scattered groups to be shown their deeds.
7. Whoever has done an atom's weight of good will see it,
8. And whoever has done an atom's weight of evil will see it.

Chapter 100: AL-ADIYAT (THE COURSER, THE CHARGERS)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. By the steeds that run with panting breath,
2. And strike sparks of fire,
3. And charge at dawn,
4. Raising clouds of dust,
5. And penetrating into the midst of the enemy,
6. Truly, man is ungrateful to his Lord,
7. And he himself bears witness to this,
8. And he is violent in his love of wealth.
9. Does he not know that when the contents of the graves are scattered,
10. And the secrets of the hearts are revealed,
11. Their Lord will be fully aware of them on that Day?

Chapter 101: AL-QARIA (THE CALAMITY, THE STUNNING BLOW, THE DISASTER)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. The Calamity!
2. What is the Calamity?
3. And what will explain to you what the Calamity is?
4. It is a Day when people will be like scattered moths,
5. And the mountains will be like carded wool.
6. Then, he whose balance of good deeds is heavy,
7. Will live a pleasant life.
8. But he whose balance is light,
9. Will have his home in a bottomless pit.
10. And what will explain to you what this is?
11. It is a Fire blazing fiercely!

Chapter 102: AT-TAKATHUR (RIVALRY IN WORLD INCREASE, COMPETITION)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. The mutual rivalry for piling up worldly things diverts you,
2. Until you visit the graves.
3. But no, you will soon know!
4. Again, you will soon know!
5. If you knew with certainty of mind, you would beware!
6. You will certainly see Hell-Fire!
7. Again, you will see it with certainty of sight!
8. Then, on that Day, you will be questioned about the joy you indulged in.

Chapter 103: AL-ASR (THE DECLINING DAY, EVENTIDE, THE EPOCH)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. By the declining day,
2. Verily, man is in loss,
3. Except those who have faith, do righteous deeds, and encourage each other to truth and patience.

Chapter 104: AL-HUMAZA (THE TRADUCER, THE GOSSIPMONGER)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. Woe to every scandal-monger and backbiter,
2. Who piles up wealth and counts it,
3. Thinking that his wealth will make him last forever!
4. By no means! He will be thrown into the Consuming Fire.
5. And what will explain to you what the Consuming Fire is?
6. It is the Fire of God, kindled,
7. Which rises above the hearts.
8. It will be closed in on them,
9. In outstretched columns.

Chapter 105: AL-FIL (THE ELEPHANT)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. Have you not seen how your Lord dealt with the Companions of the Elephant?Chapter 105: AL-FIL (THE ELEPHANT)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. Have you not seen how your Lord dealt with the companions of the elephant?
2. Did He not make their treacherous plan go astray?
3. And He sent against them flocks of birds,
4. Striking them with stones of baked clay,
5. Then He made them like eaten straw.

Chapter 106: QURAISH (WINTER, QURAYSH)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. For the protection of the Quraish,
2. Their protection during their trading journeys in winter and summer,
3. Let them worship the Lord of this House,
4. Who provides them with food against hunger and security against fear.

Chapter 107: AL-MAUN (SMALL KINDNESSES, ALMSGIVING, HAVE YOU SEEN)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. Have you seen the one who denies the Judgment?
2. That is the one who repels the orphan,
3. And does not encourage the feeding of the poor.
4. So woe to those who pray,
5. But are heedless of their prayers,
6. Those who only want to be seen,
7. And refuse small kindnesses.

Chapter 108: AL-KAUTHER (ABUNDANCE, PLENTY)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. We have granted you abundance.
2. So pray to your Lord and sacrifice.
3. Indeed, your enemy is the one cut off.

Chapter 109: AL-KAFIROON (THE DISBELIEVERS, ATHEISTS)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. Say: O disbelievers,
2. I do not worship what you worship,
3. Nor do you worship what I worship.
4. I will not worship what you worship,
5. Nor will you worship what I worship.
6. To you be your religion, and to me mine.

Chapter 110: AN-NASR (SUCCOUR, DIVINE SUPPORT)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. When the help of God and victory come,
2. And you see people entering God's religion in crowds,
3. Celebrate the praises of your Lord and seek His forgiveness. He is always ready to show mercy.

Chapter 111: AL-MASADD (PALM FIBRE, THE FLAME)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. Perish the hands of Abu Lahab, and perish he!
2. His wealth and gains will not benefit him.
3. He will be plunged into a flaming fire,
4. And his wife, the wood-carrier,
5. Will have a rope of palm-fibre around her neck.

Chapter 112: AL-IKHLAS (SINCERITY)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. Say: He is God, the One and Only;
2. God, the Eternal, Absolute;
3. He begets not, nor is He begotten;
4. And there is none like unto Him.

Chapter 113: AL-FALAQ (THE DAYBREAK, DAWN)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. Say: I seek refuge with the Lord of the Dawn,
2. From the mischief of created things;
3. From the mischief of darkness as it overspreads;
4. From the mischief of those who practice secret arts;
5. And from the mischief of the envious one as he practices envy.

Chapter 114: AN-NAS (MANKIND)

In the name of God, the Most Beneficent, the Most Merciful.

1. Say: I seek refuge with the Lord of Mankind,
2. The King of Mankind,
3. The God of Mankind,
4. From the mischief of the Whisperer (of Evil), who withdraws (after his whisper),
5. Who whispers into the hearts of Mankind,
6. Among jinns and among men.
